
if typeof(getgenv) == "function" then
    if getgenv().JEYHUB_CONNECTIONS then
        for _, conn in pairs(getgenv().JEYHUB_CONNECTIONS) do
            if conn then pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end) end
        end
    end
    getgenv().JEYHUB_CONNECTIONS = {}
end

local JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN = (typeof(getgenv) == "function") and (tick() .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1, 1e9))) or nil
if typeof(getgenv) == "function" then
    getgenv().JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN = JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN
end
local function IsCurrentRun()
    if not JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN or typeof(getgenv) ~= "function" then return true end
    return getgenv().JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN == JEYHUB_RUN_TOKEN
end

local function TrackConnection(conn)
    if conn and typeof(getgenv) == "function" then
        pcall(function() table.insert(getgenv().JEYHUB_CONNECTIONS, conn) end)
    end
    return conn
end

local function SafeService(name)
    local ok, svc = pcall(function() return game:GetService(name) end)
    if ok and typeof(svc) == "Instance" then return svc end
    if ok and svc ~= nil then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Service", name, "returned an unexpected type:", typeof(svc))
        return nil
    end
    warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to get service:", name, svc)
    return nil
end

local TweenService       = SafeService("TweenService")
local UserInputService   = SafeService("UserInputService")
local Players            = SafeService("Players")
local VoiceChatService   = SafeService("VoiceChatService")
local ContentProvider    = SafeService("ContentProvider")

local LocalPlayer = Players and Players.LocalPlayer

local HttpService = SafeService("HttpService")

-- ============================================================
-- UNIFIED JSON DATA STORE
-- ============================================================
-- SEMUA fitur JEYHUB yang butuh nyimpen data ke file (encounter
-- tracker & catatan player, histori player, item Avatar Changer yang
-- diterapkan, config+cache Animations, config Visual) sekarang nulis
-- ke SATU FILE JSON YANG SAMA: JEYHUB/data.json -- bukan file
-- terpisah per fitur seperti sebelumnya. Semua section-nya saling
-- berkaitan dalam 1 objek JSON (dikelompokkan per key), jadi
-- backup/restore/pindah semua config & data JEYHUB kamu ke device lain
-- cukup salin 1 file ini saja.
--
-- Section yang dipakai saat ini: "encounters", "playerNotes",
-- "playerHistory", "avatarApplied", "animationsConfig",
-- "animationsCache", "visualConfig". Fitur baru ke depannya tinggal
-- pakai JD_Get/JD_Set dengan section key baru -- tidak perlu bikin
-- folder/file JSON sendiri lagi.
local JD_FOLDER = "JEYHUB"
local JD_PATH = JD_FOLDER .. "/data.json"
local JD_MAX_BYTES = 8 * 1024 * 1024 -- 8MB -- longgar karena sekarang menampung semua section sekaligus

local hasFS = (typeof(writefile) == "function") and (typeof(readfile) == "function")

-- Tabel di memori yang menampung SEMUA section sekaligus.
local JD_Store = {
    _meta = { version = 1 },
}
local JD_Loaded = false

local function JD_EnsureFolder()
    pcall(function()
        if typeof(makefolder) == "function" and typeof(isfolder) == "function" then
            if not isfolder(JD_FOLDER) then makefolder(JD_FOLDER) end
        end
    end)
end

-- Nama & path file JSON versi JEYHUB sebelumnya (per-fitur, terpisah-
-- pisah) -- dipakai SEKALI di bawah untuk migrasi otomatis kalau
-- data.json belum ada tapi file-file lama ini masih ada, supaya user
-- yang update dari versi lama tidak kehilangan data lamanya.
local JD_LEGACY_FILES = {
    { key = "encounters",       path = "JEYHUB_Universal/encounters.json" },
    { key = "playerNotes",      path = "JEYHUB_Universal/player_notes.json" },
    { key = "playerHistory",    path = "JEYHUB_Universal/player_history.json" },
    { key = "avatarApplied",    path = "JEYHUB_AvatarChanger/applied_items.json" },
    { key = "animationsConfig", path = "JEYHUB_Animations/config.json" },
    { key = "animationsCache",  path = "JEYHUB_Animations/anims_cache.json" },
    { key = "visualConfig",     path = "JEYHUB_Visual/config.json" },
}

local function JD_Load()
    if JD_Loaded then return end
    JD_Loaded = true
    if not hasFS or not HttpService then return end

    if typeof(isfile) == "function" and isfile(JD_PATH) then
        local okRead, raw = pcall(function() return readfile(JD_PATH) end)
        if okRead and type(raw) == "string" then
            local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(raw) end)
            if okDecode and type(data) == "table" then
                JD_Store = data
                JD_Store._meta = JD_Store._meta or { version = 1 }
                return
            else
                warn("[JEYHUB] data.json corrupt, backed up and reset:", data)
                pcall(function() writefile(JD_PATH .. ".corrupt", raw) end)
            end
        else
            warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to read data.json:", raw)
        end
    end

    -- Belum ada data.json sama sekali -- coba migrasi dari file-file
    -- versi JEYHUB sebelumnya (kalau ada), sekali saja saat ini.
    local migratedAny = false
    for _, entry in ipairs(JD_LEGACY_FILES) do
        if typeof(isfile) == "function" and isfile(entry.path) then
            local okRead2, raw2 = pcall(function() return readfile(entry.path) end)
            if okRead2 and type(raw2) == "string" then
                local okDecode2, data2 = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(raw2) end)
                if okDecode2 and type(data2) == "table" then
                    JD_Store[entry.key] = data2
                    migratedAny = true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if migratedAny then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Migrated legacy per-feature JSON files into " .. JD_PATH)
    end
end
JD_Load()

local JD_Saving = false
local JD_SavePending = false
-- Nyimpen SELURUH JD_Store (semua section sekaligus) ke 1 file --
-- di-debounce (digabung) lewat task.defer supaya kalau beberapa
-- section berubah dalam frame yang sama (misal encounter & history
-- ke-update bareng), itu jadi SATU kali writefile, bukan berkali-kali
-- beruntun.
local function JD_Save()
    if not hasFS or not HttpService then return end
    if JD_Saving then
        JD_SavePending = true
        return
    end
    JD_Saving = true
    task.defer(function()
        repeat
            JD_SavePending = false
            local okEncode, encoded = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONEncode(JD_Store) end)
            if okEncode and type(encoded) == "string" and #encoded <= JD_MAX_BYTES then
                JD_EnsureFolder()
                local okWrite, writeErr = pcall(function() writefile(JD_PATH, encoded) end)
                if not okWrite then
                    warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to write data.json:", writeErr)
                end
            elseif okEncode then
                warn("[JEYHUB] data.json skipped: abnormal data size (", #encoded, "bytes )")
            else
                warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to encode data.json:", encoded)
            end
        until not JD_SavePending
        JD_Saving = false
    end)
end

-- Ambil isi 1 section (mis. "encounters") dari store gabungan.
local function JD_Get(sectionKey, defaultValue)
    local v = JD_Store[sectionKey]
    if v == nil then return defaultValue end
    return v
end
-- Isi/timpa 1 section, lalu jadwalkan penyimpanan ke data.json.
local function JD_Set(sectionKey, value)
    JD_Store[sectionKey] = value
    JD_Save()
end

if type(task) ~= "table" then
    task = {}
end
if type(task.wait) ~= "function" then
    task.wait = function(t) return wait(t) end
end
if type(task.spawn) ~= "function" then
    task.spawn = function(fn, ...) return spawn(fn, ...) end
end
if type(task.delay) ~= "function" then
    task.delay = function(t, fn, ...)
        local args = { ... }
        return spawn(function()
            wait(t)
            fn(table.unpack(args))
        end)
    end
end
if type(task.defer) ~= "function" then
    task.defer = function(fn, ...)
        local args = { ... }
        return spawn(function() fn(table.unpack(args)) end)
    end
end

local function SafeCall(fn, ...)
    if type(fn) ~= "function" then return end
    local args = { ... }
    task.spawn(function()
        local ok, err = pcall(function() fn(table.unpack(args)) end)
        if not ok then
            warn("[JEYHUB] Runtime error caught (safe, UI keeps running):", err)
        end
    end)
end

local function SafeConnect(signal, fn)
    if not signal or type(fn) ~= "function" then return nil end
    local ok, conn = pcall(function()
        return signal:Connect(function(...)
            SafeCall(fn, ...)
        end)
    end)
    if ok then return TrackConnection(conn) end
    warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to connect signal:", conn)
    return nil
end

local function GetSignal(obj, signalName)
    if not obj then return nil end
    local ok, sig = pcall(function() return obj[signalName] end)
    if ok and sig then return sig end
    return nil
end

local function SafeSet(obj, prop, value)
    if not obj then return end
    pcall(function() obj[prop] = value end)
end

local function TryElevateIdentity()
    pcall(function()
        if typeof(setthreadidentity) == "function" then
            setthreadidentity(7)
        elseif typeof(set_thread_identity) == "function" then
            set_thread_identity(7)
        elseif typeof(syn) == "table" and typeof(syn.set_thread_identity) == "function" then
            syn.set_thread_identity(7)
        end
    end)
end
TryElevateIdentity()

local function TryHiddenGuiFns()
    local candidates = {
        "gethui", "get_hidden_gui", "gethiddenui", "get_hidden_ui",
        "protectgui", "syn_gethui",
    }
    for _, fnName in ipairs(candidates) do
        local ok, result = pcall(function()
            local fn = (typeof(getgenv) == "function" and getgenv()[fnName]) or _G[fnName]
            if typeof(fn) == "function" then return fn() end
            return nil
        end)
        if ok and result then return result end
    end
    return nil
end

local function GetGuiParent()

    local hui = TryHiddenGuiFns()
    if hui then return hui end

    for attempt = 1, 6 do
        local ok3, playerGui = pcall(function()
            if LocalPlayer then
                return LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui", 5)
            end
            return nil
        end)
        if ok3 and playerGui then return playerGui end

        local huiRetry = TryHiddenGuiFns()
        if huiRetry then return huiRetry end
    end

    local ok4, coreGui = pcall(function() return game:GetService("CoreGui") end)
    if ok4 and coreGui then return coreGui end

    warn("[JEYHUB] Couldn't find a valid parent GUI on this executor.")
    return nil
end

local SFX_IDS = {
    Hover     = { id = "rbxassetid://6895086153", vol = 0.10, speed = 2.0 },
    Click     = { id = "rbxassetid://6895079853", vol = 0.28, speed = 1.3 },
    Tab       = { id = "rbxassetid://6895079853", vol = 0.22, speed = 1.05 },
    ToggleOn  = { id = "rbxassetid://6895079853", vol = 0.35, speed = 1.6 },
    ToggleOff = { id = "rbxassetid://6895086153", vol = 0.28, speed = 0.9 },
}

local function PlayUISound(kind)
    if not UIEnableSounds then return end
    local def = SFX_IDS[kind]
    if not def then return end
    task.spawn(function()
        pcall(function()
            local coreGui = SafeService("CoreGui")
            local snd = Instance.new("Sound")
            snd.SoundId = def.id
            snd.Volume = def.vol
            snd.PlaybackSpeed = def.speed
            snd.Parent = coreGui or workspace
            snd:Play()
            game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(snd, 2)
        end)
    end)
end

local function CreateRipple(parent, x, y)
    task.spawn(function()
        pcall(function()
            parent.ClipsDescendants = true
            local ripple = Instance.new("Frame")
            ripple.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
            ripple.BackgroundTransparency = 0.6
            ripple.BorderSizePixel = 0
            ripple.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
            ripple.ZIndex = (parent.ZIndex or 1) + 1
            ripple.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
            local relX = x and (x - parent.AbsolutePosition.X) or (parent.AbsoluteSize.X / 2)
            local relY = y and (y - parent.AbsolutePosition.Y) or (parent.AbsoluteSize.Y / 2)
            ripple.Position = UDim2.new(0, relX, 0, relY)
            ripple.Parent = parent
            Instance.new("UICorner", ripple).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

            local target = math.max(parent.AbsoluteSize.X, parent.AbsoluteSize.Y) * 1.9
            local tw = TweenService:Create(ripple, TweenInfo.new(0.45, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
                Size = UDim2.new(0, target, 0, target),
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            })
            tw:Play()
            game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(ripple, 0.5)
        end)
    end)
end

local function New(class, props, children)
    local ok, inst = pcall(Instance.new, class)
    if not ok or not inst then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to create instance:", class, inst)

        local okFolder, folder = pcall(Instance.new, "Folder")
        if okFolder and folder then
            return folder
        end
        return {}
    end

    local okBorder = pcall(function()
        if inst:IsA("GuiObject") then
            inst.BorderSizePixel = 0
        end
    end)

    pcall(function()
        if inst:IsA("TextLabel") or inst:IsA("TextButton") or inst:IsA("TextBox") then
            inst.RichText = true
        end
    end)

    for k, v in pairs(props or {}) do
        local okSet, errSet = pcall(function() inst[k] = v end)
        if not okSet then
            warn(("[JEYHUB] Failed to set property '%s' on %s: %s"):format(tostring(k), class, tostring(errSet)))
        end
    end

    for _, c in ipairs(children or {}) do
        pcall(function() c.Parent = inst end)
    end

    return inst
end

local function Tween(inst, time, style, dir, props)
    if not inst or not props then return nil end
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local info = TweenInfo.new(time or 0.2, style or Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, dir or Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
        local tw = TweenService:Create(inst, info, props)
        tw:Play()
        return tw
    end)
    if ok then return result end

    pcall(function()
        for k, v in pairs(props) do inst[k] = v end
    end)
    return nil
end

local function LoopTween(inst, time, props, style)
    if not inst or not props then return nil end
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local info = TweenInfo.new(
            time or 3, style or Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
            -1, true, 0
        )
        local tw = TweenService:Create(inst, info, props)
        tw:Play()
        return tw
    end)
    if ok then return result end
    return nil
end

local function Round(inst, radius)
    New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = inst })
    return inst
end

local function Stroke(inst, color, thickness, transparency)
    return New("UIStroke", {
        Color = color or Palette.Stroke,
        Thickness = thickness or 1,
        Transparency = transparency or 0,
        ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border,
        Parent = inst,
    })
end

local function Pad(inst, l, r, t, b)
    New("UIPadding", {
        PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, l or 8),
        PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, r or 8),
        PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, t or 8),
        PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, b or 8),
        Parent = inst,
    })
end

local function AddButtonHover(btn, strokeRef, bgLift)
    if not btn then return end
    bgLift = bgLift == nil and 0.12 or bgLift
    local okBase, baseBg = pcall(function() return btn.BackgroundTransparency end)
    if not okBase then return end
    local baseStroke = nil
    if strokeRef then
        local okStroke, val = pcall(function() return strokeRef.Transparency end)
        if okStroke then baseStroke = val end
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseEnter"), function()
        if bgLift > 0 then
            Tween(btn, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = math.max(0, baseBg - bgLift) })
        end
        if strokeRef and baseStroke then
            Tween(strokeRef, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = math.max(0, baseStroke - 0.35) })
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseLeave"), function()
        if bgLift > 0 then
            Tween(btn, 0.2, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = baseBg })
        end
        if strokeRef and baseStroke then
            Tween(strokeRef, 0.2, nil, nil, { Transparency = baseStroke })
        end
    end)
end

local GRID_GAP_SCALE = 0.012
local function ColumnWidthScale(n)
    return (1 - (n - 1) * GRID_GAP_SCALE) / n
end
local GRID_CELL_PADDING = UDim2.new(GRID_GAP_SCALE, 0, 0, 10)

local COLUMN_CELL_SIZES = {
    [3] = UDim2.new(ColumnWidthScale(3), 0, 0, 140),
    [4] = UDim2.new(ColumnWidthScale(4), 0, 0, 132),
}

local function ResolveEnumValue(enumObj, names)
    for _, n in ipairs(names) do
        local ok, val = pcall(function() return enumObj[n] end)
        if ok and val then return val end
    end
    return nil
end

local function AddChevronIcon(parent, color, rightOffset)
    local holder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -(rightOffset or 16), 0.5, -5),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = (parent.ZIndex or 1) + 1,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    local barL = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 2), Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 2), Rotation = 45,
        BackgroundColor3 = color, ZIndex = holder.ZIndex, Parent = holder,
    })
    Round(barL, 1)
    local barR = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 2), Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 2), Rotation = -45,
        BackgroundColor3 = color, ZIndex = holder.ZIndex, Parent = holder,
    })
    Round(barR, 1)
    return holder
end

local function AddCloseIcon(parent, color)
    local holder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = (parent.ZIndex or 1) + 1,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    local barA = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 2), Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -6, 0.5, -1), Rotation = 45,
        BackgroundColor3 = color, ZIndex = holder.ZIndex, Parent = holder,
    })
    Round(barA, 1)
    local barB = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 2), Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -6, 0.5, -1), Rotation = -45,
        BackgroundColor3 = color, ZIndex = holder.ZIndex, Parent = holder,
    })
    Round(barB, 1)
    return holder
end

local function AddGearIcon(parent, color)
    local holder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -7, 0.5, -7),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = (parent.ZIndex or 1) + 1,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    for i, barW in ipairs({ 14, 10, 6 }) do
        local bar = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, barW, 0, 2),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -barW / 2, 0, (i - 1) * 6),
            BackgroundColor3 = color,
            ZIndex = holder.ZIndex,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        Round(bar, 1)
    end
    return holder
end

local function CreateCatalogFilterGear(hostRow, floatParent, accent)
    local gearBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 24),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Text = "",
        Parent = hostRow,
    })
    Round(gearBtn, 10)
    local gearStroke = Stroke(gearBtn, accent, 1, 0.55)
    AddButtonHover(gearBtn, gearStroke)
    AddGearIcon(gearBtn, Palette.SubText)

    local modal = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 60),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.02,
        Visible = false,
        ZIndex = 60,
        Parent = floatParent,
    })
    Round(modal, 16)
    Stroke(modal, accent, 1.2, 0.2)
    Pad(modal, 12, 12, 10, 10)
    New("UIListLayout", { Padding = UDim.new(0, 8), SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent = modal })

    local headerRow = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20), BackgroundTransparency = 1, ZIndex = 61, Parent = modal })
    New("TextLabel", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "Opsi Pencarian",
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextSize = 13,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        ZIndex = 61,
        Parent = headerRow,
    })
    local closeBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Text = "",
        ZIndex = 61,
        Parent = headerRow,
    })
    AddCloseIcon(closeBtn, Palette.SubText)

    local function fieldLabel(text, parent)
        New("TextLabel", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 14),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,

        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28),

        GetOffSale = function() return offSaleState.value end,
        GetPersonalized = function() return personalizedState.value end,
    }
end

local function CreateGridZoomControl(hostRow, accent, defaultColumns)
    local columns = defaultColumns or 4
    local layouts = {}

    local wrap = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 24),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Parent = hostRow,
    })
    Round(wrap, 10)
    Stroke(wrap, accent, 1, 0.55)
    New("UIListLayout", { FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal, SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent = wrap })

    local function applyColumns()
        local size = COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[columns] or COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[4]
        for _, layout in ipairs(layouts) do
            if layout and layout.Parent then
                pcall(function() Tween(layout, 0.18, nil, nil, { CellSize = size }) end)
            end
        end
    end

    local zoomOutBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "－",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 13,
        Parent = wrap,
    })
    local zoomInBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "＋",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 13,
        Parent = wrap,
    })
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(zoomOutBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        columns = math.min(4, columns + 1)
        applyColumns()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(zoomInBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        columns = math.max(3, columns - 1)
        applyColumns()
    end)

    return {
        RegisterGrid = function(layout)
            table.insert(layouts, layout)
            pcall(function() layout.CellSize = COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[columns] or COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[4] end)
        end,
        GetCellSize = function() return COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[columns] or COLUMN_CELL_SIZES[4] end,
    }
end

local function AddShine(frame, insetRatio)
    return nil
end

local function AddGlowPulse(frame, color, minT, maxT, duration)
    if not frame then return end
    local glow = Stroke(frame, color, 1.5, maxT or 0.75)
    task.spawn(function()
        while glow and glow.Parent do
            Tween(glow, duration or 1.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, nil, { Transparency = minT or 0.35 })
            task.wait(duration or 1.8)
            if not (glow and glow.Parent) then break end
            Tween(glow, duration or 1.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, nil, { Transparency = maxT or 0.75 })
            task.wait(duration or 1.8)
        end
    end)
    return glow
end

local function LoadThumbnail(imageLabel, url, retryOnce)
    if not imageLabel then return end
    pcall(function() imageLabel.Image = url end)
    if not ContentProvider then return end

    task.spawn(function()
        local status
        local ok = pcall(function()
            ContentProvider:PreloadAsync({ url }, function(_, fetchStatus)
                status = fetchStatus
            end)
        end)
        if not (imageLabel and imageLabel.Parent) then return end
        if ok and status == Enum.AssetFetchStatus.Failure then
            if retryOnce ~= false then
                task.wait(0.4)
                if imageLabel and imageLabel.Parent then
                    LoadThumbnail(imageLabel, url, false)
                end
            else
                pcall(function()
                    imageLabel.Image = "rbxasset://textures/ui/GuiImagePlaceholder.png"
                    imageLabel.ImageTransparency = 0.55
                    imageLabel.ImageColor3 = Palette.SubText
                    imageLabel.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function MakeDraggable(handle, target)
    if not handle or not target then return end
    local dragging = false
    local dragStart, startPos = nil, nil

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(handle, "InputBegan"), function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
            or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            dragStart = input.Position
            startPos = target.Position
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "Changed"), function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    dragging = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(input)
        if not dragging or not dragStart or not startPos then return end
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement
            or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local delta = input.Position - dragStart
            target.Position = UDim2.new(
                startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
                startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
            )
        end
    end)
end

local function NewElementRoot(parent, height)
    local root = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, height or 40),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    Round(root, 8)
    Stroke(root, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.4)
    return root
end

local function AddTitles(root, title, subtitle, rightInset)
    local holder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -(rightInset or 0), 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Pad(holder, 10, 10, 4, 4)
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Vertical,
        VerticalAlignment = Enum.VerticalAlignment.Center,
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 1),
        Parent = holder,
    })

    local titleLabel = New("TextLabel", {
        Text = (title and tostring(title)) or "Example",
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        TextSize = 13,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
        LayoutOrder = 1,
        Parent = holder,
    })

    local subtitleLabel = nil
    if subtitle and tostring(subtitle) ~= "" then
        subtitleLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            Text = tostring(subtitle),
            Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
            TextSize = 11,
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 13),
            LayoutOrder = 2,
            Parent = holder,
        })
    end

    return { Holder = holder, TitleLabel = titleLabel, SubtitleLabel = subtitleLabel }
end

local ActiveFloatingPopup = { close = nil }
local function CloseActiveFloatingPopup(exceptCloseFn)
    if ActiveFloatingPopup.close and ActiveFloatingPopup.close ~= exceptCloseFn then
        pcall(ActiveFloatingPopup.close)
    end
end
local function RegisterFloatingPopup(closeFn)
    ActiveFloatingPopup.close = closeFn
end

-- ============================================================
-- FLOATING LAYER BERSAMA
-- ============================================================
-- Dropdown & color picker (dan popup lain yang perlu "mengambang" di
-- atas segalanya) di-reparent ke ScreenGui saat dibuka, supaya tidak
-- ke-clip oleh ScrollingFrame section dan selalu tampil di paling
-- depan. MASALAHNYA: kalau langsung ke ScreenGui, mereka jadi keluar
-- dari window JEYHUB (yang punya UIScale sendiri buat fitur "perkecil
-- UI" di Settings) -- jadi popup-nya TIDAK ikut mengecil/membesar sama
-- sekali walau window utamanya sudah di-scale.
--
-- Fix-nya: semua popup sekarang di-reparent ke 1 "layer" bersama (per
-- ScreenGui, dibuat sekali lalu dipakai ulang) yang PUNYA UIScale
-- sendiri, terus-menerus di-sync ke UserUIScale yang sama dipakai
-- window utama. Posisi popup dihitung dari AbsolutePosition box aslinya
-- (sudah otomatis kena scale window), lalu DIBAGI scale layer ini
-- sebelum di-set sebagai offset -- supaya abis dikali balik sama
-- UIScale layer pas dirender, hasilnya PAS balik ke posisi layar yang
-- sama persis (bukan meleset 2x kena scale).
local FloatingLayerCache = setmetatable({}, { __mode = "k" }) -- [screenGui] = { layer=, scaleObj= }
local function GetFloatingLayer(screenGui)
    if not screenGui then return nil, nil end
    local cached = FloatingLayerCache[screenGui]
    if cached and cached.layer and cached.layer.Parent then
        pcall(function() cached.scaleObj.Scale = UserUIScale end)
        return cached.layer, cached.scaleObj
    end
    local layer = New("Frame", {
        Name = "JEYHUB_FloatingLayer",
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        ZIndex = 50,
        Parent = screenGui,
    })
    local scaleObj = New("UIScale", { Scale = UserUIScale, Parent = layer })
    FloatingLayerCache[screenGui] = { layer = layer, scaleObj = scaleObj }
    return layer, scaleObj
end
-- Dipanggil dari slider "UI Scale" di Settings supaya SEMUA floating
-- layer yang sudah pernah dibuat (mungkin lagi ada popup terbuka saat
-- itu juga) ikut nge-tween scale-nya bareng window utama, bukan cuma
-- nunggu popup itu ditutup-buka lagi baru ke-update.
local function SyncAllFloatingLayers()
    for _, entry in pairs(FloatingLayerCache) do
        if entry.scaleObj and entry.scaleObj.Parent then
            pcall(function() Tween(entry.scaleObj, 0.15, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Scale = UserUIScale }) end)
        end
    end
end

local Section = {}
Section.__index = Section

function Section.newImpl(parent, accent, title, subtitle)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Section)
    self.Accent = accent or Palette.Accent

    self.Frame = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    Round(self.Frame, 10)
    Stroke(self.Frame, self.Accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.Glass, Palette.GlassLight),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = self.Frame,
    })

    local headerHeight = (subtitle and tostring(subtitle) ~= "") and 42 or 30
    local header = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, headerHeight),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = self.Frame,
    })
    Pad(header, 10, 12, 0, 0)
    local tickBar = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 14),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -7),
        BackgroundColor3 = self.Accent,
        Parent = header,
    })
    Round(tickBar, 2)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(self.Accent, Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Rotation = 90,
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0.55),
        }),
        Parent = tickBar,
    })

    -- CATATAN: garis aksen di bawah judul/subtitle section INI SUDAH
    -- DIHAPUS sesuai permintaan -- komponen Section ini dipakai bareng
    -- oleh SEMUA tab lewat tab:CreateSection(...) (Home, Avatar Changer,
    -- Animations, Laser, Chat AI, Settings, Credits, Shade Ultimate
    -- Engine, dst). Info card (infoPanel) & info player card (infoCard)
    -- di Main tab TIDAK memakai komponen Section ini sama sekali --
    -- headernya dibangun terpisah sendiri (SectionHeader/AddGroupHeading)
    -- dengan underline masing-masing yang TETAP ADA, tidak kena imbas.

    local titleSize = (subtitle and tostring(subtitle) ~= "") and UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 16) or UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, 0)
    local titlePos  = (subtitle and tostring(subtitle) ~= "") and UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 6) or UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    New("TextLabel", {
        Text = (title and tostring(title)) or "Example",
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        TextSize = 13,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = titlePos,
        Size = titleSize,
        Parent = header,
    })

    if subtitle and tostring(subtitle) ~= "" then
        New("TextLabel", {
            Text = tostring(subtitle),
            Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
            TextSize = 11,
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 22),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 14),
            Parent = header,
        })
    end

    self.Body = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, headerHeight),
        Parent = self.Frame,
    })
    Pad(self.Body, 10, 10, 0, 10)
    New("UIListLayout", {
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 6),
        Parent = self.Body,
    })

    return self
end

function Section.new(parent, accent, title, subtitle)
    local ok, result = pcall(Section.newImpl, parent, accent, title, subtitle)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] Section failed to build, using safe fallback Section:", result)
    local fallback = setmetatable({}, Section)
    fallback.Accent = accent or Palette.Accent
    fallback.Frame = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = parent })
    fallback.Body = fallback.Frame
    return fallback
end

function Section:CreateButtonImpl(config)
    config = (type(config) == "table") and config or {}
    local root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 40)
    AddTitles(root, config.Title, config.Subtitle, 70)

    local btn = New("TextButton", {
        Text = config.ButtonText or "Run",
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        TextSize = 12,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        AutoButtonColor = false,
        BackgroundColor3 = self.Accent,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 24),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -64, 0.5, -12),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(btn, 6)

    local sheen = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.85,
        Parent = btn,
    })
    Round(sheen, 6)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.35),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
        }),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = sheen,
    })

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseEnter"), function() Tween(btn, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.AccentDark }) end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseLeave"), function() Tween(btn, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = self.Accent }) end)

    local lastClick = 0
    local function performClick()
        if os.clock() - lastClick < 0.1 then return end
        lastClick = os.clock()

        CreateRipple(btn)
        Tween(btn, 0.08, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0, 22), Position = UDim2.new(1, -62, 0.5, -11) })
        task.delay(0.08, function()
            Tween(btn, 0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 24), Position = UDim2.new(1, -64, 0.5, -12) })
        end)

        if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback) end
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseButton1Click"), performClick)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "Activated"), performClick)

    return root
end

function Section:CreateButton(config)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateButtonImpl(config) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] CreateButton failed to build, using safe fallback element:", result)
    return NewElementRoot(self.Body, 10)
end

function Section:CreateToggleImpl(config)
    config = (type(config) == "table") and config or {}
    local state = (config.Default == true)
    local root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 40)
    AddTitles(root, config.Title, config.Subtitle, 56)

    local switch = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 20),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -48, 0.5, -10),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(switch, 10)
    local switchStroke = Stroke(switch, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)
    local switchGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(self.Accent, Palette.AccentDark),
        Parent = switch,
    })

    local knob = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.5, -7),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        Parent = switch,
    })
    Round(knob, 7)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(0.82,0.82,0.85)),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = knob,
    })

    local click = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "", BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0), Parent = switch,
    })

    local function render(instant)
        local t = instant and 0 or 0.15
        SafeSet(switchGradient, "Enabled", state)
        Tween(switch, t, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = state and self.Accent or Palette.Element })
        Tween(switchStroke, t, nil, nil, {
            Color = state and self.Accent or Palette.StrokeSoft,
            Transparency = state and 0.25 or 0.5,
        })
        Tween(knob, t, nil, nil, {
            Position = state and UDim2.new(1, -17, 0.5, -7) or UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.5, -7),
            BackgroundColor3 = state and Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255) or Palette.SubText,
        })
    end
    render(true)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(click, "MouseEnter"), function()
        Tween(switchStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = state and 0.05 or 0.2 })
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(click, "MouseLeave"), function()
        Tween(switchStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = state and 0.25 or 0.5 })
    end)

    local function setVisual(on, fireCallback)
        state = (on == true)
        render(false)
        if fireCallback and config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, state) end
    end

    local lastToggle = 0
    local function toggleState()
        if os.clock() - lastToggle < 0.1 then return end
        lastToggle = os.clock()

        state = not state
        render(false)
        if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, state) end
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(click, "MouseButton1Click"), toggleState)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(click, "Activated"), toggleState)

    return { Root = root, Set = setVisual }
end

function Section:CreateToggle(config)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateToggleImpl(config) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] CreateToggle failed to build, using safe fallback element:", result)
    return { Root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 10), Set = function() end }
end

function Section:CreateSliderImpl(config)
    config = (type(config) == "table") and config or {}
    local min  = tonumber(config.Min) or 0
    local max  = tonumber(config.Max) or 100
    if max <= min then max = min + 1 end
    local step = tonumber(config.Step) or 1
    if step <= 0 then step = 1 end
    local value = math.clamp(tonumber(config.Default) or min, min, max)

    local root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 64)
    local titles = AddTitles(root, config.Title, config.Subtitle, 0)
    titles.Holder.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 36)

    local barHolder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -106, 0, 6),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 1, -17),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(barHolder, 3)

    local fill = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = self.Accent,
        Parent = barHolder,
    })
    Round(fill, 3)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(self.Accent, Palette.AccentDark),
        Parent = fill,
    })

    local sliderKnob = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -6, 0.5, -6),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Text,
        Parent = fill,
    })
    Round(sliderKnob, 6)
    Stroke(sliderKnob, self.Accent, 1, 0.5)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(0.85,0.85,0.9)),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = sliderKnob,
    })

    local minus = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "-", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 14,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 18), Position = UDim2.new(1, -84, 1, -23),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(minus, 5)
    local minusStroke = Stroke(minus, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)

    local plus = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "+", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 14,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 18), Position = UDim2.new(1, -22, 1, -23),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(plus, 5)
    local plusStroke = Stroke(plus, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)
    AddButtonHover(minus, minusStroke)
    AddButtonHover(plus, plusStroke)

    local input = New("TextBox", {
        Text = tostring(value), Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 12,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        ClearTextOnFocus = false,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 18), Position = UDim2.new(1, -60, 1, -23),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(input, 5)
    local inputStroke = Stroke(input, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "Focused"), function()
        Tween(inputStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Color = self.Accent, Transparency = 0 })
    end)

    local dragging = false

    local function setValue(v, fromDrag)
        v = tonumber(v) or value
        local steps = math.floor((v - min) / step + 0.5)
        v = math.clamp(steps * step + min, min, max)

        local decimals = 0
        local stepStr = tostring(step)
        if stepStr:find("%.") then
            decimals = #stepStr:match("%.(%d+)")
        end
        local mult = 10 ^ decimals
        v = math.floor(v * mult + 0.5) / mult

        value = v
        local pct = (value - min) / math.max(1e-6, (max - min))
        Tween(fill, fromDrag and 0.02 or 0.12, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0) })
        input.Text = tostring(value)
        if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, value) end
    end
    setValue(value, true)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minus, "MouseButton1Click"), function() setValue(value - step) end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(plus, "MouseButton1Click"), function() setValue(value + step) end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minus, "Activated"), function() setValue(value - step) end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(plus, "Activated"), function() setValue(value + step) end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "FocusLost"), function()
        Tween(inputStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Color = Palette.StrokeSoft, Transparency = 0.5 })
        local n = tonumber(input.Text)
        if n then setValue(n) else input.Text = tostring(value) end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(barHolder, "InputBegan"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            local rel = math.clamp((inp.Position.X - barHolder.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, barHolder.AbsoluteSize.X), 0, 1)
            setValue(min + rel * (max - min), true)
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputEnded"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = false
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(inp)
        if not dragging then return end
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local rel = math.clamp((inp.Position.X - barHolder.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, barHolder.AbsoluteSize.X), 0, 1)
            setValue(min + rel * (max - min), true)
        end
    end)

    return { Root = root, Set = function(v) setValue(v, true) end }
end

function Section:CreateSlider(config)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateSliderImpl(config) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] CreateSlider failed to build, using safe fallback element:", result)
    return { Root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 10), Set = function() end }
end

function Section:CreateDropdownImpl(config)
    config = (type(config) == "table") and config or {}
    local options = config.Options
    if type(options) ~= "table" or #options == 0 then
        options = { "Example A", "Example B", "Example C" }
    end
    local selected = config.Default or options[1]
    local open = false

    local root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 40)
    root.ClipsDescendants = false
    AddTitles(root, config.Title, config.Subtitle, 100)

    local box = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "", BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, 24),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -100, 0.5, -12),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(box, 6)
    local boxStroke = Stroke(box, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = box,
    })
    AddButtonHover(box, boxStroke)

    local label = New("TextLabel", {
        Text = tostring(selected), Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 11,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -18, 1, 0), Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 0),
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
        Parent = box,
    })
    local arrow = New("TextLabel", {
        Text = "v", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 10,
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText, BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 1, 0), Position = UDim2.new(1, -16, 0, 0),
        Parent = box,
    })

    local listShadow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -99, 1, 6),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.55,
        ZIndex = 200,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(listShadow, 6)

    -- FIX: dulu Frame biasa + ClipsDescendants -- kalau Options banyak
    -- (lebih dari ~4 item), sisanya ke-clip dan TIDAK BISA DIRAIH sama
    -- sekali (nggak ada scrollbar). Sekarang ScrollingFrame beneran,
    -- CanvasSize ngikutin jumlah Options -- berapa pun banyaknya, semua
    -- tetap bisa diakses lewat scroll.
    local list = New("ScrollingFrame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -100, 1, 4),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
        ScrollBarThickness = 3,
        ScrollBarImageColor3 = self.Accent,
        CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, #options * 22),
        ZIndex = 201,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(list, 6)
    Stroke(list, self.Accent, 1, 0.4)
    New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent = list })

    local popupHomeParent = list.Parent
    local repositionConn = nil
    local function updateListPosition()
        local boxPos = box.AbsolutePosition
        local boxSize = box.AbsoluteSize
        local layer, scaleObj = GetFloatingLayer(root:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui"))
        local s = (scaleObj and scaleObj.Scale) or UserUIScale
        if s <= 0 then s = 1 end
        -- box.AbsolutePosition sudah posisi LAYAR SEBENARNYA (sudah kena
        -- scale window). List sekarang ada di floating layer yang JUGA
        -- punya UIScale sendiri -- makanya offsetnya harus dibagi scale
        -- itu dulu, supaya abis dikali balik pas dirender, hasilnya PAS
        -- balik ke posisi layar yang sama persis (tepat di bawah box),
        -- bukan meleset dobel kena scale.
        list.Position = UDim2.new(0, (boxPos.X - 8) / s, 0, (boxPos.Y + boxSize.Y + 4) / s)
        listShadow.Position = UDim2.new(0, (boxPos.X - 9) / s, 0, (boxPos.Y + boxSize.Y + 6) / s)
    end
    local function floatPopup()
        local screenGui = root:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui")
        if not screenGui then return end
        local layer = GetFloatingLayer(screenGui)
        if not layer then return end
        list.Parent = layer
        listShadow.Parent = layer
        updateListPosition()
        -- FIX: dulu posisi cuma dihitung sekali di sini, jadi kalau area
        -- di-scroll SETELAH dropdown terbuka, list-nya nyangkut di posisi
        -- lama (parent-nya sudah pindah ke ScreenGui, jadi tidak ikut
        -- geser scroll bareng box aslinya). Sekarang didengarkan live
        -- lewat AbsolutePosition box -- signal ini otomatis kepicu tiap
        -- kali box bergeser karena scroll ATAU karena window JEYHUB
        -- di-drag, jadi list selalu nempel pas di bawah box.
        if repositionConn then pcall(function() repositionConn:Disconnect() end) end
        repositionConn = SafeConnect(box:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsolutePosition"), updateListPosition)
    end
    local function unfloatPopup()
        if repositionConn then
            pcall(function() repositionConn:Disconnect() end)
            repositionConn = nil
        end
        list.Parent = popupHomeParent
        listShadow.Parent = popupHomeParent
        list.Position = UDim2.new(1, -100, 1, 4)
        listShadow.Position = UDim2.new(1, -99, 1, 6)
    end

    local function closeList()
        open = false
        Tween(list, 0.15, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, 0) })
        Tween(listShadow, 0.15, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, 0) })
        Tween(arrow, 0.15, nil, nil, { Rotation = 0 })
        task.delay(0.16, function()
            pcall(function()
                if not open then
                    root.ZIndex = 1
                    unfloatPopup()
                end
            end)
        end)
    end

    for _, opt in ipairs(options) do
        local optText = tostring(opt)
        local item = New("TextButton", {
            Text = optText, Font = Enum.Font.Gotham, TextSize = 11,
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22), ZIndex = 201,
            Parent = list,
        })
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseEnter"), function() Tween(item, 0.1, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.ElementHover }) end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseLeave"), function() Tween(item, 0.1, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass }) end)

        local lastPick = 0
        local function pick()
            if os.clock() - lastPick < 0.1 then return end
            lastPick = os.clock()

            selected = opt
            label.Text = optText
            if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, selected) end
            closeList()
        end
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseButton1Click"), pick)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "Activated"), pick)
    end

    local lastOpen = 0
    local function toggleOpen()
        if os.clock() - lastOpen < 0.1 then return end
        lastOpen = os.clock()

        open = not open
        if open then
            CloseActiveFloatingPopup(closeList)
            RegisterFloatingPopup(closeList)
            root.ZIndex = 20
            floatPopup()
        end
        -- Maks tinggi dibatasi PERSIS 5 item (5*22=110) -- sisanya
        -- (berapa pun banyaknya) tinggal di-scroll pakai scrollbar tipis
        -- di pinggir, tidak lagi ke-clip dan hilang.
        local targetHeight = open and math.min(#options * 22, 110) or 0
        list.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, #options * 22)
        Tween(list, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, targetHeight) })
        Tween(listShadow, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 92, 0, targetHeight) })
        Tween(arrow, 0.18, nil, nil, { Rotation = open and 180 or 0, TextColor3 = open and self.Accent or Palette.SubText })
        if not open then
            task.delay(0.16, function()
                pcall(function()
                    if not open then
                        root.ZIndex = 1
                        unfloatPopup()
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(box, "MouseButton1Click"), toggleOpen)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(box, "Activated"), toggleOpen)

    local function setSelected(v)
        if v == nil then return end
        selected = v
        label.Text = tostring(v)
        if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, selected) end
    end

    return { Root = root, Set = setSelected }
end

function Section:CreateDropdown(config)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateDropdownImpl(config) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] CreateDropdown failed to build, using safe fallback element:", result)
    return { Root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 10), Set = function() end }
end

function Section:CreateColorPickerImpl(config)
    config = (type(config) == "table") and config or {}
    local current = config.Default or Color3.fromRGB(154, 82, 246)
    local open = false

    local root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 40)
    root.ClipsDescendants = false
    AddTitles(root, config.Title, config.Subtitle, 46)

    local swatch = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "", BackgroundColor3 = current,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 28, 0, 20),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -38, 0.5, -10),
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(swatch, 6)
    local swatchStroke = Stroke(swatch, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.3)
    AddButtonHover(swatch, swatchStroke, 0)

    local popupShadow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -139, 1, 6),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.55,
        ZIndex = 200,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(popupShadow, 8)

    local popup = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -140, 1, 4),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
        ZIndex = 201,
        Parent = root,
    })
    Round(popup, 8)
    Stroke(popup, self.Accent, 1, 0.35)
    Pad(popup, 8, 8, 8, 8)

    local popupHomeParent = popup.Parent
    local colorRepositionConn = nil
    local function updatePopupPosition()
        local swPos = swatch.AbsolutePosition
        local swSize = swatch.AbsoluteSize
        local layer, scaleObj = GetFloatingLayer(root:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui"))
        local s = (scaleObj and scaleObj.Scale) or UserUIScale
        if s <= 0 then s = 1 end
        -- Sama seperti dropdown: swatch.AbsolutePosition itu posisi LAYAR
        -- SEBENARNYA (sudah kena scale window), sedangkan popup sekarang
        -- ada di floating layer yang JUGA punya UIScale sendiri --
        -- offsetnya dibagi scale itu dulu supaya abis dikali balik pas
        -- dirender, hasilnya PAS di posisi layar yang sama persis.
        popup.Position = UDim2.new(0, (swPos.X - 112) / s, 0, (swPos.Y + swSize.Y + 4) / s)
        popupShadow.Position = UDim2.new(0, (swPos.X - 113) / s, 0, (swPos.Y + swSize.Y + 6) / s)
    end
    local function floatPopup()
        local screenGui = root:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui")
        if not screenGui then return end
        local layer = GetFloatingLayer(screenGui)
        if not layer then return end
        popup.Parent = layer
        popupShadow.Parent = layer
        updatePopupPosition()
        -- FIX: sama seperti dropdown -- dulu posisi cuma dihitung sekali
        -- di sini, jadi kalau area di-scroll SETELAH color picker dibuka,
        -- popup-nya nyangkut di posisi lama. Sekarang didengarkan live
        -- lewat AbsolutePosition swatch, otomatis update tiap kali swatch
        -- bergeser karena scroll atau window di-drag.
        if colorRepositionConn then pcall(function() colorRepositionConn:Disconnect() end) end
        colorRepositionConn = SafeConnect(swatch:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsolutePosition"), updatePopupPosition)
    end
    local function unfloatPopup()
        if colorRepositionConn then
            pcall(function() colorRepositionConn:Disconnect() end)
            colorRepositionConn = nil
        end
        popup.Parent = popupHomeParent
        popupShadow.Parent = popupHomeParent
        popup.Position = UDim2.new(1, -140, 1, 4)
        popupShadow.Position = UDim2.new(1, -139, 1, 6)
    end

    local svBox = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 70),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0),
        ZIndex = 6,
        Parent = popup,
    })
    Round(svBox, 6)
    local satGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0, 1),
        Parent = svBox,
    })

    local valOverlay = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), BackgroundTransparency = 0, ZIndex = 6, Parent = svBox,
    })
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0), Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new(1, 0),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = valOverlay,
    })

    local svCursorShadow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0,12,0,12), AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0,0,0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.5,
        ZIndex = 6, Parent = svBox,
    })
    Round(svCursorShadow, 6)
    local svCursor = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0,8,0,8), AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1),
        ZIndex = 7, Parent = svBox,
    })
    Round(svCursor, 4)
    Stroke(svCursor, Color3.new(0,0,0), 1, 0)

    local hueBar = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 14),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 78),
        ZIndex = 6,
        Parent = popup,
    })
    Round(hueBar, 6)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new({
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.00, Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.17, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,0)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.33, Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.50, Color3.fromRGB(0,255,255)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.67, Color3.fromRGB(0,0,255)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.83, Color3.fromRGB(255,0,255)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1.00, Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)),
        }),
        Parent = hueBar,
    })

    local hueCursor = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0,3,1,4), AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0.5,0), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1),
        ZIndex = 7, Parent = hueBar,
    })
    Round(hueCursor, 2)

    local okInitHSV, hue, sat, val = pcall(function() return current:ToHSV() end)
    if not okInitHSV then hue, sat, val = 0.75, 1, 1 end

    svCursor.Position = UDim2.new(sat, 0, 1 - val, 0)
    svCursorShadow.Position = UDim2.new(sat, 0, 1 - val, 0)
    hueCursor.Position = UDim2.new(hue, 0, 0.5, 0)

    local function updateColor(fireCallback)
        local ok, c = pcall(Color3.fromHSV, hue, sat, val)
        if not ok then c = current end
        swatch.BackgroundColor3 = c
        pcall(function()
            svBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, 1, 1)
            satGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromHSV(hue,0,1), Color3.fromHSV(hue,1,1))
        end)
        if fireCallback and config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, c) end
    end
    updateColor(false)

    local draggingSV, draggingHue = false, false

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(svBox, "InputBegan"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            draggingSV = true
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(hueBar, "InputBegan"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            draggingHue = true
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputEnded"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            draggingSV, draggingHue = false, false
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement and inp.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Touch then return end
        if draggingSV then
            local relX = math.clamp((inp.Position.X - svBox.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, svBox.AbsoluteSize.X), 0, 1)
            local relY = math.clamp((inp.Position.Y - svBox.AbsolutePosition.Y) / math.max(1, svBox.AbsoluteSize.Y), 0, 1)
            sat, val = relX, 1 - relY
            svCursor.Position = UDim2.new(relX, 0, relY, 0)
            svCursorShadow.Position = UDim2.new(relX, 0, relY, 0)
            updateColor(true)
        elseif draggingHue then
            local relX = math.clamp((inp.Position.X - hueBar.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, hueBar.AbsoluteSize.X), 0, 1)
            hue = relX
            hueCursor.Position = UDim2.new(relX, 0, 0.5, 0)
            updateColor(true)
        end
    end)

    local lastPicker = 0
    local function closePopup()
        open = false
        Tween(popup, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 0) })
        Tween(popupShadow, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 0) })
        task.delay(0.19, function()
            pcall(function()
                if not open then
                    root.ZIndex = 1
                    unfloatPopup()
                end
            end)
        end)
    end
    local function toggleOpen()
        if os.clock() - lastPicker < 0.1 then return end
        lastPicker = os.clock()

        open = not open
        if open then
            CloseActiveFloatingPopup(closePopup)
            RegisterFloatingPopup(closePopup)
            root.ZIndex = 20
            floatPopup()
        end
        local h = open and 100 or 0
        Tween(popup, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, h) })
        Tween(popupShadow, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, h) })
        if not open then
            task.delay(0.19, function()
                pcall(function()
                    if not open then
                        root.ZIndex = 1
                        unfloatPopup()
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(swatch, "MouseButton1Click"), toggleOpen)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(swatch, "Activated"), toggleOpen)

    local function setColor(c)
        if typeof(c) ~= "Color3" then return end
        current = c
        local okHSV, h, s, v = pcall(function() return c:ToHSV() end)
        if okHSV then hue, sat, val = h, s, v end
        updateColor(true)
    end

    return { Root = root, Set = setColor }
end

function Section:CreateColorPicker(config)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateColorPickerImpl(config) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] CreateColorPicker failed to build, using safe fallback element:", result)
    return { Root = NewElementRoot(self.Body, 10), Set = function() end }
end

local Library = {}
Library.__index = Library

function Library.newImpl(title, subtitle)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Library)
    self.Tabs = {}
    self.CurrentTab = nil

    local parent = GetGuiParent()
    if not parent then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Can't build UI: parent GUI isn't available on this executor.")
        return self
    end

    pcall(function()
        for _, child in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("ScreenGui") and typeof(child.Name) == "string" and string.find(child.Name, "JEYHUB") then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)

    local gui = New("ScreenGui", {
        Name = "JEYHUB_UNIVERSAL",
        ResetOnSpawn = false,
        ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling,
        DisplayOrder = 999,
        Parent = parent,
    })
    self.Gui = gui

    local glowOuter = New("Frame", {
        Name = "GlowOuter",
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 604, 0, 362),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.93,
        ZIndex = 0,
        Parent = gui,
    })
    Round(glowOuter, 26)
    local glowInner = New("Frame", {
        Name = "GlowInner",
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 594, 0, 350),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.86,
        ZIndex = 0,
        Parent = gui,
    })
    Round(glowInner, 22)
    self.GlowOuter = glowOuter
    self.GlowInner = glowInner

    local glowOuterScale = New("UIScale", { Scale = UserUIScale, Parent = glowOuter })
    local glowInnerScale = New("UIScale", { Scale = UserUIScale, Parent = glowInner })
    self.GlowOuterScale = glowOuterScale
    self.GlowInnerScale = glowInnerScale

    local root = New("Frame", {
        Name = "Root",
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 580, 0, 340),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.06,
        ClipsDescendants = false,
        ZIndex = 1,
        Parent = gui,
    })

    root.BackgroundTransparency = 0.25

    local rootCorner = New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = root })

    local rootStroke = Stroke(root, Palette.Accent, 1.5, 0.15)
    local rootStrokeGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.Accent, Palette.AccentDark),
        Rotation = 45,
        Parent = rootStroke,
    })

    LoopTween(rootStrokeGradient, 5, { Rotation = 225 })

    local DropShadow = New("ImageLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, -30, 0, -30),
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 60, 1, 60),
        ZIndex = 0,
        Image = "rbxassetid://13169365514",

        ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0),

        ImageTransparency = 0.85,
        ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Slice,
        SliceCenter = Rect.new(60, 60, 440, 440),
        Parent = root,
    })
    self.DropShadow = DropShadow

    local main = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
        Parent = root
    })
    New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = main })
    self.Main = main

    local rootSheen = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.45, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.92,
        ZIndex = 0,
        Parent = main,
    })
    New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = rootSheen })
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.55),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
        }),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = rootSheen,
    })

    local MouseSpotlight = New("ImageLabel", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 350, 0, 350),
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Image = "rbxassetid://8992237877",
        ImageColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        ImageTransparency = 0.88,
        ZIndex = 0,
        Parent = main,
    })

    local UserMouse = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
    if UserMouse then
        local RunService = SafeService("RunService")
        if RunService then
             local lastUpdate = 0
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunService, "RenderStepped"), function()
                local now = os.clock()
                if now - lastUpdate < 0.05 then return end
                lastUpdate = now

                if root.Visible and MouseSpotlight.Parent then
                    local relX = UserMouse.X - root.AbsolutePosition.X
                    local relY = UserMouse.Y - root.AbsolutePosition.Y
                    Tween(MouseSpotlight, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, nil, { Position = UDim2.new(0, relX, 0, relY) })
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local rootGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.Background, Color3.fromRGB(22, 16, 34)),
        Rotation = 100,
        Parent = root,
    })
    self.Root = root
    self.RootCorner = rootCorner

    local rootGradientLoop = LoopTween(rootGradient, 7, { Rotation = 130 })
    self.RootGradientLoop = rootGradientLoop

    self.SetReducedMotion = function(state)
        pcall(function()
            if state then
                if self.RootGradientLoop then
                    self.RootGradientLoop:Pause()
                end
            else
                if self.RootGradientLoop then
                    self.RootGradientLoop:Play()
                else
                    self.RootGradientLoop = LoopTween(rootGradient, 7, { Rotation = 130 })
                end
            end
        end)
    end

    local scale = New("UIScale", { Scale = 0.85, Parent = root })
    self.Scale = scale

    local topbar = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 36),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.35,
        Parent = main,
    })
    Round(topbar, 8)

    New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 8),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -8),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.35,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Parent = topbar,
    })

    local topbarDivider = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 1),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.7,
        Parent = topbar,
    })
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 1),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, 0.3),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
        }),
        Parent = topbarDivider,
    })

    local logo = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -11),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        Parent = topbar,
    })
    Round(logo, 6)
    local logoGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.Accent, Palette.AccentDark),
        Rotation = 135,
        Parent = logo,
    })
    New("TextLabel", {
        Text = "J", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack, TextSize = 13,
        TextColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1), BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), Parent = logo,
    })
    self.Logo = logo
    self.LogoGradient = logoGradient

    local titleHolder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 96, 1, 0), Position = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = topbar,
    })
    New("TextLabel", {
        Text = (title and tostring(title)) or "JEYHUB", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 14,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16), Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,4),
        Parent = titleHolder,
    })
    New("TextLabel", {
        Text = (subtitle and tostring(subtitle)) or "UNIVERSAL", Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 10,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Accent, BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 12), Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,19),
        Parent = titleHolder,
    })

    local searchWrap = New("Frame", {
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 280, 0, 24),
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
        Parent = topbar,
    })
    Round(searchWrap, 6)
    Stroke(searchWrap, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.45)

    local searchIconHolder = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 16),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0.5, -8),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = searchWrap,
    })
    local searchIconRing = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = searchIconHolder,
    })
    Round(searchIconRing, 5)
    local searchIconStroke = Stroke(searchIconRing, Palette.SubText, 1.4, 0)
    local searchIconHandle = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 1.6),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 10),
        Rotation = 45,
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        Parent = searchIconHolder,
    })
    Round(searchIconHandle, 1)

    local searchBox = New("TextBox", {
        Text = "", PlaceholderText = "Search...", ClearTextOnFocus = false,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 11, TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text, PlaceholderColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -30, 1, 0), Position = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 0),
        Parent = searchWrap,
    })
    self.SearchBox = searchBox

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBox, "Focused"), function()
        Tween(searchWrap, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.ElementHover })
        Tween(searchIconStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Color = Palette.Accent })
        Tween(searchIconHandle, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent })
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBox, "FocusLost"), function()
        Tween(searchWrap, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element })
        Tween(searchIconStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Color = Palette.SubText })
        Tween(searchIconHandle, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.SubText })
    end)

    local okTextSig, textSig = pcall(function() return searchBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text") end)
    if okTextSig then
        local searchDebounceToken = 0
        SafeConnect(textSig, function()
            searchDebounceToken = searchDebounceToken + 1
            local myToken = searchDebounceToken
            task.delay(0.12, function()
                if myToken ~= searchDebounceToken then return end -- ada ketikan baru lagi, batalkan yang ini
                if not IsCurrentRun() then return end
                local query = string.lower(searchBox.Text or "")
                if not self.CurrentTab or not self.CurrentTab.Page then return end
                for _, sectionFrame in ipairs(self.CurrentTab.Page:GetChildren()) do
                    if sectionFrame:IsA("Frame") then
                        local anyVisible = (query == "")
                        for _, root2 in ipairs(sectionFrame:GetDescendants()) do
                            if root2:IsA("Frame") and root2:GetAttribute("JeyhubSearchTitle") ~= nil then
                                local matches = query == "" or string.find(root2:GetAttribute("JeyhubSearchTitle"), query, 1, true)
                                root2.Visible = matches
                                if matches then anyVisible = true end
                            end
                        end
                        sectionFrame.Visible = anyVisible
                    end
                end
            end)
        end)
    end

    local closeBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "x", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 13,
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22), Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0.5, -11),
        Parent = topbar,
    })
    Round(closeBtn, 6)
    local minBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Text = "-", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize = 15,
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22), Position = UDim2.new(1, -56, 0.5, -11),
        Parent = topbar,
    })
    Round(minBtn, 6)

    for _, b in ipairs({closeBtn, minBtn}) do
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(b, "MouseEnter"), function() Tween(b, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.ElementHover }) end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(b, "MouseLeave"), function() Tween(b, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element }) end)
    end

    local sidebar = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 1, -36), Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 36),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = 0.5,
        Parent = main,
    })
    Round(sidebar, 8)

    New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 8),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.5,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Parent = sidebar,
    })

    New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 8, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.5,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Parent = sidebar,
    })
    local sidebarDivider = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 1, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.75,
        Parent = sidebar,
    })
    New("UIGradient", {
