        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Rotation = 90,
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 1),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, 0.3),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
        }),
        Parent = sidebarDivider,
    })
    local sidebarScroll = New("ScrollingFrame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ScrollBarThickness = 2,
        ScrollBarImageColor3 = Palette.Accent,

        VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always,
        CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0),
        AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Parent = sidebar,
    })
    Pad(sidebarScroll, 6, 6, 8, 8)
    New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Padding = UDim.new(0,4), Parent = sidebarScroll })
    self.Sidebar = sidebarScroll

    local pages = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -150, 1, -46), Position = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 36),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = main,
    })
    self.Pages = pages

    local miniIcon = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,

        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Visible = false,
        Parent = root,
    })

    local miniSheen = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.85,
        Parent = miniIcon,
    })
    New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = miniSheen })
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.45),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
        }),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = miniSheen,
    })

    local miniLabel = New("TextLabel", {
        Text = "J", Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack, TextSize = 16,
        TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1), BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), ZIndex = 2, Parent = miniIcon,
    })
    local miniLabelGradient = New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.Accent, Palette.AccentDark),
        Rotation = 135,
        Parent = miniLabel,
    })
    self.MiniLabelGradient = miniLabelGradient

    local miniScale = New("UIScale", { Scale = 1, Parent = miniIcon })
    self.MiniIcon = miniIcon

    local edgeThickness = 6
    local edgeTop = New("Frame", {
        Name = "DragEdgeTop",
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, edgeThickness),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = 5,
        Parent = root,
    })
    local edgeBottom = New("Frame", {
        Name = "DragEdgeBottom",
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, edgeThickness),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -edgeThickness),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = 5,
        Parent = root,
    })
    local edgeLeft = New("Frame", {
        Name = "DragEdgeLeft",
        Size = UDim2.new(0, edgeThickness, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = 5,
        Parent = root,
    })
    local edgeRight = New("Frame", {
        Name = "DragEdgeRight",
        Size = UDim2.new(0, edgeThickness, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -edgeThickness, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        ZIndex = 5,
        Parent = root,
    })
    self.EdgeTop, self.EdgeBottom = edgeTop, edgeBottom
    self.EdgeLeft, self.EdgeRight = edgeLeft, edgeRight

    MakeDraggable(topbar, root)
    MakeDraggable(miniIcon, root)
    MakeDraggable(sidebar, root)
    MakeDraggable(edgeTop, root)
    MakeDraggable(edgeBottom, root)
    MakeDraggable(edgeLeft, root)
    MakeDraggable(edgeRight, root)

    local function syncGlowPosition()
        SafeSet(glowOuter, "Position", root.Position)
        SafeSet(glowInner, "Position", root.Position)
    end
    syncGlowPosition()
    local okPosSignal, posSignal = pcall(function() return root:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Position") end)
    if okPosSignal then SafeConnect(posSignal, syncGlowPosition) end

    self.Minimized = false
    local savedPosition = root.Position
    local lastMinToggle = 0

    local function setMinimized(state)

        local ok, err = pcall(function()
            if self.Minimized == state then return end
            self.Minimized = state
            if state then
                savedPosition = root.Position
                SafeSet(main, "Visible", false)
                if self.DropShadow then SafeSet(self.DropShadow, "Visible", false) end

                Tween(root, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0,32,0,32), Position = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30), BackgroundTransparency = 0.45, BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 30, 55) })
                if rootCorner then Tween(rootCorner, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0) }) end

                if rootStroke then Tween(rootStroke, 0.3, nil, nil, { Thickness = 1.5, Transparency = 0 }) end
                Tween(glowOuter, 0.22, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 })
                Tween(glowInner, 0.22, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 })
                task.delay(0.05, function()
                    SafeSet(miniIcon, "Visible", true)
                    SafeSet(miniScale, "Scale", 0.6)
                    Tween(miniScale, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, nil, { Scale = 1 })
                end)
                task.delay(0.22, function()
                    SafeSet(glowOuter, "Visible", false)
                    SafeSet(glowInner, "Visible", false)
                end)
            else
                SafeSet(miniIcon, "Visible", false)
                SafeSet(glowOuter, "Visible", true)
                SafeSet(glowInner, "Visible", true)
                if self.DropShadow then SafeSet(self.DropShadow, "Visible", true) end

                Tween(root, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0,580,0,340), Position = savedPosition, BackgroundTransparency = 0.25, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background })
                if rootCorner then Tween(rootCorner, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0) }) end

                if rootStroke then Tween(rootStroke, 0.4, nil, nil, { Thickness = 1.5, Transparency = 0.15 }) end
                Tween(glowOuter, 0.32, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.93 })
                Tween(glowInner, 0.32, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.86 })
                task.delay(0.05, function()
                    SafeSet(main, "Visible", true)
                end)
            end
        end)
        if not ok then
            warn("[JEYHUB] setMinimized failed (caught safely):", err)

            self.Minimized = state
            SafeSet(main, "Visible", not state)
            SafeSet(miniIcon, "Visible", state)
        end
    end

    local function requestMinimize(state)

        if os.clock() - lastMinToggle < 0.15 then return end
        lastMinToggle = os.clock()
        -- FIX: dropdown/color picker yang lagi kebuka itu di-float ke
        -- ScreenGui LANGSUNG (sengaja keluar dari frame utama biar tidak
        -- ikut ke-clip/ZIndex kalah) -- jadi kalau nge-minimize sementara
        -- salah satu lagi kebuka, dia tidak ikut ikut hilang/mengecil
        -- bareng frame utama yang di-minimize. Tutup dulu di sini sebelum
        -- benar-benar minimize.
        if state then CloseActiveFloatingPopup(nil) end
        setMinimized(state)
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        PlayUISound("Click")
        CreateRipple(minBtn)
        requestMinimize(true)
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minBtn, "Activated"), function() requestMinimize(true) end)

    local iconPressPos = nil
    local iconDidMove = false

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(miniIcon, "InputBegan"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            iconPressPos = inp.Position
            iconDidMove = false
            Tween(miniScale, 0.1, nil, nil, { Scale = 0.92 })
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(inp)
        if not iconPressPos then return end
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local delta = (inp.Position - iconPressPos).Magnitude
            if delta > 5 then
                iconDidMove = true
            end
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(miniIcon, "InputEnded"), function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            Tween(miniScale, 0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, nil, { Scale = 1 })
            if iconPressPos and not iconDidMove and self.Minimized then
                PlayUISound("Click")
                CreateRipple(miniIcon)
                requestMinimize(false)
            end
            iconPressPos = nil
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(miniIcon, "Activated"), function()
        if self.Minimized and not iconDidMove then
            requestMinimize(false)
        end
    end)

    local function doClose()

        -- FIX: sama seperti minimize -- dropdown/color picker yang lagi
        -- kebuka itu di-float ke ScreenGui langsung, jadi tutup dulu di
        -- sini supaya list-nya ikut nutup rapi (bukan cuma ketimpa
        -- Destroy) dan tidak sempat kelihatan "nyangkut" selama animasi
        -- close 0.25 detik di bawah ini berjalan.
        CloseActiveFloatingPopup(nil)

        Tween(scale, 0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In, { Scale = 0 })
        Tween(glowOuter, 0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 })
        Tween(glowInner, 0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 })

        task.delay(0.28, function()
            pcall(function() gui:Destroy() end)
        end)
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(closeBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        PlayUISound("Click")
        CreateRipple(closeBtn)
        doClose()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(closeBtn, "Activated"), doClose)

    local introActive = not getgenv().JEYHUB_INTRO_DONE
    getgenv().JEYHUB_INTRO_DONE = true

    if introActive then
        SafeSet(main, "Visible", false)

        local introFrame = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 8, 15),
            BackgroundTransparency = 0,
            ZIndex = 50,
            Parent = root,
        })
        Round(introFrame, 8)

        local centerGlow = New("ImageLabel", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 450, 0, 450),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Image = "rbxassetid://8992237877",
            ImageColor3 = Palette.Accent,
            ImageTransparency = 1,
            ZIndex = 50,
            Parent = introFrame,
        })

        local introLogo = New("TextLabel", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, -5),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40),
            Text = (title and tostring(title)) or "JEYHUB",
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack, TextSize = 26,
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text, TextTransparency = 1,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, ZIndex = 51,
            Parent = introFrame,
        })
        local introSub = New("TextLabel", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 20),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20),
            Text = "INITIALIZING CORE",
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 9,
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText, TextTransparency = 1,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, ZIndex = 51,
            Parent = introFrame,
        })
        local barBg = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 45),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 1),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 35, 55),
            ZIndex = 51,
            Parent = introFrame,
        })
        local barFill = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Accent,
            ZIndex = 52,
            Parent = barBg,
        })
        Stroke(barFill, Palette.Accent, 1, 0.5)

        task.spawn(function()
            Tween(centerGlow, 1.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, nil, { ImageTransparency = 0.85 })
            Tween(introLogo, 1, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic, nil, { TextTransparency = 0, Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, -20) })
            PlayUISound("ToggleOn")
            task.wait(0.6)

            Tween(introSub, 0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic, nil, { TextTransparency = 0, Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 10) })
            Tween(barBg, 1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 160, 0, 1) })

            local phases = {
                {txt = "ESTABLISHING CONNECTION", size = 0.35, delay = 0.4},
                {txt = "RENDERING GLASSMORPHISM", size = 0.65, delay = 0.5},
                {txt = "BYPASSING PROTOCOLS", size = 0.90, delay = 0.4},
                {txt = "SYSTEM READY", size = 1, delay = 0.3}
            }

            for _, phase in ipairs(phases) do
                Tween(introSub, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextTransparency = 0.6 })
                task.wait(0.15)
                introSub.Text = phase.txt
                PlayUISound("ToggleOff")
                Tween(introSub, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextTransparency = 0 })

                Tween(barFill, phase.delay, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(phase.size, 0, 1, 0) })
                task.wait(phase.delay + 0.1)
            end

            PlayUISound("ToggleOn")
            task.wait(0.3)

            Tween(introLogo, 0.6, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic, Enum.EasingDirection.In, { TextTransparency = 1, Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, -40) })
            Tween(introSub, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic, Enum.EasingDirection.In, { TextTransparency = 1, Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 25) })
            Tween(barFill, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0) })
            Tween(barBg, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 1) })
            Tween(centerGlow, 0.6, nil, nil, { ImageTransparency = 1 })

            task.wait(0.5)
            SafeSet(main, "Visible", true)
            Tween(introFrame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 })

            task.delay(0.7, function()
                pcall(function() introFrame:Destroy() end)
            end)
        end)
    end

    SafeSet(scale, "Scale", 0.85)
    SafeSet(root, "BackgroundTransparency", 1)
    SafeSet(glowOuter, "BackgroundTransparency", 1)
    SafeSet(glowInner, "BackgroundTransparency", 1)
    Tween(scale, 0.35, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, nil, { Scale = UserUIScale })

    Tween(root, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.25 })

    Tween(glowOuter, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.93 })
    Tween(glowInner, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.86 })

    return self
end

function Library.new(title, subtitle)
    local ok, result = pcall(Library.newImpl, title, subtitle)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] Window creation failed entirely (caught safely):", result)
    return setmetatable({ Tabs = {}, CurrentTab = nil }, Library)
end

function Library:CreateTabImpl(name)
    if not self.Sidebar then

        return {
            CreateSection = function() return setmetatable({ Body = Instance.new("Folder") }, Section) end,
            OnBuild = function() end,
        }
    end

    name = tostring(name or "Tab")
    local accent = TabAccents[name] or Palette.Accent

    local btn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        Text = "",
        Parent = self.Sidebar,
    })
    Round(btn, 7)
    local btnGlow = Stroke(btn, accent, 1, 1)
    local tick = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 14),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0.5, -7),
        BackgroundColor3 = accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = btn,
    })
    Round(tick, 2)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(accent, Color3.new(1,1,1)),
        Rotation = 90,
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0.5),
        }),
        Parent = tick,
    })
    local label = New("TextLabel", {
        Text = name, Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 12,
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText, BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0), Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        Parent = btn,
    })

    local page = New("ScrollingFrame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ScrollBarThickness = 3,
        ScrollBarImageColor3 = accent,
        VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always,
        CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0),
        AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Visible = false,
        Parent = self.Pages,
    })
    Pad(page, 8, 8, 8, 8)
    New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Padding = UDim.new(0,8), Parent = page })

    local tabObj = {
        Name = name, Accent = accent, Page = page, Button = btn,
        Label = label, Tick = tick, Glow = btnGlow, GlowLoop = nil,
        Built = false, BuildFn = nil,
    }

    function tabObj:CreateSection(title, subtitle)
        return Section.new(self.Page, self.Accent, title, subtitle)
    end

    function tabObj:OnBuild(fn)
        self.BuildFn = fn
    end

    local library = self

    local function selectTab()
        if library.CurrentTab == tabObj then return end

        -- Ekstra pencegahan: kalau ada dropdown/color picker yang lagi
        -- kebuka (posisinya di-float ke ScreenGui), tutup dulu sebelum
        -- pindah tab -- biar tidak ada popup yang "nyangkut" ketinggalan
        -- mengambang padahal halamannya sudah disembunyikan.
        CloseActiveFloatingPopup(nil)

        for _, t in ipairs(library.Tabs) do
            if t.Page then SafeSet(t.Page, "Visible", false) end
            Tween(t.Button, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element, BackgroundTransparency = 0.2 })
            if t.Label then Tween(t.Label, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = Palette.SubText }) end
            if t.Tick then Tween(t.Tick, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 1 }) end
            if t.GlowLoop then
                pcall(function() t.GlowLoop:Cancel() end)
                t.GlowLoop = nil
            end
            if t.Glow then Tween(t.Glow, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 1 }) end
        end

        if not tabObj.Built and tabObj.BuildFn then
            tabObj.Built = true
            SafeCall(tabObj.BuildFn)
        end

        SafeSet(page, "Visible", true)
        Tween(btn, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = accent, BackgroundTransparency = 0.75 })
        Tween(label, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = Palette.Text })
        Tween(tick, 0.15, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0 })

        tabObj.GlowLoop = LoopTween(btnGlow, 1.8, { Transparency = 0.85 })
        library.CurrentTab = tabObj
    end
    tabObj.Select = selectTab

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        if library.CurrentTab ~= tabObj then
            PlayUISound("Tab")
            CreateRipple(btn)
        end
        selectTab()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "Activated"), selectTab)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseEnter"), function()
        if library.CurrentTab ~= tabObj then
            Tween(btn, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.05 })
            Tween(btnGlow, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.75 })
        end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseLeave"), function()
        if library.CurrentTab ~= tabObj then
            Tween(btn, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.2 })
            Tween(btnGlow, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 1 })
        end
    end)

    table.insert(self.Tabs, tabObj)
    if #self.Tabs == 1 then
        task.defer(selectTab)
    end

    return tabObj
end

function Library:CreateTab(name)
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return self:CreateTabImpl(name) end)
    if ok and result then return result end
    warn("[JEYHUB] Tab '"..tostring(name).."' failed to build, using safe fallback tab:", result)
    return {
        CreateSection = function() return setmetatable({ Body = Instance.new("Folder") }, Section) end,
        OnBuild = function() end,
    }
end

local function WaitForGameLoaded()
    pcall(function()
        if not game:IsLoaded() then
            local finished = false
            local conn
            conn = game.Loaded:Connect(function() finished = true end)
            local waited = 0
            while not finished and waited < 20 do
                task.wait(0.5)
                waited = waited + 0.5
            end
            if conn then pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end) end
        end
    end)
end
WaitForGameLoaded()

local Window = nil

local okWindow, windowErr = pcall(function()
    Window = Library.new("JEYHUB", "UNIVERSAL")
end)
if not okWindow or not Window then
    warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to build main window (caught safely):", windowErr)
    Window = setmetatable({ Tabs = {}, CurrentTab = nil }, Library)
end

local CreatedTabs = {}
for _, tabName in ipairs(TabOrder) do
    CreatedTabs[tabName] = Window:CreateTab(tabName)
end

local function ApplyGlobalTheme(newColor)
    if typeof(newColor) ~= "Color3" then return end
    local ok = pcall(function()
        local h, s, v = newColor:ToHSV()
        local darker = Color3.fromHSV(h, s, math.max(0, v * 0.55))

        Palette.Accent     = newColor
        Palette.Stroke     = newColor
        Palette.AccentDark = darker
        Palette.StrokeSoft = darker

        for key in pairs(TabAccents) do
            TabAccents[key] = newColor
        end

        if Window then
            SafeSet(Window.GlowOuter, "BackgroundColor3", newColor)
            SafeSet(Window.GlowInner, "BackgroundColor3", newColor)
            SafeSet(Window.LogoGradient, "Color", ColorSequence.new(newColor, darker))
            SafeSet(Window.MiniLabelGradient, "Color", ColorSequence.new(newColor, darker))

            for _, t in ipairs(Window.Tabs or {}) do
                t.Accent = newColor
                local isActive = (Window.CurrentTab == t)
                if t.Tick then
                    Tween(t.Tick, 0.2, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = newColor, BackgroundTransparency = isActive and 0 or 1 })
                end
                if t.Glow then
                    Tween(t.Glow, 0.2, nil, nil, { Color = newColor, Transparency = isActive and 0.6 or 1 })
                end
                if isActive then
                    Tween(t.Button, 0.2, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = newColor })
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    if not ok then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to apply Global Theme (caught safely).")
    end
end

local Stats = SafeService("Stats")
local HttpService = SafeService("HttpService")

local function DoHttpRequestGlobal(opts)
    local requester = (typeof(request) == "function" and request)
        or (typeof(http_request) == "function" and http_request)
        or (syn and typeof(syn.request) == "function" and syn.request)
        or (typeof(fluxus) == "table" and typeof(fluxus.request) == "function" and fluxus.request)
    if not requester then
        return nil, "This executor doesn't support outbound HTTP requests (needs 'request' / 'http_request' / 'syn.request')."
    end
    local ok, response = pcall(requester, opts)
    if not ok then return nil, tostring(response) end
    return response, nil
end

local function SafeHttpGet(url)
    local okDirect, bodyDirect = pcall(function() return game:HttpGet(url) end)
    if okDirect and type(bodyDirect) == "string" and bodyDirect ~= "" then
        return bodyDirect, nil
    end
    local response, err = DoHttpRequestGlobal({ Url = url, Method = "GET" })
    if response and (response.Success == nil or response.Success == true) and response.Body then
        return response.Body, nil
    end
    if response and response.StatusCode then
        return nil, ("HTTP " .. tostring(response.StatusCode))
    end
    return nil, err or (not okDirect and tostring(bodyDirect)) or "Request failed (unknown)."
end

local VIEWPORT_LIGHT_COLOR     = Color3.fromRGB(255, 248, 255)
local VIEWPORT_LIGHT_DIRECTION = Vector3.new(-0.4, -1, -0.6)
local VIEWPORT_AMBIENT         = Color3.fromRGB(160, 145, 190)

local function ApplyViewportLighting(viewportFrame)
    SafeSet(viewportFrame, "LightColor", VIEWPORT_LIGHT_COLOR)
    SafeSet(viewportFrame, "LightDirection", VIEWPORT_LIGHT_DIRECTION)
    SafeSet(viewportFrame, "Ambient", VIEWPORT_AMBIENT)
end

local function ComputeAvatarCameraCFrame(character, camera, opts)
    if not character or not camera then return false end
    opts = opts or {}
    local verticalBias = opts.VerticalBias or 0.6
    local tiltUp       = opts.TiltUp or 0.14

    local ok, cframe, size = pcall(function() return character:GetBoundingBox() end)
    if not ok or not cframe or not size or size.Y <= 0 then return false end

    local distance = opts.Distance or math.max(size.Y * 0.92, 3)

    local center = cframe.Position
    local lookAt = center + Vector3.new(0, size.Y * (verticalBias - 0.5), 0)
    local camPos = lookAt + Vector3.new(0, size.Y * tiltUp, -distance)

    return pcall(function() camera.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(camPos, lookAt) end)
end

local function SanitizeClonedCharacter(clone)
    if not clone then return end
    for _, v in ipairs(clone:GetDescendants()) do
        local ok, isScript = pcall(function()
            return v:IsA("Script") or v:IsA("LocalScript") or v:IsA("ModuleScript")
        end)
        if ok and isScript then pcall(function() v:Destroy() end) end
    end
end

-- Kamera FIXED (jarak TIDAK dihitung dari ukuran bounding box avatar)
-- + model yang berputar sendiri di tempat -- persis teknik yang dipakai
-- JEYHUB versi lama di tab Credits, yang terbukti nggak pernah "kamera
-- jauh". Beda dari ComputeAvatarCameraCFrame (yang menghitung jarak
-- dari GetBoundingBox() tiap frame -- bisa salah/kejauhan kalau
-- bounding box-nya sempat aneh, misal ada accessory besar atau model
-- belum full ke-load), di sini kamera cuma dihitung SEKALI (posisi &
-- arahnya tetap selamanya) -- yang muter tiap frame cuma MODEL-nya
-- sendiri lewat SetPrimaryPartCFrame, jadi kamera itu sendiri TIDAK
-- PERNAH bisa "salah hitung" dan melenceng jauh.
--
-- Paling cocok dipakai buat avatar yang direkonstruksi langsung dari
-- userId (Players:CreateHumanoidModelFromUserId) -- baik avatar yang
-- lagi offline/cuma tersimpan di JSON, maupun kartu Credits -- karena
-- avatar hasil fungsi itu selalu proporsi standar (bukan clone
-- karakter live yang scale-nya bisa ekstrem).
local function SetupFixedAvatarDisplay(model, camera, opts)
    if not model or not camera then return nil end
    opts = opts or {}
    local root = model.PrimaryPart or model:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not root then return nil end

    -- CATATAN (revisi): sebelumnya di sini sempat diubah jadi jarak yang
    -- lebih jauh dengan asumsi "kameranya kependekan" -- ternyata itu
    -- diagnosis yang SALAH. Setelah dibandingkan dengan referensi yang
    -- terbukti render-nya bagus & jaraknya pas (tab Credits versi lama),
    -- nilai (0, 1.6, -3.8) ini PERSIS SAMA dengan yang dipakai referensi
    -- itu dan hasilnya normal. Bug "avatar kelihatan blob/cacat" yang
    -- dilaporkan itu BUKAN soal jarak kamera -- itu karena model karakter
    -- (yang punya Humanoid + Motor6D joints) di-parent LANGSUNG ke
    -- ViewportFrame tanpa WorldModel, yang bikin joint-nya salah
    -- render/collapse. Sudah diperbaiki di titik pemanggilan (lihat
    -- WorldModel yang ditambahkan di tiap ViewportFrame). Nilai jarak di
    -- sini dikembalikan ke aslinya karena memang sudah benar.
    local camOffset   = opts.CamOffset or Vector3.new(0, 1.6, -3.8)
    local lookOffset  = opts.LookOffset or Vector3.new(0, 0.8, 0)
    local spinPerSec   = opts.SpinPerSec or 0.35 -- radian/detik
    local startRotRad = math.rad(opts.StartRotationDeg or 180)

    local baseRot = startRotRad
    pcall(function()
        model:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(0, 0, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, baseRot, 0))
    end)
    pcall(function()
        camera.CFrame = CFrame.new(camOffset, root.Position + lookOffset)
    end)

    local RunSvc = SafeService("RunService")
    if not RunSvc then return nil end
    local conn
    conn = SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunSvc, "RenderStepped"), function(dt)
        if not (model and model.Parent) then
            if conn then pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end) end
            return
        end
        if opts.ShouldSpin and not opts.ShouldSpin() then return end
        baseRot = baseRot + (spinPerSec * dt)
        pcall(function()
            model:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(0, 0, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, baseRot, 0))
        end)
    end)
    return conn
end

local function BuildHomeTab()
    local homeTab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Home"]
    if not homeTab or not homeTab.CreateSection then return end

    local function GreetingText()
        local hour = tonumber(os.date("%H")) or 12
        local greet = (hour < 5 and "Good evening")
            or (hour < 11 and "Good morning")
            or (hour < 15 and "Good afternoon")
            or (hour < 19 and "Good evening")
            or "Good evening"
        local name = (LocalPlayer and (LocalPlayer.DisplayName or LocalPlayer.Name)) or "Player"
        return greet .. ", " .. name .. " — ringkasan akun & performa kamu"
    end

    local section = homeTab:CreateSection("Player Overview", GreetingText())
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body
    if not body then return end

    local row = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 238),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = body,
    })
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal,
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 8),
        Parent = row,
    })

    local avatarCard = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0.36, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
        LayoutOrder = 1,
        Parent = row,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
    })
    Round(avatarCard, 18)
    Stroke(avatarCard, accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    AddShine(avatarCard, 0.1)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Element),
        Rotation = 100,
        Parent = avatarCard,
    })

    -- Scrim gelap tipis di bawah avatar card supaya name pill tetap
    -- kebaca jelas di atas viewport karakter, tanpa perlu background
    -- solid yang nutupin avatar -- sentuhan premium standar buat card
    -- yang isinya foto/render 3D.
    local scrim = New("Frame", {
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 56),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -56),
        ZIndex = 2,
        Parent = avatarCard,
    })
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(0,0,0), Color3.new(0,0,0)),
        Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 1),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0.55),
        }),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = scrim,
    })

    local nameBar = New("Frame", {
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 24),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, -15),
        AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0),
        ZIndex = 3,
        Parent = avatarCard,
    })
    Round(nameBar, 12)
    Stroke(nameBar, accent, 1, 0.35)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = nameBar,
    })
    Pad(nameBar, 8, 10, 0, 0)
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal,
        VerticalAlignment = Enum.VerticalAlignment.Center,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 5),
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Parent = nameBar,
    })

    local onlineDot = New("Frame", {
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 235, 150),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
        LayoutOrder = 1,
        Parent = nameBar,
    })
    Round(onlineDot, 3)

    local nameLabel = New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X,
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "@" .. (LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Name or "Unknown"),
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextSize = 10,
        LayoutOrder = 2,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
        Parent = nameBar,
    })

    local viewport = New("ViewportFrame", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        Parent = avatarCard,
    })
    ApplyViewportLighting(viewport)
    -- WorldModel: wadah RESMI Roblox buat naruh rig (Humanoid+Motor6D) di
    -- dalam ViewportFrame. Tanpa ini, karakter yang punya joint (Motor6D)
    -- bisa salah ke-render/collapse jadi bentuk aneh ("blob") karena
    -- solver joint-nya nggak punya konteks simulasi yang tepat. Model
    -- selalu di-parent ke SINI, bukan langsung ke `viewport`.
    local worldModel = New("WorldModel", { Parent = viewport })

    local okCam, vpCamera = pcall(Instance.new, "Camera")
    if okCam and vpCamera then SafeSet(viewport, "CurrentCamera", vpCamera) end

    local clonedChar = nil
    local avatarUpdating = false
    local rotationConnection = nil

    local function UpdateHomeAvatar()
        if avatarUpdating then return end
        avatarUpdating = true
        local ok = pcall(function()
            if clonedChar then
                pcall(function() clonedChar:Destroy() end)
                clonedChar = nil
            end

            if rotationConnection then
                pcall(function() rotationConnection:Disconnect() end)
                rotationConnection = nil
            end
            -- Bersihkan isi WorldModel SAJA (bukan seluruh viewport) --
            -- supaya WorldModel-nya sendiri nggak ikut ke-destroy tiap
            -- refresh.
            worldModel:ClearAllChildren()

            local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return end
            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 then return end

            local wasArchivable = char.Archivable
            char.Archivable = true
            clonedChar = char:Clone()
            char.Archivable = wasArchivable
            if not clonedChar then return end

            SanitizeClonedCharacter(clonedChar)
            clonedChar.Parent = worldModel
            nameLabel.Text = "@" .. LocalPlayer.Name

            if vpCamera then

                -- Jarak sedikit dijauhkan dari sebelumnya (dulu size.Y*0.92,
                -- sekarang *1.15) sesuai permintaan -- avatar Home tab
                -- kelihatan sedikit lebih "lega", nggak terlalu mepet ke
                -- kamera. Dihitung SEKALI di sini (bukan dibiarkan pakai
                -- default function) supaya posisi awal & posisi pas mulai
                -- auto-rotate konsisten -- kamera nggak "loncat" jarak.
                local okSize0, _, size0 = pcall(function() return clonedChar:GetBoundingBox() end)
                local homeDistance = (okSize0 and size0 and size0.Y > 0) and math.max(size0.Y * 1.15, 3.4) or 5

                ComputeAvatarCameraCFrame(clonedChar, vpCamera, {
                    VerticalBias = 0.6, TiltUp = 0.14, Distance = homeDistance,
                })

                local RunSvc = SafeService("RunService")
                if RunSvc then
                    local okCFrame, cframe, size = pcall(function() return clonedChar:GetBoundingBox() end)
                    if okCFrame and size.Y > 0 then
                        local center = cframe.Position
                        local lookAt = center + Vector3.new(0, size.Y * (0.6 - 0.5), 0)

                        local distance = homeDistance
                        local tiltUp = 0.14
                        local angle = 0
                        local speed = 0.6

                        rotationConnection = SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunSvc, "RenderStepped"), function(dt)
                            angle = angle + (dt * speed)
                            local offsetX = math.sin(angle) * distance
                            local offsetZ = math.cos(angle) * distance
                            local camPos = lookAt + Vector3.new(offsetX, size.Y * tiltUp, offsetZ)

                            pcall(function()
                                vpCamera.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(camPos, lookAt)
                            end)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        if not ok then warn("[JEYHUB] Failed to update Home tab avatar.") end
        avatarUpdating = false
    end

    task.spawn(UpdateHomeAvatar)
    if LocalPlayer then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(LocalPlayer, "CharacterAdded"), function()
            task.wait(0.5)
            UpdateHomeAvatar()
        end)
    end
    if Players then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(Players, "PlayerRemoving"), function(plr)
            if plr == LocalPlayer and clonedChar then
                pcall(function() clonedChar:Destroy() end)
                clonedChar = nil
            end
        end)
    end

    local infoPanel = New("ScrollingFrame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0.64, -8, 1, 0),
        Position = UDim2.new(0.36, 8, 0, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
        ScrollBarThickness = 2,
        ScrollBarImageColor3 = accent,
        VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always,
        CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
        LayoutOrder = 2,
        Parent = row,
    })
    Round(infoPanel, 18)
    Stroke(infoPanel, accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    AddShine(infoPanel, 0.1)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Element),
        Rotation = 100,
        Parent = infoPanel,
    })
    Pad(infoPanel, 12, 12, 12, 12)
    New("UIListLayout", {
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 8),
        Parent = infoPanel,
    })

    local function SectionHeader(labelText, layoutOrder)
        local header = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22),
            LayoutOrder = layoutOrder,
            Parent = infoPanel,
        })
        local dot = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -3),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
            Parent = header,
        })
        Round(dot, 3)
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack,
            Text = string.upper(labelText),
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 10,
            LetterSpacing = 1.5,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            Parent = header,
        })
        local underline = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.35,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 2),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -2),
            Parent = header,
        })
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
            Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0),
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
            }),
            Parent = underline,
        })
    end

    local function InfoRow(titleStr, layoutOrder, withCopyBtn)
        local container = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.5,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40),
            LayoutOrder = layoutOrder,
            Parent = infoPanel,
        })
        Round(container, 10)
        Stroke(container, accent, 1, 0.75)
        Pad(container, 10, 10, 6, 6)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 90,
            Parent = container,
        })

        local LABEL_W = 76
        local GAP = 8
        local COPY_RESERVE = 58

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(0, LABEL_W, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = string.upper(titleStr),
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            Parent = container,
        })

        local value = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, LABEL_W + GAP, 0, 0),
            Size = withCopyBtn
                and UDim2.new(1, -(LABEL_W + GAP + COPY_RESERVE), 1, 0)
                or UDim2.new(1, -(LABEL_W + GAP), 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "—",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 11,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            Parent = container,
        })

        if withCopyBtn then
            local copyBtn = New("TextButton", {
                Position = UDim2.new(1, -50, 0.5, -9),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 18),
                BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
                BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
                Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
                Text = "Copy",
                TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
                TextSize = 8,
                Parent = container,
            })
            Round(copyBtn, 6)
            Stroke(copyBtn, accent, 1, 0.55)
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(copyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
                local okCopy = pcall(function()
                    if typeof(setclipboard) == "function" then
                        setclipboard(value.Text)
                    elseif typeof(toclipboard) == "function" then
                        toclipboard(value.Text)
                    end
                end)
                local original = copyBtn.Text
                copyBtn.Text = okCopy and "OK!" or "N/A"
                task.delay(1, function()
                    pcall(function() copyBtn.Text = original end)
                end)
            end)
        end

        return value
    end

    local function CreateStatCard(parent, titleStr, layoutOrder)
        local card = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.12,
            Size = UDim2.new(1 / 3, -5, 1, 0),
            LayoutOrder = layoutOrder,
            Parent = parent,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
        })
        Round(card, 12)
        Stroke(card, accent, 1.1, 0.55)
        AddShine(card, 0.12)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 90,
            Parent = card,
        })

        local statusStrip = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 3),
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(statusStrip, 2)

        local valueLbl = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 10),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack,
            Text = "—",
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 15,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            Parent = card,
        })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -16),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 12),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = string.upper(titleStr),
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 7.5,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            Parent = card,
        })
        return valueLbl, statusStrip
    end

    local function Spacer(h, lo)
        New("Frame", { BackgroundTransparency = 1, Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, h), LayoutOrder = lo, Parent = infoPanel })
    end

    local ISLAND_KEYWORDS = {
        { "Jakarta", "Pulau Jawa" },
        { "Java", "Pulau Jawa" },
        { "Jawa", "Pulau Jawa" },
        { "Sumatra", "Pulau Sumatera" },
        { "Sumatera", "Pulau Sumatera" },
        { "Kalimantan", "Pulau Kalimantan" },
        { "Borneo", "Pulau Kalimantan" },
        { "Sulawesi", "Pulau Sulawesi" },
        { "Celebes", "Pulau Sulawesi" },
        { "Papua", "Pulau Papua" },
        { "Bali", "Bali & Nusa Tenggara" },
        { "Nusa Tenggara", "Bali & Nusa Tenggara" },
        { "Maluku", "Kepulauan Maluku" },
        { "Molucca", "Kepulauan Maluku" },
    }
    local function GuessIsland(provinceName, cityName, countryName)
        if countryName and countryName ~= "" and countryName ~= "Indonesia" and countryName ~= "Unknown" and countryName ~= "N/A" then
            return "-"
        end
        local haystack = string.lower(tostring(provinceName or "") .. " " .. tostring(cityName or ""))
        for _, pair in ipairs(ISLAND_KEYWORDS) do
            if string.find(haystack, string.lower(pair[1]), 1, true) then
                return pair[2]
            end
        end
        return "Other"
    end

    local playerIP, playerRegionCode, playerProvince, playerCountry, playerCity, playerIsland =
        "Fetching...", "Fetching...", "Fetching...", "Fetching...", "Fetching...", "Fetching..."
    task.spawn(function()
        for attempt = 1, 3 do
            local ok, result = pcall(function()
                local response = game:HttpGetAsync("http://ip-api.com/json/")
                return HttpService and HttpService:JSONDecode(response)
            end)
            if ok and result and result.status == "success" then
                playerIP = result.query or "Hidden"
                playerRegionCode = result.region or "Unknown"
                playerProvince = result.regionName or "Unknown"
                playerCountry = result.country or "Unknown"
                playerCity = result.city or "Unknown"
                playerIsland = GuessIsland(playerProvince, playerCity, playerCountry)
                return
            end
            task.wait(2 * attempt)
        end
        playerIP, playerRegionCode, playerProvince, playerCountry, playerCity, playerIsland =
            "Unavailable", "N/A", "N/A", "N/A", "N/A", "N/A"
    end)

    SectionHeader("OVERVIEW", 0)

    local kpiRow = New("Frame", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 52),
        LayoutOrder = 1,
        Parent = infoPanel,
    })
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal,
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 6),
        Parent = kpiRow,
    })
    local lblPing, pingStrip = CreateStatCard(kpiRow, "Ping", 1)
    local lblFPS, fpsStrip = CreateStatCard(kpiRow, "FPS", 2)
    local lblPlayers = CreateStatCard(kpiRow, "Players", 3)

    Spacer(2, 5)
    SectionHeader("PLAYER", 10)
    local lblTime = InfoRow("Local Time", 11)
    local lblName = InfoRow("Username", 12)
    lblName.Text = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Name or "N/A"
    local lblDisplay = InfoRow("Display Name", 13)
    lblDisplay.Text = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.DisplayName or "N/A"
    local lblId = InfoRow("User ID", 14, true)
    lblId.Text = LocalPlayer and tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId) or "N/A"
    local lblAge = InfoRow("Account Age", 15)
    if LocalPlayer then
        local days = LocalPlayer.AccountAge
        if days >= 365 then
            local years = math.floor(days / 365)
            local remDays = days % 365
            lblAge.Text = string.format("%dy %dd", years, remDays)
        else
            lblAge.Text = tostring(days) .. " days"
        end
    else
        lblAge.Text = "N/A"
    end

    Spacer(4, 19)
    SectionHeader("NETWORK", 20)
    local lblIP = InfoRow("IP Address", 21, true)
    local lblRegion = InfoRow("Region", 22)
    local lblIsland = InfoRow("Pulau", 23)
    local lblProvince = InfoRow("Provinsi", 24)
    local lblCity = InfoRow("Kota", 25)

    local frameCount, lastFPS = 0, 60
    local RunService = SafeService("RunService")
    if RunService then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunService, "Heartbeat"), function() frameCount = frameCount + 1 end)
    end

    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(1) do
            if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
            if not (lblTime and lblTime.Parent) then break end
            lastFPS = frameCount
            frameCount = 0

            pcall(function() lblTime.Text = os.date("%H:%M:%S") end)
            lblIP.Text = playerIP
            lblRegion.Text = playerRegionCode
            lblIsland.Text = playerIsland
            lblProvince.Text = playerProvince
            lblCity.Text = playerCity

            local ping = 0
            if Stats then pcall(function() ping = Stats.PerformanceStats.Ping:GetValue() end) end
            lblPing.Text = string.format("%d", ping)
            local pingColor = ping < 80 and Color3.fromRGB(100, 245, 155)
                or (ping < 150 and Color3.fromRGB(255, 215, 80) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 90, 90))
            lblPing.TextColor3 = pingColor
            Tween(pingStrip, 0.4, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = pingColor })

            lblFPS.Text = string.format("%d", lastFPS)
            local fpsColor = lastFPS >= 55 and Color3.fromRGB(100, 245, 155)
                or (lastFPS >= 30 and Color3.fromRGB(255, 215, 80) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 90, 90))
            lblFPS.TextColor3 = fpsColor
            Tween(fpsStrip, 0.4, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = fpsColor })

            local count = 0
            if Players then pcall(function() count = #Players:GetPlayers() end) end
            lblPlayers.Text = tostring(count)
        end
    end)
end

local function BuildMainTab()
    local mainTab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Main"]
    if not mainTab or not mainTab.CreateSection then return end
    local Stats = {}

    local mainAccent = mainTab.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local wrapper = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -14),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = mainTab.Page,
    })
    if mainTab.Page then
        pcall(function() mainTab.Page.ScrollingEnabled = false end)
    end

    local accent = mainAccent or Palette.Accent

    local premiumCard = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.22,
        Parent = wrapper,
    })
    Round(premiumCard, 16)
    Stroke(premiumCard, accent, 1.1, 0.45)
    AddShine(premiumCard, 0.12)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = premiumCard,
    })

    local body = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = premiumCard,
    })
    Pad(body, 10, 10, 10, 10)
    New("UIListLayout", {

    local function MakeChip(parent, text, bg)
        local chip = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = bg or accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 16),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X,
            Visible = false,
            Parent = parent,
        })
        Round(chip, 8)
        New("UIPadding", { PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 7), PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 7), Parent = chip })
        local chipLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X,
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = text or "",
            TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
            TextSize = 8,
            Parent = chip,
        })
        return chip, chipLabel
    end

    local function AddGroupHeading(order, text, subtitle)
        -- CATATAN: subtitle di bawah judul section SUDAH DIHAPUS sesuai
        -- permintaan -- parameter `subtitle` sengaja tetap diterima biar
        -- semua pemanggilan AddGroupHeading(...) di bawah tidak perlu
        -- diubah satu-satu, tapi memang tidak pernah dirender lagi.
        local holder = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 18),
            LayoutOrder = order,
            Parent = infoCard,
        })
        local dot = New("Frame", {
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 1),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        Round(dot, 3)
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 12),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = text,
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 9,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        local underline = New("Frame", {
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -2),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 2),
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.35,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(1,1,1)),
            Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0),
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
            }),
            Parent = underline,
        })
        table.insert(statToggleFrames, holder)
        return holder
    end

    local WrapTextService = SafeService("TextService")
    local function MakeAutoWrapLabel(lbl)
        lbl.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.None
        local resizing = false
        local function Resize()
            if resizing then return end
            resizing = true
            local width = lbl.AbsoluteSize.X
            if width <= 1 then

                resizing = false
                task.defer(function() pcall(Resize) end)
                return
            end
            if WrapTextService then
                local okSize, textSize = pcall(function()
                    return WrapTextService:GetTextSize(lbl.Text, lbl.TextSize, lbl.Font, Vector2.new(width, 100000))
                end)
                if okSize and textSize then
                    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, math.ceil(textSize.Y) + 2)
                end
            end
            resizing = false
        end
        SafeConnect(lbl:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"), Resize)
        SafeConnect(lbl:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteSize"), Resize)
        task.defer(Resize)
        return lbl
    end

    local emptyStateLbl = New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        Text = "No target available to select in this server yet.",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 10,
        TextWrapped = true,
        Visible = false,
        LayoutOrder = 1,
        Parent = infoCard,
    })

    local TargetPlayers = {}
    local CurrentTargetIndex = 0
    local clonedTargetChar = nil
    local targetRotationConnection = nil

    local autoRotate = true
    local rotateSpeed = 0.6

    local PlayerCache = {}
    local OfflineOrder = {}

    local AssetNameCache = {}
    local MarketplaceServiceRef = SafeService("MarketplaceService")
    local function GetAssetName(assetId)
        if not assetId or assetId == 0 then return nil end
        if AssetNameCache[assetId] ~= nil then
            local cached = AssetNameCache[assetId]
            return (cached ~= false) and cached or nil
        end
        local name = nil
        if MarketplaceServiceRef then
            local ok, info = pcall(function()
                return MarketplaceServiceRef:GetProductInfo(assetId, Enum.InfoType.Asset)
            end)
            if ok and type(info) == "table" and type(info.Name) == "string" and info.Name ~= "" then
                name = info.Name
            end
        end
        AssetNameCache[assetId] = name or false
        return name
    end

    local function ExtractAnimId(animIdString)
        if type(animIdString) ~= "string" then return nil end
        local numStr = string.match(animIdString, "(%d+)%D*$")
        return numStr and tonumber(numStr) or nil
    end

    local function GetOfficialAnimationIds(character)
        local ids = {}
        if not character then return ids end
        local animateScript = character:FindFirstChild("Animate")
        if not animateScript then return ids end
        local okScan = pcall(function()
            for _, inst in ipairs(animateScript:GetDescendants()) do
                if inst:IsA("Animation") then
                    local id = ExtractAnimId(inst.AnimationId)
                    if id then ids[id] = true end
                end
            end
        end)
        if not okScan then return {} end
        return ids
    end

    local function DefaultStatsText()
        return {
            hp = "- / -", hpFillSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0), hpFillColor = nil,
            walkSpeed = "-", jumpPower = "-", tool = "-",
            distance = "-", position = "-", inventory = "-",
            leaderstats = "-", afk = "-",
            respawnCount = "-",
            statAnomaly = "-",
            nearestPlayer = "-",
        }
    end

    local function SnapshotPlayer(p)
        local snap = {
            userId = p.UserId,
            name = p.Name,
            displayName = (p.DisplayName and p.DisplayName ~= "") and p.DisplayName or p.Name,
        }
        pcall(function() snap.accountAge = p.AccountAge end)
        pcall(function() snap.isPremium = (p.MembershipType == Enum.MembershipType.Premium) end)
        pcall(function() snap.membershipName = p.MembershipType.Name end)
        pcall(function() snap.hasVerifiedBadge = p.HasVerifiedBadge end)
        pcall(function() snap.localeId = p.LocaleId end)
        pcall(function() snap.teamName = p.Team and p.Team.Name or "None" end)
        pcall(function()
            if p.Team and p.TeamColor then
                local c = p.TeamColor.Color
                snap.teamColorHex = string.format("#%02X%02X%02X", c.R * 255, c.G * 255, c.B * 255)
            end
        end)
        pcall(function() snap.isFriend = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer:IsFriendsWith(p.UserId) end)
        return snap
    end

    local function EnsureCache(userId)
        if not PlayerCache[userId] then
            PlayerCache[userId] = {
                online = false,
                statsText = DefaultStatsText(),

                firstSeenTick = tick(),
                lastPos = nil, lastMoveTick = tick(),

                respawnCount = 0, chatHooked = false, respawnHooked = false,
                lastChatMsg = "No messages monitored yet", chatCount = 0,

                chatLog = {},

                animLog = {},
                animHooked = false,
                officialAnimIds = nil,

                cheatPos = nil, cheatTick = nil,
                cheatLookVec = nil, cheatSpinHits = 0,
                cheatFlyTicks = 0,
                cheatTeleportHits = 0,
                cheatFlags = {},
                isUsingLaser = false,
            }
        end
        return PlayerCache[userId]
    end

    local CHAT_LOG_MAX = 200
    local ANIM_LOG_MAX = 150

    -- CATATAN: fitur label 3D "LASER" yang mengambang di atas kepala target
    -- sudah DIHAPUS sesuai permintaan. Deteksi & chip "LASER" di kartu info
    -- (badge row) tetap dipertahankan -- cuma tag yang muncul di dunia
    -- game di atas kepala yang dihilangkan.

    local function HookCharacterAnimations(p, character)
        if not character then return end
        local c = EnsureCache(p.UserId)

        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid then return end
        local okAnimator, animator = pcall(function()
            return humanoid:WaitForChild("Animator", 3)
        end)
        if not okAnimator or not animator then return end

        c.officialAnimIds = GetOfficialAnimationIds(character)

        -- Cek animasi yang SUDAH lagi jalan SAAT hook ini pertama kali
        -- dipasang (mis. player sudah lebih dulu ada di server & sudah
        -- lebih dulu mainin animasi laser sebelum kita sempat mantau) --
        -- AnimationPlayed di bawah cuma nangkep animasi yang BARU
        -- diputar setelah ini, jadi tanpa pengecekan ini, animasi yang
        -- sudah terlanjur lagi jalan akan terlewat.
        pcall(function()
            for _, track in ipairs(animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                local anim = track.Animation
                if anim then
                    local id = ExtractAnimId(anim.AnimationId)
                    if id == 70883871260184 then
                        c.isUsingLaser = true
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        SafeConnect(animator.AnimationPlayed, function(track)
            local okLog = pcall(function()
                local anim = track.Animation
                if not anim then return end
                local id = ExtractAnimId(anim.AnimationId)
                if not id then return end
                local name = GetAssetName(id)
                local isOriginal = c.officialAnimIds and c.officialAnimIds[id] == true

                c.animLog = c.animLog or {}
                table.insert(c.animLog, 1, {
                    id = id,
                    name = name or "Unknown Asset",
                    trackName = (track.Name ~= "" and track.Name) or "Animation",
                    original = isOriginal,
                    at = os.time(),
                })
                while #c.animLog > ANIM_LOG_MAX do table.remove(c.animLog) end

                -- Deteksi "Laser" -- Animation ID spesifik 70883871260184.
                -- STICKY: begitu ketahuan sekali, c.isUsingLaser TIDAK
                -- pernah di-set balik ke false lagi di sini (dibiarkan
                -- true selamanya untuk sesi ini) -- dipakai buat chip
                -- "LASER" di badge row kartu info. Ini jalan untuk SEMUA
                -- player yang lagi online (HookPlayerTracking dipasang ke
                -- semua orang di RefreshPlayerList), bukan cuma target
                -- yang lagi diselect di kartu Main tab.
                if id == 70883871260184 then
                    c.isUsingLaser = true
                end
            end)
            if not okLog then return end
        end)
    end

    -- Forward-declare (diisi belakangan, di dekat sistem histori player
    -- di bawah) supaya RefreshPlayerList, PlayerRemoving, DAN
    -- HookPlayerTracking bisa manggil ini sebagai upvalue yang sama persis.
    local PersistPlayerSnapshot = nil
    local PersistLastSeen = nil
    local PersistExtendedField = nil
    local PersistChatLog = nil
    local PlayerHistory = nil -- diisi ke {} saat sistem histori di bawah diinisialisasi

    -- Berapa banyak pesan chat per player yang dipersist ke disk (beda
    -- sama CHAT_LOG_MAX yang buat batas tampilan in-memory selama sesi --
    -- ini sengaja lebih kecil supaya file JSON gabungan tidak membengkak
    -- kalau sudah ketemu ratusan player).
    local CHAT_LOG_PERSIST_MAX = 50

    -- Bersihin & batasi 1 entri chat log biar aman ditulis ke JSON
    -- (teks dipotong, timestamp harus number) -- dipakai buat persist
    -- MAUPUN buat validasi pas load balik dari file.
    local function SanitizeChatLogForPersist(log)
        if type(log) ~= "table" then return nil end
        local out = {}
        for i = 1, math.min(#log, CHAT_LOG_PERSIST_MAX) do
            local entry = log[i]
            if type(entry) == "table" and type(entry.text) == "string" then
                local text = entry.text
                if #text > 300 then text = text:sub(1, 300) end
                table.insert(out, { text = text, at = (type(entry.at) == "number" and entry.at) or os.time() })
            end
        end
        return #out > 0 and out or nil
    end

    local function HookPlayerTracking(p)
        local c = EnsureCache(p.UserId)
        if not c.chatHooked then
            c.chatHooked = true
            pcall(function()
                SafeConnect(p.Chatted, function(msg)
                    local text = (type(msg) == "string" and msg ~= "") and msg or "(pesan kosong)"
                    c.lastChatMsg = text
                    c.chatCount = (c.chatCount or 0) + 1
                    c.chatLog = c.chatLog or {}
                    table.insert(c.chatLog, 1, { text = text, at = os.time() })
                    while #c.chatLog > CHAT_LOG_MAX do table.remove(c.chatLog) end
                    -- FIX: chat log sekarang juga dipersist ke disk, bukan
                    -- cuma disimpan di memori selama sesi ini saja.
                    if PersistChatLog then PersistChatLog(p.UserId, c.chatLog) end
                end)
            end)
        end
        if not c.respawnHooked then
            c.respawnHooked = true
            pcall(function()
                SafeConnect(p.CharacterAdded, function(newChar)
                    c.respawnCount = (c.respawnCount or 0) + 1
                    task.defer(function()
                        pcall(function() HookCharacterAnimations(p, newChar) end)
                    end)
                end)
            end)
        end
        if not c.animHooked then
            c.animHooked = true
            if p.Character then
                pcall(function() HookCharacterAnimations(p, p.Character) end)
            end
        end
    end

    local function RefreshPlayerList()

        local previousUserId = TargetPlayers[CurrentTargetIndex]

        TargetPlayers = {}
        local seen = {}

        if LocalPlayer then
            table.insert(TargetPlayers, LocalPlayer.UserId)
            seen[LocalPlayer.UserId] = true
            local c = EnsureCache(LocalPlayer.UserId)
            c.online = true
            c.snapshot = SnapshotPlayer(LocalPlayer)
            HookPlayerTracking(LocalPlayer)
        end
        for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if not seen[p.UserId] then
                table.insert(TargetPlayers, p.UserId)
                seen[p.UserId] = true
                local c = EnsureCache(p.UserId)
                c.online = true
                c.snapshot = SnapshotPlayer(p)
                if PersistPlayerSnapshot then PersistPlayerSnapshot(p.UserId, c.snapshot) end
                HookPlayerTracking(p)
            end
        end

        for _, uid in ipairs(OfflineOrder) do
            if not seen[uid] and PlayerCache[uid] then
                table.insert(TargetPlayers, uid)
                seen[uid] = true
            end
        end

        if previousUserId then
            for i, uid in ipairs(TargetPlayers) do
                if uid == previousUserId then
                    CurrentTargetIndex = i
                    return
                end
            end
        end
        if CurrentTargetIndex > #TargetPlayers then CurrentTargetIndex = #TargetPlayers end
        if CurrentTargetIndex < 1 and #TargetPlayers > 0 then CurrentTargetIndex = 1 end
    end

    -- Encounter tracker sekarang nyimpen datanya di section "encounters"
    -- pada file JSON gabungan JEYHUB/data.json (lihat modul JD_* di awal
    -- file) -- bukan file encounters.json terpisah lagi.
    local CurrentJobId = (type(game.JobId) == "string" and game.JobId ~= "")
        and game.JobId
        or ("local-" .. tostring(os.time()) .. "-" .. tostring(math.random(100000, 999999)))

    local EncounterData = {}

    local function saveEncounterData()
        JD_Set("encounters", EncounterData)
    end

    local function loadEncounterData()
        local data = JD_Get("encounters", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end

        local clean = {}
        for key, v in pairs(data) do
            if type(key) == "string" and type(v) == "table" and type(v.count) == "number" then
                local history = {}
                if type(v.history) == "table" then
                    for _, t in ipairs(v.history) do
                        if type(t) == "number" then table.insert(history, t) end
                    end
                end
                clean[key] = {
                    count = math.max(0, math.floor(v.count)),
                    lastSeen = (type(v.lastSeen) == "number") and v.lastSeen or nil,
                    firstSeen = (type(v.firstSeen) == "number") and v.firstSeen or nil,
                    lastJobId = (type(v.lastJobId) == "string") and v.lastJobId or nil,
                    name = (type(v.name) == "string") and v.name or nil,
                    history = history,
                }
            end
        end
        EncounterData = clean
    end

    loadEncounterData()

    local ENC_HISTORY_MAX = 30 -- batas wajar per player -- histori terlalu panjang cuma bikin file membengkak tanpa nambah manfaat

    -- Forward-declare (diisi function-nya belakangan, di dekat sistem
    -- Leaderboard di bawah) supaya RecordEncounter bisa manggil ini
    -- sebagai upvalue yang sama persis -- Lua butuh local-nya dideklarasi
    -- SEBELUM closure yang makai dibuat, walau isinya baru diisi belakangan.
    local RefreshLeaderboardDisplay = nil

    local function RecordEncounter(plr)
        if not plr or plr == LocalPlayer then return end
        local ok, userId = pcall(function() return plr.UserId end)
        if not ok or not userId then return end
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = EncounterData[key]
        if entry and entry.lastJobId == CurrentJobId then return end
        if not entry then
            entry = { count = 0, history = {} }
            EncounterData[key] = entry
        end
        entry.history = entry.history or {}
        local now = os.time()
        entry.count = (entry.count or 0) + 1
        entry.firstSeen = entry.firstSeen or now
        entry.lastSeen = now
        entry.lastJobId = CurrentJobId
        table.insert(entry.history, 1, now) -- terbaru di depan
        while #entry.history > ENC_HISTORY_MAX do table.remove(entry.history) end
        pcall(function() entry.name = plr.Name end)
        saveEncounterData()

        -- PENTING: pastikan player yang baru saja tercatat "bertemu" ini
        -- juga punya snapshot LENGKAP di PlayerHistory (bukan cuma nama
        -- doang di EncounterData) -- supaya dia bisa dicek profil, umur
        -- akun, membership, dst persis seperti player yang sudah offline
        -- lain, sekalipun sesi kali ini dia cuma sempat kelihatan sebentar
        -- lalu keluar sebelum RefreshPlayerList/PlayerRemoving sempat
        -- menyimpan snapshot-nya sendiri.
        pcall(function()
            local c = EnsureCache(userId)
            c.snapshot = SnapshotPlayer(plr)
            if PersistPlayerSnapshot then PersistPlayerSnapshot(userId, c.snapshot) end
        end)

        if RefreshLeaderboardDisplay then RefreshLeaderboardDisplay() end
    end

    local function GetEncounterCount(userId)
        local entry = EncounterData[tostring(userId)]
        return entry and entry.count or 0
    end

    -- Info lengkap 1 player: total, kapan pertama & terakhir ketemu, dan
    -- daftar timestamp tiap pertemuan (terbaru dulu).
    local function GetEncounterInfo(userId)
        local entry = EncounterData[tostring(userId)]
        if not entry then return { count = 0, firstSeen = nil, lastSeen = nil, history = {} } end
        return {
            count = entry.count or 0,
            firstSeen = entry.firstSeen,
            lastSeen = entry.lastSeen,
            history = entry.history or {},
        }
    end

    for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        RecordEncounter(plr)
    end

    -- ============================================================
    -- CATATAN PRIBADI: catatan manual per player (mis. "baik", "toxic"),
    -- sekarang di section "playerNotes" pada file JSON gabungan yang
    -- sama (JEYHUB/data.json) -- bukan file player_notes.json terpisah.
    -- ============================================================
    local NOTE_MAX_LEN = 500 -- batas wajar per catatan
    local PlayerNotes = {} -- [userIdString] = { note=, updatedAt=, name= }

    local function saveNotesData()
        JD_Set("playerNotes", PlayerNotes)
    end

    local function loadNotesData()
        local data = JD_Get("playerNotes", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end
        local clean = {}
        for key, v in pairs(data) do
            if type(key) == "string" and type(v) == "table" and type(v.note) == "string" then
                clean[key] = {
                    note = v.note,
                    updatedAt = (type(v.updatedAt) == "number") and v.updatedAt or nil,
                    name = (type(v.name) == "string") and v.name or nil,
                }
            end
        end
        PlayerNotes = clean
    end

    loadNotesData()

    local function SetPlayerNote(userId, text, plrForName)
        local key = tostring(userId)
        text = tostring(text or "")
        if #text > NOTE_MAX_LEN then text = text:sub(1, NOTE_MAX_LEN) end
        if text == "" then
            PlayerNotes[key] = nil
        else
            local entry = PlayerNotes[key] or {}
            entry.note = text
            entry.updatedAt = os.time()
            if plrForName then pcall(function() entry.name = plrForName.Name end) end
            PlayerNotes[key] = entry
        end
        saveNotesData()
    end

    local function GetPlayerNote(userId)
        local entry = PlayerNotes[tostring(userId)]
        return (entry and entry.note) or "", entry and entry.updatedAt or nil
    end

    -- ============================================================
    -- HISTORI PLAYER PERSISTEN: semua player yang PERNAH ditemui (lintas
    -- sesi/rejoin) sekarang di section "playerHistory" pada file JSON
    -- gabungan yang sama (JEYHUB/data.json) -- mencakup snapshot
    -- profil (SnapshotPlayer: username, display name, account age,
    -- premium, verified, dll) DAN field "extended" yang butuh HTTP fetch
    -- (Bio, Groups, Followers, dst).
    --
    -- Field yang TIDAK disimpan: semua yang sifatnya live/real-time saat
    -- player online di server ini (WalkSpeed, Position, Distance, AFK,
    -- Session Time, Nearest Player, Stat Anomaly, dst) -- itu memang cuma
    -- valid selagi player ada di map, jadi tidak masuk akal dipersist.
    --
    -- Status online/offline TETAP ditentukan sepenuhnya oleh apakah
    -- player itu ada di Players:GetPlayers() SEKARANG (lihat RefreshPlayerList
    -- & UpdateTargetUI) -- history ini cuma menyediakan DATA-nya supaya
    -- begitu player itu offline (keluar map / rejoin script), profil &
    -- entrinya tetap muncul di list, bukan hilang.
    -- ============================================================
    PlayerHistory = {} -- [userIdString] = { snapshot = {...}, lastSeenAt = , extended = {...} }

    local function saveHistoryData()
        JD_Set("playerHistory", PlayerHistory)
    end

    -- Whitelist field snapshot yang boleh masuk (jaga-jaga kalau
    -- SnapshotPlayer nanti nambah field baru yang tipenya aneh/besar).
    local HIST_SNAPSHOT_KEYS = {
        "userId", "name", "displayName", "accountAge", "isPremium",
        "membershipName", "hasVerifiedBadge", "localeId", "teamName",
        "teamColorHex", "isFriend",
    }
    local HIST_EXTENDED_KEYS = {
        "bio", "socialLinks", "ugcItems", "gameBadges", "gamesCreated",
        "favoriteGames", "usernameHistory", "friendsCount", "followers",
        "following", "groups", "allGroups", "primaryGroup", "gameGroupRank",
        "bodyParts", "equippedEmotes", "inventory",
    }

    local function cleanBySchema(tbl, allowedKeys)
        if type(tbl) ~= "table" then return nil end
        local out = {}
        local any = false
        for _, k in ipairs(allowedKeys) do
            local v = tbl[k]
            if v ~= nil and (type(v) == "string" or type(v) == "number" or type(v) == "boolean") then
                out[k] = v
                any = true
            end
        end
        return any and out or nil
    end

    local function loadHistoryData()
        local data = JD_Get("playerHistory", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end
        local clean = {}
        for key, v in pairs(data) do
            if type(key) == "string" and type(v) == "table" then
                local snap = cleanBySchema(v.snapshot, HIST_SNAPSHOT_KEYS)
                local ext = cleanBySchema(v.extended, HIST_EXTENDED_KEYS)
                local chatLog = SanitizeChatLogForPersist(v.chatLog)
                if snap or ext or chatLog then
                    clean[key] = {
                        snapshot = snap,
                        extended = ext,
                        lastSeenAt = (type(v.lastSeenAt) == "number") and v.lastSeenAt or nil,
                        chatLog = chatLog,
                    }
                end
            end
        end
        PlayerHistory = clean
    end

    loadHistoryData()

    -- Dipanggil setiap kali kita punya snapshot profil terbaru seorang
    -- player (biasanya dari RefreshPlayerList/HookPlayerTracking saat
    -- masih online) -- menimpa snapshot lama di histori dengan yang baru.
    PersistPlayerSnapshot = function(userId, snap)
        if not userId or not snap then return end
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = PlayerHistory[key] or {}
        entry.snapshot = cleanBySchema(snap, HIST_SNAPSHOT_KEYS)
        PlayerHistory[key] = entry
        saveHistoryData()
    end
