    -- Dipanggil tiap kali 1 field "extended" (Bio, Groups, dst) seorang
    -- player selesai di-fetch -- disimpan progresif per-field, JANGAN
    -- nunggu semua field selesai (masing-masing fetch HTTP-nya independen
    -- & butuh waktu beda-beda).
    PersistExtendedField = function(userId, fieldKey, value)
        if not userId or not fieldKey then return end
        if not (type(value) == "string" or type(value) == "number" or type(value) == "boolean") then return end
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = PlayerHistory[key] or {}
        entry.extended = entry.extended or {}
        entry.extended[fieldKey] = value
        PlayerHistory[key] = entry
        saveHistoryData()
    end

    PersistLastSeen = function(userId, ts)
        if not userId then return end
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = PlayerHistory[key] or {}
        entry.lastSeenAt = ts or os.time()
        PlayerHistory[key] = entry
        saveHistoryData()
    end

    -- Dipanggil tiap kali ada pesan chat baru dari player manapun yang
    -- lagi di-track (lihat HookPlayerTracking) -- disimpan permanen biar
    -- histori chat-nya tidak hilang begitu player itu offline/rejoin.
    PersistChatLog = function(userId, chatLog)
        if not userId then return end
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = PlayerHistory[key] or {}
        entry.chatLog = SanitizeChatLogForPersist(chatLog)
        PlayerHistory[key] = entry
        saveHistoryData()
    end

    -- Terapkan histori snapshot/extended yang sudah tersimpan ke cache
    -- SEBELUM ada satupun player online -- ini yang membuat semua player
    -- yang pernah ditemui tetap muncul di list (sebagai OFFLINE) walau
    -- script baru saja di-run ulang / rejoin server.
    local function seenInOfflineOrder(userId)
        for _, uid in ipairs(OfflineOrder) do
            if uid == userId then return true end
        end
        return false
    end
    for key, entry in pairs(PlayerHistory) do
        local userId = tonumber(key)
        if userId then
            local c = EnsureCache(userId)
            if entry.snapshot then
                c.snapshot = entry.snapshot
            end
            c.lastSeenAt = entry.lastSeenAt
            c.online = false
            -- FIX: chat log yang tersimpan ikut dimuat balik di sini juga
            -- -- ini yang bikin tetap muncul walau player-nya offline
            -- ATAU script baru saja di-restart. Avatar 3D-nya sendiri
            -- TIDAK perlu direstore dari sini lagi -- cukup userId (key
            -- di atas), langsung dirender lewat
            -- Players:CreateHumanoidModelFromUserId() di viewport (lihat
            -- UpdateTargetUI), jadi selalu menampilkan avatar TERKINI,
            -- bukan snapshot lama yang bisa basi/gagal direkonstruksi.
            if entry.chatLog then
                c.chatLog = entry.chatLog
            end
            if not seenInOfflineOrder(userId) then
                table.insert(OfflineOrder, userId)
            end
        end
    end

    -- ============================================================
    -- LEADERBOARD PERTEMUAN: top player yang paling sering satu server
    -- sama kamu, dihitung LANGSUNG dari EncounterData (nggak nambah data
    -- baru/request HTTP sama sekali) -- cuma disortir & ditampilkan.
    -- ============================================================
    local RenderMoreLeaderboard = nil
    local leaderboardRefreshPending = false
    RefreshLeaderboardDisplay = function()
        if not Stats.statLeaderboard then return end
        -- Di-defer + di-debounce (leaderboardRefreshPending) supaya scan
        -- awal yang manggil RecordEncounter puluhan kali beruntun nggak
        -- nge-sort ulang leaderboard puluhan kali juga -- cukup 1x per
        -- "batch" perubahan.
        if leaderboardRefreshPending then return end
        leaderboardRefreshPending = true
        task.defer(function()
            leaderboardRefreshPending = false
            local rows = {}
            for key, entry in pairs(EncounterData) do
                if type(entry) == "table" and (entry.count or 0) > 0 then
                    table.insert(rows, {
                        userId = tonumber(key),
                        name = entry.name or ("User " .. key),
                        count = entry.count or 0,
                        lastSeen = entry.lastSeen,
                    })
                end
            end
            table.sort(rows, function(a, b)
                if a.count ~= b.count then return a.count > b.count end
                return (a.lastSeen or 0) > (b.lastSeen or 0)
            end)

            if #rows == 0 then
                Stats.statLeaderboard.Text = "Belum ada data pertemuan yang tercatat"
                if Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn then Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false end
                RenderMoreLeaderboard = nil
                return
            end

            local LB_PAGE_SIZE = 20
            local shown = 0
            local function RenderLeaderboardPage()
                shown = math.min(shown + LB_PAGE_SIZE, #rows)
                local lines = {}
                for i = 1, shown do
                    local r = rows[i]
                    local lastSeenText = "-"
                    if r.lastSeen then
                        local okFmt, text = pcall(function() return os.date("%d %b %Y", r.lastSeen) end)
                        if okFmt then lastSeenText = text end
                    end
                    table.insert(lines, ("#%d %s — %d kali (terakhir %s)"):format(i, r.name, r.count, lastSeenText))
                end
                Stats.statLeaderboard.Text = ("(%d player tercatat, menampilkan %d)\n"):format(#rows, shown)
                    .. table.concat(lines, "\n")
                if Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn then
                    Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn.Visible = shown < #rows
                end
            end
            RenderLeaderboardPage()
            RenderMoreLeaderboard = RenderLeaderboardPage
        end)
    end
    RefreshLeaderboardDisplay()

    local liveStatGen = 0
    local function StopLiveStats()
        liveStatGen = liveStatGen + 1
    end

    local CACHE_TTL = 300
    local REQUEST_GAP = 0.45
    local PlayerDataCache = {}

    local requestQueue = {}
    local queueRunning = false

    local function EnqueueRequest(job)
        table.insert(requestQueue, job)
        if queueRunning then return end
        queueRunning = true
        task.spawn(function()
            while #requestQueue > 0 do
                local job2 = table.remove(requestQueue, 1)
                pcall(job2)
                task.wait(REQUEST_GAP)
            end
            queueRunning = false
        end)
    end

    local function GetCacheEntry(userId)
        local key = tostring(userId)
        local entry = PlayerDataCache[key]
        if not entry then
            entry = {}
            PlayerDataCache[key] = entry
        end
        return entry
    end

    local currentDisplayedUserId = nil

    local RenderMoreMutualFriends = nil

    local activeFriendsMap = {}
    local friendsInServerText = {}

    local FRIENDS_LEFT_MAX = 50

    -- Riwayat "teman yang sudah keluar server" sekarang disimpan
    -- persisten di section "friendsLeft" pada JEYHUB/data.json (pola
    -- sama seperti Encounter Tracker di atas) -- sebelumnya cuma
    -- in-memory (table biasa), jadi hilang total tiap kali script
    -- direset/rejoin, padahal ini data penting yang harus tetap ada.
    local friendsLeftMap = {}
    local friendsLeftText = {}

    local function saveFriendsLeftData()
        local out = {}
        for userId, list in pairs(friendsLeftMap) do
            out[tostring(userId)] = list
        end
        JD_Set("friendsLeft", out)
    end

    local function loadFriendsLeftData()
        local data = JD_Get("friendsLeft", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end
        local clean = {}
        for key, list in pairs(data) do
            local userId = tonumber(key)
            if userId and type(list) == "table" then
                local cleanList = {}
                for _, rec in ipairs(list) do
                    if type(rec) == "table" and type(rec.name) == "string" and type(rec.at) == "number" then
                        table.insert(cleanList, { name = rec.name, at = rec.at })
                    end
                end
                if #cleanList > 0 then clean[userId] = cleanList end
            end
        end
        friendsLeftMap = clean
    end

    loadFriendsLeftData()

    local function RebuildFriendsLeftText(userId)
        local list = friendsLeftMap[userId]
        if list and #list > 0 then
            local parts = {}
            for _, rec in ipairs(list) do
                table.insert(parts, rec.name .. " (pukul " .. os.date("%H:%M:%S", rec.at) .. ")")
            end
            friendsLeftText[userId] = table.concat(parts, ", ")
        else
            friendsLeftText[userId] = "No friends have left the server while monitored"
        end
        if currentDisplayedUserId == userId and Stats.statFriendsLeft then
            pcall(function() Stats.statFriendsLeft.Text = friendsLeftText[userId] end)
        end
    end

    local function RecordFriendLeft(forUserId, leftName)
        local list = friendsLeftMap[forUserId]
        if not list then
            list = {}
            friendsLeftMap[forUserId] = list
        end
        table.insert(list, 1, { name = leftName, at = os.time() })
        while #list > FRIENDS_LEFT_MAX do table.remove(list) end
        saveFriendsLeftData()
        RebuildFriendsLeftText(forUserId)
    end

    for userId in pairs(friendsLeftMap) do RebuildFriendsLeftText(userId) end

    local function RebuildFriendsInServerText(userId)
        local names = {}
        local map = activeFriendsMap[userId]
        if map then
            for otherId, _ in pairs(map) do
                local otherPlr = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(otherId)
                if otherPlr then
                    table.insert(names, (otherPlr.DisplayName or otherPlr.Name) .. " (@" .. otherPlr.Name .. ")")
                end
            end
        end
        if #names > 0 then
            friendsInServerText[userId] = table.concat(names, ", ")
        else
            friendsInServerText[userId] = "No friends currently in this server"
        end

        if currentDisplayedUserId == userId and Stats.statFriendsInServer then
            pcall(function() Stats.statFriendsInServer.Text = friendsInServerText[userId] end)
        end
    end

    local function RebuildMutualFriendsDisplay()
        local uid = currentDisplayedUserId
        if not uid or not Stats.statMutualCount or not statMutualNames then return end
        if uid == (LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.UserId) then
            Stats.statMutualCount.Text = "This is you"
            statMutualNames.Text = "-"
            if statMutualLoadMoreBtn then statMutualLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false end
            return
        end

        local myMap = LocalPlayer and activeFriendsMap[LocalPlayer.UserId]
        local targetMap = activeFriendsMap[uid]
        local mutualPlrs = {}
        if myMap and targetMap then
            for otherId, _ in pairs(myMap) do
                if targetMap[otherId] then
                    local otherPlr = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(otherId)
                    if otherPlr then table.insert(mutualPlrs, otherPlr) end
                end
            end
        end

        Stats.statMutualCount.Text = tostring(#mutualPlrs)
        if #mutualPlrs == 0 then
            statMutualNames.Text = "No mutual friends currently in this server"
            if statMutualLoadMoreBtn then statMutualLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false end
            RenderMoreMutualFriends = nil
            return
        end

        local MUTUAL_PAGE_SIZE = 20
        local shown = 0
        local function RenderMutualPage()
            shown = math.min(shown + MUTUAL_PAGE_SIZE, #mutualPlrs)
            local names = {}
            for i = 1, shown do
                local p = mutualPlrs[i]
                table.insert(names, (p.DisplayName or p.Name) .. " (@" .. p.Name .. ")")
            end
            statMutualNames.Text = ("(%d total, showing %d) "):format(#mutualPlrs, shown)
                .. table.concat(names, ", ")
            if statMutualLoadMoreBtn then statMutualLoadMoreBtn.Visible = shown < #mutualPlrs end
        end
        RenderMutualPage()
        RenderMoreMutualFriends = RenderMutualPage
    end

    local function CheckFriendPair(p1, p2)
        if not (p1 and p2 and p1.Parent and p2.Parent) then return end
        if activeFriendsMap[p1.UserId] and activeFriendsMap[p1.UserId][p2.UserId] then return end
        local ok, isFriend = pcall(function() return p1:IsFriendsWith(p2.UserId) end)
        if ok and isFriend then
            activeFriendsMap[p1.UserId] = activeFriendsMap[p1.UserId] or {}
            activeFriendsMap[p1.UserId][p2.UserId] = true
            activeFriendsMap[p2.UserId] = activeFriendsMap[p2.UserId] or {}
            activeFriendsMap[p2.UserId][p1.UserId] = true
            RebuildFriendsInServerText(p1.UserId)
            RebuildFriendsInServerText(p2.UserId)
            RebuildMutualFriendsDisplay()
        end
    end

    local function ScanAllFriendPairs()
        local plrs = Players:GetPlayers()
        for i = 1, #plrs do
            for j = i + 1, #plrs do
                CheckFriendPair(plrs[i], plrs[j])
                task.wait(0.05)
            end
        end
    end

    SafeConnect(Players.PlayerAdded, function(newPlr)
        RebuildFriendsInServerText(newPlr.UserId)
        task.spawn(function()
            task.wait(1)
            for _, other in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if other ~= newPlr then
                    CheckFriendPair(newPlr, other)
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
            end
        end)
    end)

    SafeConnect(Players.PlayerRemoving, function(leavingPlr)
        local leavingName = leavingPlr.DisplayName and (leavingPlr.DisplayName .. " (@" .. leavingPlr.Name .. ")") or leavingPlr.Name
        activeFriendsMap[leavingPlr.UserId] = nil
        for uid, map in pairs(activeFriendsMap) do
            if map[leavingPlr.UserId] then
                map[leavingPlr.UserId] = nil
                RebuildFriendsInServerText(uid)
                RecordFriendLeft(uid, leavingName)
            end
        end
        RebuildMutualFriendsDisplay()
    end)

    task.spawn(ScanAllFriendPairs)
    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(30)
            if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
            ScanAllFriendPairs()
        end
    end)

    local FAILED_CACHE_TTL = 20
    local function GetOrFetchFriends(userId, callback)
        local entry = GetCacheEntry(userId)
        if entry.friendsAt then
            local age = os.clock() - entry.friendsAt
            local ttl = entry.friends and CACHE_TTL or FAILED_CACHE_TTL
            if age < ttl then
                if callback then pcall(callback, entry.friends, entry.friendsError) end
                return
            end
        end
        if entry.friendsPending then
            if callback then table.insert(entry.friendsWaiters or {}, callback) end
            return
        end
        entry.friendsPending = true
        entry.friendsWaiters = entry.friendsWaiters or {}
        if callback then table.insert(entry.friendsWaiters, callback) end
        EnqueueRequest(function()
            local body, httpErr = SafeHttpGet("https://friends.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/friends")
            local records = nil
            local errText = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    records = {}
                    for _, f in ipairs(data.data) do
                        if type(f) == "table" and f.id then
                            table.insert(records, { id = f.id, name = f.displayName or f.name or tostring(f.id) })
                        end
                    end
                else
                    errText = "Failed to read friend data (unrecognized format)."
                end
            else
                errText = "Failed to fetch friend data: " .. tostring(httpErr or "unknown")
            end
            local e = GetCacheEntry(userId)
            e.friends = records
            e.friendsError = errText
            e.friendsAt = os.clock()
            e.friendsPending = false
            local waiters = e.friendsWaiters or {}
            e.friendsWaiters = {}
            for _, cb in ipairs(waiters) do pcall(cb, records, errText) end
        end)
    end

    local function BackgroundPrefetchPlayer(plr)
        if not plr or plr == LocalPlayer then return end
        local ok, userId = pcall(function() return plr.UserId end)
        if not ok or not userId then return end
        GetOrFetchFriends(userId, nil)
    end

    local function BackgroundScanAllPlayers()
        for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            BackgroundPrefetchPlayer(plr)
        end
    end

    local RenderMoreFriends = nil

    local RenderMoreChatLog = nil

    local RenderMoreAnimLog = nil

    local RenderMoreEncounterHistory = nil

    local profileGen = 0
    local function FetchSocialStats(userId)
        profileGen = profileGen + 1
        local myGen = profileGen
        Stats.statFriendsCount.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statFollowers.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statFollowing.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statGroups.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statPrimaryGroup.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statAllGroups.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statGamesCreated.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statFavoriteGames.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statUsernameHistory.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statBio.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statSocialLinks.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statUgcItems.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statGameBadges.Text = "Loading..."

        -- Tampilkan dulu data histori tersimpan (kalau ada) SEBELUM fetch
        -- HTTP baru selesai -- supaya profil player yang sudah offline
        -- (dari player_history.json) langsung menampilkan data lama secara
        -- instan, bukan cuma "Loading..." selamanya kalau API sudah tidak
        -- bisa diakses untuk user itu. Kalau fetch HTTP di bawah berhasil,
        -- teks ini akan DITIMPA dengan data terbaru seperti biasa.
        do
            local histEntry = PlayerHistory and PlayerHistory[tostring(userId)]
            local ext = histEntry and histEntry.extended
            if ext then
                if ext.friendsCount ~= nil then Stats.statFriendsCount.Text = tostring(ext.friendsCount) end
                if ext.followers ~= nil then Stats.statFollowers.Text = tostring(ext.followers) end
                if ext.following ~= nil then Stats.statFollowing.Text = tostring(ext.following) end
                if ext.groups ~= nil then Stats.statGroups.Text = tostring(ext.groups) end
                if ext.primaryGroup ~= nil then Stats.statPrimaryGroup.Text = tostring(ext.primaryGroup) end
                if ext.allGroups ~= nil then Stats.statAllGroups.Text = tostring(ext.allGroups) end
                if ext.gameGroupRank ~= nil then Stats.statGameGroupRank.Text = tostring(ext.gameGroupRank) end
                if ext.gamesCreated ~= nil then Stats.statGamesCreated.Text = tostring(ext.gamesCreated) end
                if ext.favoriteGames ~= nil then Stats.statFavoriteGames.Text = tostring(ext.favoriteGames) end
                if ext.usernameHistory ~= nil then Stats.statUsernameHistory.Text = tostring(ext.usernameHistory) end
                if ext.bio ~= nil then Stats.statBio.Text = tostring(ext.bio) end
                if ext.socialLinks ~= nil then Stats.statSocialLinks.Text = tostring(ext.socialLinks) end
                if ext.ugcItems ~= nil then Stats.statUgcItems.Text = tostring(ext.ugcItems) end
                if ext.gameBadges ~= nil then Stats.statGameBadges.Text = tostring(ext.gameBadges) end
                if ext.inventory ~= nil then Stats.statInventory.Text = tostring(ext.inventory) end
            end
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            local body = SafeHttpGet("https://users.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId))
            local bioText = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" then
                    if type(data.description) == "string" then
                        bioText = (data.description ~= "") and data.description or "(Kosong, tidak ada bio)"
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statBio.Text = bioText or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(userId, "bio", bioText or "-") end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local body = SafeHttpGet(
                "https://accountinformation.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/promotion-channels"
            )
            local text = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" then
                    local links = {}
                    local CHANNELS = { "facebook", "twitter", "youtube", "twitch", "guilded" }
                    for _, ch in ipairs(CHANNELS) do
                        if type(data[ch]) == "string" and data[ch] ~= "" then
                            table.insert(links, ch:sub(1,1):upper() .. ch:sub(2) .. ": " .. data[ch])
                        end
                    end
                    text = (#links > 0) and table.concat(links, " | ") or "Nothing linked"
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statSocialLinks.Text = text or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(userId, "socialLinks", text or "-") end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local body = SafeHttpGet(
                "https://catalog.roblox.com/v1/search/items?category=1&creatorTargetId="
                    .. tostring(userId) .. "&creatorType=User&limit=30&sortType=3"
            )
            local text = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    local n = #data.data
                    if n == 0 then
                        text = "Not a UGC Creator (no catalog items)"
                    else
                        local names = {}
                        for _, item in ipairs(data.data) do
                            if type(item) == "table" and item.name then table.insert(names, item.name) end
                        end
                        text = ("(%d%s) "):format(n, (#data.data == 30) and "+" or "") .. table.concat(names, ", ")
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statUgcItems.Text = text or "Unknown"
                if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(userId, "ugcItems", text or "Unknown") end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local text = nil
            local okBadges, err = pcall(function()
                local BadgeService = SafeService("BadgeService")
                local universeId = game.GameId
                local pages = BadgeService:GetBadgesInUniverseAsync(universeId)
                local allBadges = {}
                local guard = 0
                while true do
                    guard = guard + 1
                    for _, b in ipairs(pages:GetCurrentPage()) do table.insert(allBadges, b) end
                    if pages.IsFinished or guard > 20 then break end
                    pages:AdvanceToNextPageAsync()
                end
                if #allBadges == 0 then
                    text = "This game has no badges at all"
                    return
                end
                local badgeIds = {}
                for _, b in ipairs(allBadges) do table.insert(badgeIds, b.Id) end
                local owned = BadgeService:CheckUserBadgesAsync(userId, badgeIds)
                local ownedNames = {}
                for i, isOwned in ipairs(owned) do
                    if isOwned then table.insert(ownedNames, allBadges[i].Name) end
                end
                text = (#ownedNames > 0) and table.concat(ownedNames, ", ") or "Belum ada badge game ini yang dimiliki"
            end)
            if not okBadges then
                text = "Not accessible from this environment"
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statGameBadges.Text = text or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(userId, "gameBadges", text or "-") end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local body, httpErr = SafeHttpGet(
                "https://games.roblox.com/v2/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/games?accessFilter=Public&limit=25&sortOrder=Desc"
            )
            local text = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    local n = #data.data
                    local hasMore = data.nextPageCursor ~= nil and data.nextPageCursor ~= ""
                    if n == 0 then
                        text = "No games created/published"
                    else
                        local names = {}
                        for _, g in ipairs(data.data) do
                            if type(g) == "table" and g.name then table.insert(names, g.name) end
                        end
                        text = ("(%d%s) "):format(n, hasMore and "+" or "") .. table.concat(names, ", ")
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                local finalText = text or ("Failed to load: " .. tostring(httpErr or "-"))
                Stats.statGamesCreated.Text = finalText
                if PersistExtendedField and text then PersistExtendedField(userId, "gamesCreated", text) end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local body, httpErr = SafeHttpGet(
                "https://games.roblox.com/v2/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/favorite/games?limit=25&sortOrder=Desc"
            )
            local text = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    local n = #data.data
                    local hasMore = data.nextPageCursor ~= nil and data.nextPageCursor ~= ""
                    if n == 0 then
                        text = "No favorite games (or hidden)"
                    else
                        local names = {}
                        for _, g in ipairs(data.data) do
                            if type(g) == "table" and g.name then table.insert(names, g.name) end
                        end
                        text = ("(%d%s) "):format(n, hasMore and "+" or "") .. table.concat(names, ", ")
                    end
                else
                    text = "Not accessible (likely made private by its owner)"
                end
            else
                text = "Not accessible (likely made private by its owner)"
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statFavoriteGames.Text = text
                if PersistExtendedField and text then PersistExtendedField(userId, "favoriteGames", text) end
            end
        end)

        task.spawn(function()
            local body, httpErr = SafeHttpGet(
                "https://users.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/username-history?limit=50&sortOrder=Desc"
            )
            local text = nil
            if body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    if #data.data == 0 then
                        text = "Never changed username"
                    else
                        local names = {}
                        for _, u in ipairs(data.data) do
                            if type(u) == "table" and u.name then table.insert(names, u.name) end
                        end
                        text = ("(%d) "):format(#names) .. table.concat(names, ", ")
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                local finalText = text or ("Failed to load: " .. tostring(httpErr or "-"))
                Stats.statUsernameHistory.Text = finalText
                if PersistExtendedField and text then PersistExtendedField(userId, "usernameHistory", text) end
            end
        end)

        local function fetchCount(url)
            local okReq, body = pcall(function() return game:HttpGet(url) end)
            if not okReq or not body then return nil end
            local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
            if not okDecode or type(data) ~= "table" then return nil end
            return data.count
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            local n = fetchCount("https://friends.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/friends/count")
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statFriendsCount.Text = n and tostring(n) or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField and n then PersistExtendedField(userId, "friendsCount", n) end
            end
        end)
        task.spawn(function()
            local n = fetchCount("https://friends.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/followers/count")
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statFollowers.Text = n and tostring(n) or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField and n then PersistExtendedField(userId, "followers", n) end
            end
        end)
        task.spawn(function()
            local n = fetchCount("https://friends.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/followings/count")
            if myGen == profileGen then
                Stats.statFollowing.Text = n and tostring(n) or "-"
                if PersistExtendedField and n then PersistExtendedField(userId, "following", n) end
            end
        end)
        task.spawn(function()
            local okReq, body = pcall(function()
                return game:HttpGet("https://groups.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/groups/roles")
            end)
            local groupCount = nil
            local groupNamesText = nil
            local gameGroupRankText = nil

            local okGameGroup, gameCreatorType, gameCreatorId = pcall(function()
                return game.CreatorType, game.CreatorId
            end)
            local isGameGroupOwned = okGameGroup and gameCreatorType == Enum.CreatorType.Group
            if okReq and body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.data) == "table" then
                    groupCount = #data.data
                    if groupCount == 0 then
                        groupNamesText = "Not following any groups"
                    else
                        local names = {}
                        for _, g in ipairs(data.data) do
                            if type(g) == "table" and type(g.group) == "table" and g.group.name then
                                table.insert(names, g.group.name)
                                if isGameGroupOwned and g.group.id == gameCreatorId and type(g.role) == "table" then
                                    gameGroupRankText = (g.role.name or "?") .. " (Rank " .. tostring(g.role.rank or "?") .. ")"
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        groupNamesText = (#names > 0) and table.concat(names, ", ") or "-"
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                local finalGameGroupRank = (not isGameGroupOwned) and "This game isn't owned by a group"
                    or (gameGroupRankText or "Not a member of this game's owner group")
                Stats.statGroups.Text = groupCount and tostring(groupCount) or "-"
                Stats.statAllGroups.Text = groupNamesText or "-"
                Stats.statGameGroupRank.Text = finalGameGroupRank
                if PersistExtendedField then
                    if groupCount then PersistExtendedField(userId, "groups", groupCount) end
                    if groupNamesText then PersistExtendedField(userId, "allGroups", groupNamesText) end
                    PersistExtendedField(userId, "gameGroupRank", finalGameGroupRank)
                end
            end
        end)
        task.spawn(function()
            local okReq, body = pcall(function()
                return game:HttpGet("https://groups.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. tostring(userId) .. "/groups/primary/role")
            end)
            local groupText = nil
            if okReq and body then
                local okDecode, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(body) end)
                if okDecode and type(data) == "table" and type(data.group) == "table" then
                    local groupName = data.group.name or "?"
                    if type(data.role) == "table" then
                        groupText = groupName .. " — " .. (data.role.name or "?") .. " (Rank " .. tostring(data.role.rank or "?") .. ")"
                    else
                        groupText = groupName
                    end
                end
            end
            if myGen == profileGen then
                local finalText = groupText or "None"
                Stats.statPrimaryGroup.Text = finalText
                if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(userId, "primaryGroup", finalText) end
            end
        end)

        currentDisplayedUserId = userId

        statAllFriends.Text = "Loading..."
        statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
        GetOrFetchFriends(userId, function(records, errText)
            if myGen ~= profileGen then return end
            if not records then
                statAllFriends.Text = errText or "Failed to load friend data."
                statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
                return
            end
            if #records == 0 then
                statAllFriends.Text = "No friends"
                statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
                return
            end

            local FRIENDS_PAGE_SIZE = 20
            local shown = 0
            local function RenderFriendsPage()
                shown = math.min(shown + FRIENDS_PAGE_SIZE, #records)
                local names = {}
                for i = 1, shown do table.insert(names, records[i].name) end
                statAllFriends.Text = ("(%d total, showing %d) "):format(#records, shown)
                    .. table.concat(names, ", ")
                statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn.Visible = shown < #records
            end
            RenderFriendsPage()
            RenderMoreFriends = RenderFriendsPage
        end)

        Stats.statFriendsInServer.Text = friendsInServerText[userId] or "No friends currently in this server"
        Stats.statFriendsLeft.Text = friendsLeftText[userId] or "No friends have left the server while monitored"

        RebuildMutualFriendsDisplay()

        if LocalPlayer and userId == LocalPlayer.UserId then
            Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = "This is you"
        else
            Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = "Loading..."
            GetOrFetchFriends(userId, function(targetFriends, targetErr)
                if myGen ~= profileGen then return end
                if not targetFriends then
                    Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = targetErr or "Failed to load."
                    return
                end
                if not LocalPlayer then Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = "-"; return end
                GetOrFetchFriends(LocalPlayer.UserId, function(myFriends, myErr)
                    if myGen ~= profileGen then return end
                    if not myFriends then
                        Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = myErr or "Failed to load your friends list."
                        return
                    end
                    local myFriendSet = {}
                    for _, f in ipairs(myFriends) do myFriendSet[f.id] = true end
                    local count = 0
                    for _, f in ipairs(targetFriends) do
                        if myFriendSet[f.id] then count = count + 1 end
                    end
                    Stats.statMutualGlobal.Text = tostring(count)
                end)
            end)
        end
    end


    local function FetchAvatarStats(userId)
        local myGen = profileGen
        Stats.statEquippedEmotes.Text = "Loading..."
        Stats.statBodyParts.Text = "Loading..."

        do
            local histEntry = PlayerHistory and PlayerHistory[tostring(userId)]
            local ext = histEntry and histEntry.extended
            if ext then
                if ext.bodyParts ~= nil then Stats.statBodyParts.Text = tostring(ext.bodyParts) end
                if ext.equippedEmotes ~= nil then Stats.statEquippedEmotes.Text = tostring(ext.equippedEmotes) end
            end
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            local okDesc, desc = pcall(function()
                return Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(userId)
            end)
            if myGen ~= profileGen then return end
            if okDesc and desc then
                local okParts, partsText = pcall(function()
                    local PART_ORDER = {
                        { key = "Head", label = "Head" },
                        { key = "Torso", label = "Torso" },
                        { key = "LeftArm", label = "Left Arm" },
                        { key = "RightArm", label = "Right Arm" },
                        { key = "LeftLeg", label = "Left Leg" },
                        { key = "RightLeg", label = "Right Leg" },
                    }
                    local lines = {}
                    for _, part in ipairs(PART_ORDER) do
                        local assetId = desc[part.key]
                        if type(assetId) == "number" and assetId > 0 then
                            local name = GetAssetName(assetId)
                            table.insert(lines, string.format(
                                "%s: %s (ID: %d)", part.label, name or "Unknown Asset", assetId
                            ))
                        else
                            table.insert(lines, string.format("%s: Default (Roblox)", part.label))
                        end
                    end
                    return table.concat(lines, "\n")
                end)
                if myGen == profileGen then
                    local finalParts = (okParts and partsText) or "-"
                    Stats.statBodyParts.Text = finalParts
                    if PersistExtendedField and okParts then PersistExtendedField(userId, "bodyParts", finalParts) end
                end

                local okEmote, emoteText = pcall(function()
                    local raw = desc.EmotesData
                    if not raw or raw == "" then return "No emote equipped" end
                    local okJson, parsed = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(raw) end)
                    if not okJson or type(parsed) ~= "table" then return "No emote equipped" end
                    local names = {}
                    for _, entry in pairs(parsed) do
                        if type(entry) == "table" and entry.Name then
                            table.insert(names, entry.Name)
                        end
                    end
                    if #names == 0 then return "No emote equipped" end
                    return table.concat(names, ", ")
                end)
                local finalEmote = (okEmote and emoteText) or "-"
                Stats.statEquippedEmotes.Text = finalEmote
                if PersistExtendedField and okEmote then PersistExtendedField(userId, "equippedEmotes", finalEmote) end
            else
                Stats.statEquippedEmotes.Text = "-"
                Stats.statBodyParts.Text = "-"
            end
        end)
    end

    local function FormatChatLogText(cache, shownCount)
        local log = (cache and cache.chatLog) or {}
        if #log == 0 then
            return "No messages monitored yet", false, 0
        end
        local shown = math.min(shownCount, #log)
        local parts = {}
        for i = 1, shown do
            local rec = log[i]
            table.insert(parts, os.date("%H:%M:%S", rec.at) .. "  " .. rec.text)
        end
        local text = ("(%d total, showing %d, newest first)\n"):format(#log, shown) .. table.concat(parts, "\n")
        return text, shown < #log, shown
    end

    local function FormatAnimLogText(cache, shownCount)
        local log = (cache and cache.animLog) or {}
        if #log == 0 then
            return "No animation/emote detected yet", false, 0
        end
        local shown = math.min(shownCount, #log)
        local parts = {}
        for i = 1, shown do
            local rec = log[i]
            local status = rec.original and "Original" or "SCRIPT/INJECTED"
            table.insert(parts, string.format(
                "%s  [%s] %s -- ID: %d (%s)",
                os.date("%H:%M:%S", rec.at), rec.trackName, status, rec.id, rec.name
            ))
        end
        local text = ("(%d total, showing %d, newest first)\n"):format(#log, shown) .. table.concat(parts, "\n")
        return text, shown < #log, shown
    end

    -- Label 3D "LASER" yang muncul MENGAMBANG DI ATAS KEPALA target di
    -- dunia game (BillboardGui, bukan cuma di kartu info) -- gaya visual
    -- disamain sama identitas JEYHUB: kartu glass gelap, border tipis
    -- warna accent, tick-bar ungu kecil di kiri (pola yang sama dipakai
    -- di header section & pill komponen lain), font tebal & clean.
    -- Di-attach LANGSUNG ke part Head (bukan CoreGui/PlayerGui terpisah)
    -- supaya otomatis ikut hilang kalau karakter respawn/dihancurkan --
    -- nggak perlu logic cleanup manual tambahan.
    local function StartLiveStats(target)
        liveStatGen = liveStatGen + 1
        local myGen = liveStatGen
        local liveUserId = target and target.UserId
        local chatLogShown = 20
        local function RenderChatLogPage()
            local cache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
            local text, hasMore = FormatChatLogText(cache, chatLogShown)
            statChatLog.Text = text
            statChatLogLoadMoreBtn.Visible = hasMore
        end
        RenderMoreChatLog = function()
            chatLogShown = chatLogShown + 20
            RenderChatLogPage()
        end

        local animLogShown = 20
        local function RenderAnimLogPage()
            local cache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
            local text, hasMore = FormatAnimLogText(cache, animLogShown)
            statAnimLog.Text = text
            statAnimLogLoadMoreBtn.Visible = hasMore
        end
        RenderMoreAnimLog = function()
            animLogShown = animLogShown + 20
            RenderAnimLogPage()
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            while myGen == liveStatGen do
                local okLoop = pcall(function()
                    if not (target and target.Parent) then return end

                    local hum = target.Character and target.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                    pcall(function()
                        local animator = hum and hum:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
                        if not animator then
                            Stats.statAnimNow.Text = "No character/Animator"
                            return
                        end
                        local okTracks, tracks = pcall(function() return animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks() end)
                        if not okTracks or not tracks or #tracks == 0 then
                            Stats.statAnimNow.Text = "No animation playing right now"
                            return
                        end
                        local cacheForOfficial = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                        local lines = {}
                        for _, track in ipairs(tracks) do
                            local id = track.Animation and ExtractAnimId(track.Animation.AnimationId)
                            if id then
                                local name = GetAssetName(id) or "Unknown Asset"
                                local isOriginal = cacheForOfficial.officialAnimIds and cacheForOfficial.officialAnimIds[id] == true
                                local status = isOriginal and "Original" or "SCRIPT/INJECTED"
                                table.insert(lines, string.format(
                                    "[%s] %s -- ID: %d (%s)",
                                    (track.Name ~= "" and track.Name) or "Animation", status, id, name
                                ))
                            end
                        end
                        Stats.statAnimNow.Text = (#lines > 0) and table.concat(lines, "\n") or "No animation playing right now"
                    end)
                    pcall(RenderAnimLogPage)

                    local okSess, sessText = pcall(function()
                        local cache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                        local elapsed = math.floor(tick() - (cache.firstSeenTick or tick()))
                        local h = math.floor(elapsed / 3600)
                        local m = math.floor((elapsed % 3600) / 60)
                        local s = elapsed % 60
                        if h > 0 then
                            return string.format("%d:%02d:%02d", h, m, s)
                        end
                        return string.format("%02d:%02d", m, s)
                    end)
                    Stats.statSessionTime.Text = (okSess and sessText) or "-"

                    pcall(function()
                        local chatCache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                        Stats.statLastChat.Text = chatCache.lastChatMsg or "No messages monitored yet"
                        Stats.statChatCount.Text = tostring(chatCache.chatCount or 0)
                        Stats.statRespawnCount.Text = tostring(chatCache.respawnCount or 0)
                    end)
                    pcall(RenderChatLogPage)

                    local okLeader, leaderText = pcall(function()
                        local ls = target:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        if not ls then return nil end
                        local parts = {}
                        for _, stat in ipairs(ls:GetChildren()) do
                            if stat:IsA("ValueBase") then
                                table.insert(parts, stat.Name .. ": " .. tostring(stat.Value))
                            end
                        end
                        return (#parts > 0) and table.concat(parts, "  •  ") or nil
                    end)
                    Stats.statLeaderstats.Text = (okLeader and leaderText) or "This game has no leaderstats"

                    if hum then
                        local hp, maxHp = hum.Health, hum.MaxHealth
                        if maxHp and maxHp > 0 then
                            local pct = math.clamp(hp / maxHp, 0, 1)
                            hpValueLbl.Text = string.format("%d / %d", math.floor(hp + 0.5), math.floor(maxHp))
                            Tween(hpFill, 0.25, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0) })
                            local barColor = pct > 0.6 and Color3.fromRGB(90, 220, 130)
                                or (pct > 0.3 and Color3.fromRGB(240, 200, 80) or Color3.fromRGB(230, 90, 90))
                            Tween(hpFill, 0.25, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = barColor })
                        end
                        Stats.statWalkSpeed.Text = tostring(math.floor(hum.WalkSpeed))
                        local jp = hum.UseJumpPower and hum.JumpPower or hum.JumpHeight
                        Stats.statJumpPower.Text = tostring(math.floor(jp * 10) / 10)

                        local okNearest, nearestText = pcall(function()
                            local myRoot2 = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not myRoot2 then return nil end
                            local bestName, bestDist = nil, math.huge
                            for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                                if p ~= target then
                                    local oc = p.Character
                                    local orp = oc and oc:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if orp then
                                        local d = (myRoot2.Position - orp.Position).Magnitude
                                        if d < bestDist then bestDist, bestName = d, p.Name end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            if not bestName then return nil end
                            return string.format("%s (%d studs)", bestName, math.floor(bestDist))
                        end)
                        Stats.statNearestPlayer.Text = (okNearest and nearestText) or "No other players nearby"

                        local okAnomaly, anomalyFlags = pcall(function()
                            local flags = {}
                            local liveCache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                            local root = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local now = tick()

                            -- Threshold ABSOLUT: dianggap "indikasi" cuma
                            -- kalau nilainya di atas 50 -- bukan lagi
                            -- dibandingkan seberapa jauh dari default
                            -- (sebelumnya: WalkSpeed dianggap aneh kalau
                            -- beda >4 dari 16, JumpPower kalau beda >50%
                            -- dari default). Sekarang murni: >50 = flag.
                            if hum.WalkSpeed > 50 then
                                table.insert(flags, string.format("Speed Hack (WalkSpeed %.0f, di atas 50)", hum.WalkSpeed))
                            end

                            local jpVal = hum.UseJumpPower and hum.JumpPower or hum.JumpHeight
                            if jpVal > 50 then
                                table.insert(flags, string.format("Jump Power Hack (%.1f, di atas 50)", jpVal))
                            end

                            if math.abs(hum.MaxHealth - 100) > 0.5 then
                                table.insert(flags, string.format("Stat Dimodifikasi (MaxHealth %.0f, default 100)", hum.MaxHealth))
                            end

                            -- Status "Laser" -- SUDAH dideteksi secara
                            -- event-driven & sticky untuk SEMUA player di
                            -- HookCharacterAnimations (lihat di atas), jadi
                            -- di sini cuma BACA hasilnya, bukan recompute
                            -- ulang. Kalau dihitung ulang tiap tick di sini
                            -- (cuma dari animasi yang PAS SEDANG jalan detik
                            -- ini), status sticky-nya bisa ketimpa balik ke
                            -- false pas animasinya nggak lagi diputar
                            -- persis di tick itu (mis. lagi respawn).
                            if liveCache.isUsingLaser then
                                table.insert(flags, "Laser (Animation ID 70883871260184 pernah/sedang terdeteksi)")
                            end

                            if root then
                                if liveCache.cheatPos and liveCache.cheatTick then
                                    local dt = now - liveCache.cheatTick
                                    if dt > 0.05 and dt < 2 then
                                        local dist = (root.Position - liveCache.cheatPos).Magnitude
                                        local maxPossible = math.max(hum.WalkSpeed, 16) * dt * 3 + 20
                                        if dist > maxPossible then
                                            liveCache.cheatTeleportHits = (liveCache.cheatTeleportHits or 0) + 1
                                        else
                                            liveCache.cheatTeleportHits = math.max(0, (liveCache.cheatTeleportHits or 0) - 1)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                                liveCache.cheatPos = root.Position
                                liveCache.cheatTick = now
                                if (liveCache.cheatTeleportHits or 0) >= 3 then
                                    table.insert(flags, "Teleport (berpindah tempat berulang secara tidak wajar)")
                                end

                                local okState, stateType = pcall(function() return hum:GetState() end)
                                local yVel = root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Y
                                if okState and stateType == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall and math.abs(yVel) < 2 then
                                    liveCache.cheatFlyTicks = (liveCache.cheatFlyTicks or 0) + 1
                                else
                                    liveCache.cheatFlyTicks = 0
                                end
                                if liveCache.cheatFlyTicks >= 3 then
                                    table.insert(flags, "Fly Hack (melayang tanpa jatuh)")
                                end

                                local look = root.CFrame.LookVector
                                if liveCache.cheatLookVec and liveCache.cheatTick then
                                    local dot = math.clamp(liveCache.cheatLookVec:Dot(look), -1, 1)
                                    local angleDeg = math.deg(math.acos(dot))
                                    if angleDeg > 120 then
                                        liveCache.cheatSpinHits = (liveCache.cheatSpinHits or 0) + 1
                                    else
                                        liveCache.cheatSpinHits = math.max(0, (liveCache.cheatSpinHits or 0) - 1)
                                    end
                                end
                                liveCache.cheatLookVec = look
                                if (liveCache.cheatSpinHits or 0) >= 4 then
                                    table.insert(flags, "Spinbot (rotasi tidak wajar)")
                                end

                                local totalParts, noCollideParts = 0, 0
                                for _, child in ipairs(target.Character:GetChildren()) do
                                    if child:IsA("BasePart") then
                                        totalParts = totalParts + 1
                                        if not child.CanCollide then noCollideParts = noCollideParts + 1 end
                                    end
                                end
                                if totalParts > 0 and noCollideParts == totalParts then
                                    table.insert(flags, "Noclip (semua part non-collide)")
                                end
                            end

                            return flags
                        end)
                        local flags = (okAnomaly and anomalyFlags) or {}
                        if #flags == 0 then
                            Stats.statStatAnomaly.Text = "Normal (tidak ada indikasi)"
                            cheaterChip.Visible = false
                        else
                            Stats.statStatAnomaly.Text = table.concat(flags, "; ")
                            cheaterChip.Visible = true
                            cheaterChipLabel.Text = "CHEATER"
                        end
                        -- Chip LASER terpisah dari CHEATER -- biar kelihatan
                        -- spesifik jenis deteksinya di badge row.
                        local isUsingLaserNow = (EnsureCache(liveUserId).isUsingLaser == true)
                        laserChip.Visible = isUsingLaserNow

                        local tool = target.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                        Stats.statTool.Text = tool and tool.Name or "None"

                        local invList = ""
                        if target:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
                            local tools = target.Backpack:GetChildren()
                            local toolNames = {}
                            for _, t in ipairs(tools) do table.insert(toolNames, t.Name) end
                            invList = table.concat(toolNames, ", ")
                        end
                        local invText = (invList == "") and "Kosong" or invList
                        Stats.statInventory.Text = invText
                        -- Simpan snapshot terakhir isi Backpack ke JSON --
                        -- supaya "barang yang dia bawa terakhir sebelum
                        -- keluar" tetap kelihatan walau player sudah
                        -- offline/script direstart (sebelumnya cuma
                        -- bertahan di memori selama sesi berjalan).
                        if PersistExtendedField then PersistExtendedField(liveUserId, "inventory", invText) end

                        local targetRoot = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local okDist, distText = pcall(function()
                            local myRoot = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
                                and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if myRoot and targetRoot then
                                local d = (myRoot.Position - targetRoot.Position).Magnitude
                                return string.format("%d studs", math.floor(d))
                            end
                            return nil
                        end)
                        Stats.statDistance.Text = (okDist and distText) or "-"

                        local okPos, posText = pcall(function()
                            if targetRoot then
                                local p = targetRoot.Position
                                return string.format("%d, %d, %d", math.floor(p.X), math.floor(p.Y), math.floor(p.Z))
                            end
                            return nil
                        end)
                        Stats.statPosition.Text = (okPos and posText) or "-"

                        local okAfk, afkText = pcall(function()
                            local cache = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                            local now = tick()
                            if targetRoot then
                                local p = targetRoot.Position
                                if cache.lastPos and (p - cache.lastPos).Magnitude > 2 then
                                    cache.lastMoveTick = now
                                end
                                cache.lastPos = p
                            end
                            local idleFor = math.floor(now - (cache.lastMoveTick or now))
                            if idleFor <= 8 then return "Active" end
                            local durText
                            if idleFor >= 60 then
                                durText = string.format("%dm %ds", math.floor(idleFor / 60), idleFor % 60)
                            else
                                durText = idleFor .. "s"
                            end
                            return "Likely AFK (idle for " .. durText .. ")"
                        end)
                        Stats.statAfk.Text = (okAfk and afkText) or "-"
                    else
                        hpValueLbl.Text = "- / -"
                        Tween(hpFill, 0.25, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0) })
                        Stats.statWalkSpeed.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statJumpPower.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statStatAnomaly.Text = "-"
                        cheaterChip.Visible = false
                        -- Laser bersifat sticky -- JANGAN dipaksa false di
                        -- sini (karakter lagi respawn/nggak ada humanoid),
                        -- baca status terakhir dari cache biar tetap
                        -- kelihatan flag-nya walau lagi di antara respawn.
                        laserChip.Visible = (EnsureCache(liveUserId).isUsingLaser == true)
                        Stats.statTool.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statInventory.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statDistance.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statPosition.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statAfk.Text = "-"
                        Stats.statNearestPlayer.Text = "-"
                    end

                    if liveUserId then
                        local c = EnsureCache(liveUserId)
                        c.statsText.hp = hpValueLbl.Text
                        c.statsText.hpFillSize = hpFill.Size
                        c.statsText.hpFillColor = hpFill.BackgroundColor3
                        c.statsText.walkSpeed = Stats.statWalkSpeed.Text
                        c.statsText.jumpPower = Stats.statJumpPower.Text
                        c.statsText.tool = Stats.statTool.Text
                        c.statsText.distance = Stats.statDistance.Text
                        c.statsText.position = Stats.statPosition.Text
                        c.statsText.inventory = Stats.statInventory.Text
                        c.statsText.leaderstats = Stats.statLeaderstats.Text
                        c.statsText.afk = Stats.statAfk.Text
                        c.statsText.respawnCount = Stats.statRespawnCount.Text
                        c.statsText.statAnomaly = Stats.statStatAnomaly.Text
                        c.statsText.nearestPlayer = Stats.statNearestPlayer.Text

                        if target.Character then
                            local wasArchivable = target.Character.Archivable
                            local okClone, freshClone = pcall(function()
                                target.Character.Archivable = true
                                return target.Character:Clone()
                            end)
                            pcall(function() target.Character.Archivable = wasArchivable end)
                            if okClone and freshClone then
                                if c.clonedChar then pcall(function() c.clonedChar:Destroy() end) end
                                SanitizeClonedCharacter(freshClone)
                                c.clonedChar = freshClone
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                if not okLoop then

                    warn("[JEYHUB] Live stats tick failed (skipped, loop continues).")
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end

    local function SetInfoCardEmpty(isEmpty)
        emptyStateLbl.Visible = isEmpty
        for _, f in ipairs(statToggleFrames) do
            pcall(function() f.Visible = not isEmpty end)
        end
        if isEmpty then StopLiveStats() end

        task.defer(function()
            pcall(function() infoCard.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, 0) end)
            SyncInfoCardCanvas()
        end)
    end

    local function ApplyCachedStatsToUI(cache)
        cache = cache or {}
        local statsText = cache.statsText or DefaultStatsText()
        hpValueLbl.Text = statsText.hp
        hpFill.Size = statsText.hpFillSize or UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
        if statsText.hpFillColor then hpFill.BackgroundColor3 = statsText.hpFillColor end
        Stats.statWalkSpeed.Text = statsText.walkSpeed
        Stats.statJumpPower.Text = statsText.jumpPower
        Stats.statTool.Text = statsText.tool
        Stats.statDistance.Text = "- (offline)"
        Stats.statPosition.Text = statsText.position
        Stats.statInventory.Text = statsText.inventory
        Stats.statLeaderstats.Text = statsText.leaderstats
        Stats.statAfk.Text = statsText.afk or "-"
        Stats.statSessionTime.Text = "- (offline)"
        Stats.statStatAnomaly.Text = "- (offline)"
        cheaterChip.Visible = false
        laserChip.Visible = (cache.isUsingLaser == true)
        Stats.statNearestPlayer.Text = statsText.nearestPlayer or "-"

        Stats.statRespawnCount.Text = tostring(cache.respawnCount or 0)
        Stats.statLastChat.Text = cache.lastChatMsg or "No messages monitored yet"
        Stats.statChatCount.Text = tostring(cache.chatCount or 0)

        local ghostChatShown = 20
        local function RenderGhostChatLog()
            local text, hasMore = FormatChatLogText(cache, ghostChatShown)
            statChatLog.Text = text
            statChatLogLoadMoreBtn.Visible = hasMore
        end
        RenderGhostChatLog()
        RenderMoreChatLog = function()
            ghostChatShown = ghostChatShown + 20
            RenderGhostChatLog()
        end

        Stats.statAnimNow.Text = "- (offline, showing last detected log below)"
        local ghostAnimShown = 20
        local function RenderGhostAnimLog()
            local text, hasMore = FormatAnimLogText(cache, ghostAnimShown)
            statAnimLog.Text = text
            statAnimLogLoadMoreBtn.Visible = hasMore
        end
        RenderGhostAnimLog()
        RenderMoreAnimLog = function()
            ghostAnimShown = ghostAnimShown + 20
            RenderGhostAnimLog()
        end
    end

    local function UpdateTargetUI()
        if #TargetPlayers == 0 then
            searchBox.Text = ""
            searchBox.PlaceholderText = "No other players"
            profileGen = profileGen + 1
            SetInfoCardEmpty(true)
            if clonedTargetChar then
                pcall(function() clonedTargetChar:Destroy() end)
                clonedTargetChar = nil
            end
            return
        end

        local userId = TargetPlayers[CurrentTargetIndex]
        if not userId then return end
        local cache = EnsureCache(userId)
        local snap = cache.snapshot or { userId = userId, name = "Unknown", displayName = "Unknown" }
        local livePlayer = cache.online and Players:GetPlayerByUserId(userId) or nil
        if cache.online and not livePlayer then cache.online = false end

        SetInfoCardEmpty(false)

        -- FIX: leaderboard pertemuan cuma ditampilkan kalau kartu yang
        -- lagi dibuka itu kartu kamu SENDIRI, bukan player lain --
        -- ditaruh SETELAH SetInfoCardEmpty(false) di atas karena fungsi
        -- itu nyalain Visible = true buat SEMUA statToggleFrames
        -- (termasuk leaderboard), jadi override-nya harus di sini.
        local isViewingSelf = LocalPlayer and (userId == LocalPlayer.UserId)
        leaderboardHeading.Visible = isViewingSelf
        leaderboardRowFrame.Visible = isViewingSelf

        searchBox.Text = snap.displayName or snap.name

        pcall(function()
            headshot.Image = "rbxthumb://type=AvatarHeadShot&id=" .. tostring(userId) .. "&w=150&h=150"
        end)
        displayNameLbl.Text = snap.displayName or snap.name or "Unknown"
        usernameLbl.Text = "@" .. tostring(snap.name or "?")

        onlineChip.Visible = true
        if cache.online then
            onlineChipLabel.Text = "ONLINE"
            onlineChip.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 200, 120)
        else
            onlineChipLabel.Text = "OFFLINE"
            onlineChip.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 150)
        end

        premiumChip.Visible = snap.isPremium == true
        verifiedChip.Visible = snap.hasVerifiedBadge == true
        cheaterChip.Visible = false
        laserChip.Visible = (cache.isUsingLaser == true)

        if cache.online then
            Stats.statLastSeen.Text = "Currently online"
        elseif cache.lastSeenAt then
            local okDate, dateText = pcall(function()
                return os.date("%d %b %Y, %H:%M", cache.lastSeenAt)
            end)
            local agoSeconds = math.max(0, os.time() - cache.lastSeenAt)
            local agoText
            if agoSeconds < 60 then
                agoText = "just now"
            elseif agoSeconds < 3600 then
                agoText = math.floor(agoSeconds / 60) .. " minutes ago"
            elseif agoSeconds < 86400 then
                agoText = math.floor(agoSeconds / 3600) .. " hours ago"
            else
                agoText = math.floor(agoSeconds / 86400) .. " days ago"
            end
            Stats.statLastSeen.Text = (okDate and dateText or "-") .. " (" .. agoText .. ")"
        else
            Stats.statLastSeen.Text = "-"
        end

        statUserId.Text = tostring(userId)
        Stats.statAccAge.Text = tostring(snap.accountAge or "-") .. " Hari"
        local okCreated, createdText = pcall(function()
            return os.date("%d %b %Y", os.time() - ((snap.accountAge or 0) * 86400))
        end)
        Stats.statAccCreated.Text = (snap.accountAge and okCreated) and createdText or "-"

        Stats.statVerifiedBadge.Text = snap.hasVerifiedBadge and "Ya ✅" or "No"

        local teamText = snap.teamName or "None"
        Stats.statTeam.Text = snap.teamColorHex and (teamText .. " (" .. snap.teamColorHex .. ")") or teamText

        Stats.statMembership.Text = (snap.membershipName and snap.membershipName ~= "None") and snap.membershipName or "Reguler"
        Stats.statFriend.Text = snap.isFriend and "Berteman" or "Not Friends Yet"

        do
            local info = GetEncounterInfo(userId)
            local n = info.count
            if userId == (LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.UserId) then
                Stats.statEncounterCount.Text = "This is you"
                Stats.statFirstMet.Text = "-"
                Stats.statLastMet.Text = "-"
                Stats.statEncounterHistory.Text = "-"
                Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
                RenderMoreEncounterHistory = nil
            elseif n <= 0 then
                Stats.statEncounterCount.Text = "First time"
                Stats.statFirstMet.Text = "Baru sekarang"
                Stats.statLastMet.Text = "Baru sekarang"
                Stats.statEncounterHistory.Text = "Belum ada riwayat (baru pertama kali ketemu)"
                Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
                RenderMoreEncounterHistory = nil
            else
                Stats.statEncounterCount.Text = (n == 1) and "1 kali" or (tostring(n) .. " times")

                local function fmtDateTime(ts)
                    local okFmt, text = pcall(function() return os.date("%d %b %Y, %H:%M", ts) end)
                    return okFmt and text or "-"
                end
                Stats.statFirstMet.Text = info.firstSeen and fmtDateTime(info.firstSeen) or "-"
                Stats.statLastMet.Text = info.lastSeen and fmtDateTime(info.lastSeen) or "-"

                local history = info.history or {}
                if #history == 0 then
                    -- Player ini sempat tercatat SEBELUM fitur riwayat detail
                    -- ini ada -- count-nya tetap akurat, cuma log tanggal per
                    -- pertemuannya belum kesimpan dari dulu.
                    Stats.statEncounterHistory.Text = "Riwayat detail belum tersedia (tercatat sebelum fitur ini ada)"
                    Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn.Visible = false
                    RenderMoreEncounterHistory = nil
                else
                    local HISTORY_PAGE_SIZE = 20
                    local shown = 0
                    local function RenderHistoryPage()
                        shown = math.min(shown + HISTORY_PAGE_SIZE, #history)
                        local lines = {}
                        for i = 1, shown do
                            table.insert(lines, (i .. ". " .. fmtDateTime(history[i])))
                        end
                        local suffix = (#history < n) and (" — riwayat lama sebelum " .. #history .. " terakhir tidak tersimpan") or ""
                        Stats.statEncounterHistory.Text = ("(%d tercatat, menampilkan %d)%s\n"):format(#history, shown, suffix)
                            .. table.concat(lines, "\n")
                        Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn.Visible = shown < #history
                    end
                    RenderHistoryPage()
                    RenderMoreEncounterHistory = RenderHistoryPage
                end
            end
        end

        -- Muat catatan pribadi player ini ke textbox (cuma reload kalau
        -- textbox-nya lagi TIDAK sedang difokus/diketik user -- supaya
        -- kalau UpdateTargetUI kebetulan kepanggil lagi selagi kamu
        -- lagi ngetik catatan untuk target yang SAMA, teksmu nggak
        -- ketimpa).
        if Stats.statNoteBox then
            local isFocused = false
            pcall(function() isFocused = (UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() == Stats.statNoteBox) end)
            if not isFocused then
                local noteText, updatedAt = GetPlayerNote(userId)
                Stats.statNoteBox.Text = noteText
                if updatedAt then
                    local okFmt, text = pcall(function() return os.date("%d %b %Y, %H:%M", updatedAt) end)
                    Stats.statNoteSavedAt.Text = "Terakhir diedit: " .. (okFmt and text or "-")
                else
                    Stats.statNoteSavedAt.Text = "Belum ada catatan"
                end
            end
        end

        FetchSocialStats(userId)
        FetchAvatarStats(userId)

        if clonedTargetChar then
            pcall(function() clonedTargetChar:Destroy() end)
            clonedTargetChar = nil
        end
        if targetRotationConnection then
            pcall(function() targetRotationConnection:Disconnect() end)
            targetRotationConnection = nil
        end
        targetWorldModel:ClearAllChildren()

        if cache.online and livePlayer then

            StartLiveStats(livePlayer)

            local char = livePlayer.Character
            if char then
                local wasArchivable = char.Archivable
                char.Archivable = true
                local ok, clone = pcall(function() return char:Clone() end)
                char.Archivable = wasArchivable

                if ok and clone then
                    clonedTargetChar = clone
                    SanitizeClonedCharacter(clonedTargetChar)
                    clonedTargetChar.Parent = targetWorldModel
                end
            end
        else

            StopLiveStats()
            ApplyCachedStatsToUI(cache)

            if cache.clonedChar then
                -- Prioritas 1: clone Instance langsung dari sesi ini
                -- (masih ada di memori) -- paling akurat, pose persis
                -- terakhir kelihatan.
                local okGhost, ghostClone = pcall(function() return cache.clonedChar:Clone() end)
                if okGhost and ghostClone then
                    clonedTargetChar = ghostClone
                    clonedTargetChar.Parent = targetWorldModel
                end
            else
                -- Prioritas 2: player offline & belum ada clone di memori
                -- (baru pertama kali dibuka sesi ini, atau script baru
                -- di-restart) -- render LANGSUNG dari userId lewat
                -- Players:CreateHumanoidModelFromUserId(), teknik yang
                -- sama persis dipakai JEYHUB versi lama di tab Credits.
                -- Ini jauh lebih simpel & tidak gampang bug dibanding
                -- merekonstruksi dari HumanoidDescription yang disimpan
                -- manual (field yang gampang miss/salah format) -- userId
                -- SAJA sudah cukup, dan avatarnya selalu yang TERKINI
                -- (bukan snapshot lama yang bisa basi).
                local okModel, model = pcall(function()
                    return Players:CreateHumanoidModelFromUserId(userId)
                end)
                if okModel and model then
                    SanitizeClonedCharacter(model)
                    clonedTargetChar = model
                    clonedTargetChar.Parent = targetWorldModel
                    -- Simpan juga sebagai clonedChar sesi ini, biar kalau
                    -- dibuka lagi berkali-kali di sesi yang sama tidak
                    -- perlu fetch ulang ke Roblox tiap kali.
                    local okCacheClone, cacheClone = pcall(function() return model:Clone() end)
                    if okCacheClone then cache.clonedChar = cacheClone end
                end
            end
        end

        if clonedTargetChar and targetCamera then
            if cache.online then
                -- Player LIVE: tetap pakai kamera dinamis (jarak ngikutin
                -- tinggi avatar sebenarnya) -- avatar live bisa punya
                -- body scale ekstrem, jadi jarak fixed kurang cocok di
                -- sini, dan sistem ini memang belum pernah dilaporkan
                -- bug untuk kasus live.
                local camDistance = CAM_DISTANCE
                local okSize0, _, size0 = pcall(function() return clonedTargetChar:GetBoundingBox() end)
                if okSize0 and size0 and size0.Y > 0 then
                    camDistance = math.clamp(size0.Y * 1.35, 3.2, CAM_DISTANCE)
                end
                ComputeAvatarCameraCFrame(clonedTargetChar, targetCamera, { Distance = camDistance, VerticalBias = 0.55, TiltUp = 0.12 })

                local RunSvc = SafeService("RunService")
                if RunSvc then
                    local okCFrame, cframe, size = pcall(function() return clonedTargetChar:GetBoundingBox() end)
                    if okCFrame and size.Y > 0 then
                        local center = cframe.Position
                        local lookAt = center + Vector3.new(0, size.Y * (0.55 - 0.5), 0)
                        local angle = 0
                        targetRotationConnection = SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunSvc, "RenderStepped"), function(dt)
                            if not autoRotate then return end
                            angle = angle + (dt * rotateSpeed)
                            local camPos = lookAt + Vector3.new(math.sin(angle) * camDistance, size.Y * 0.12, math.cos(angle) * camDistance)
