                            pcall(function() targetCamera.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(camPos, lookAt) end)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            else
                -- Player OFFLINE (ghost/JSON): kamera FIXED (nggak pernah
                -- salah hitung -- lihat SetupFixedAvatarDisplay), tapi
                -- jaraknya di-override di sini biar SAMA PERSIS kayak
                -- avatar ONLINE (CAM_DISTANCE = 7.4), sesuai permintaan.
                -- Offset ini dikalibrasi dari formula kamera online:
                --   lookAt = center + (0, size.Y*0.05, 0)   -- VerticalBias 0.55
                --   camPos = lookAt + (0, size.Y*0.12, -7.4)
                -- Untuk rig standar (root.Position ≈ center bounding box).
                targetRotationConnection = SetupFixedAvatarDisplay(clonedTargetChar, targetCamera, {
                    CamOffset = Vector3.new(0, 0.95, -CAM_DISTANCE),
                    LookOffset = Vector3.new(0, 0.3, 0),
                    ShouldSpin = function() return autoRotate end,
                    SpinPerSec = rotateSpeed,
                })
            end
        end
    end

    if statUserIdCopyBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(statUserIdCopyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            local activeUserId = TargetPlayers[CurrentTargetIndex]
            if not activeUserId then return end
            local okCopy = pcall(function()
                if typeof(setclipboard) == "function" then
                    setclipboard(tostring(activeUserId))
                elseif typeof(toclipboard) == "function" then
                    toclipboard(tostring(activeUserId))
                end
            end)
            local original = statUserIdCopyBtn.Text
            statUserIdCopyBtn.Text = okCopy and "Disalin!" or "N/A"
            task.delay(1, function()
                pcall(function() statUserIdCopyBtn.Text = original end)
            end)
        end)
    end

    if statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(statAllFriendsLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreFriends then RenderMoreFriends() end
        end)
    end

    if statMutualLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(statMutualLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(statMutualLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreMutualFriends then RenderMoreMutualFriends() end
        end)
    end

    if statChatLogLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(statChatLogLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(statChatLogLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreChatLog then RenderMoreChatLog() end
        end)
    end

    if statAnimLogLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(statAnimLogLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(statAnimLogLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreAnimLog then RenderMoreAnimLog() end
        end)
    end

    if Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(Stats.statEncounterHistoryLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreEncounterHistory then RenderMoreEncounterHistory() end
        end)
    end

    if Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(Stats.statLeaderboardLoadMoreBtn)
            if RenderMoreLeaderboard then RenderMoreLeaderboard() end
        end)
    end

    if Stats.statNoteSaveBtn then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(Stats.statNoteSaveBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(Stats.statNoteSaveBtn)
            local activeUserId = TargetPlayers[CurrentTargetIndex]
            if not activeUserId then return end
            local activePlr = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(activeUserId)
            SetPlayerNote(activeUserId, Stats.statNoteBox.Text, activePlr)
            local _, updatedAt = GetPlayerNote(activeUserId)
            if updatedAt then
                local okFmt, text = pcall(function() return os.date("%d %b %Y, %H:%M", updatedAt) end)
                Stats.statNoteSavedAt.Text = "Tersimpan: " .. (okFmt and text or "-")
            else
                Stats.statNoteSavedAt.Text = "Catatan dihapus"
            end
            local original = Stats.statNoteSaveBtn.Text
            Stats.statNoteSaveBtn.Text = "Tersimpan!"
            task.delay(1, function()
                pcall(function() Stats.statNoteSaveBtn.Text = original end)
            end)
        end)
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(leftBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        RefreshPlayerList()
        if #TargetPlayers > 0 then
            CurrentTargetIndex = CurrentTargetIndex - 1
            if CurrentTargetIndex < 1 then CurrentTargetIndex = #TargetPlayers end
            UpdateTargetUI()
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(rightBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        RefreshPlayerList()
        if #TargetPlayers > 0 then
            CurrentTargetIndex = CurrentTargetIndex + 1
            if CurrentTargetIndex > #TargetPlayers then CurrentTargetIndex = 1 end
            UpdateTargetUI()
        end
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(1)
        RefreshPlayerList()
        if #TargetPlayers > 0 then CurrentTargetIndex = 1 end
        UpdateTargetUI()
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(2)
        BackgroundScanAllPlayers()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(Players, "PlayerAdded"), function(plr)

        if PlayerCache[plr.UserId] then
            PlayerCache[plr.UserId] = nil
            for i = #OfflineOrder, 1, -1 do
                if OfflineOrder[i] == plr.UserId then table.remove(OfflineOrder, i) end
            end
        end
        RefreshPlayerList()
        RecordEncounter(plr)
        task.wait(2)
        BackgroundPrefetchPlayer(plr)
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(Players, "PlayerRemoving"), function(leavingPlr)

        local c = PlayerCache[leavingPlr.UserId]
        if c then
            c.online = false

            c.lastSeenAt = os.time()
            if not c.snapshot then
                pcall(function() c.snapshot = SnapshotPlayer(leavingPlr) end)
            end
            if not seenInOfflineOrder(leavingPlr.UserId) then
                table.insert(OfflineOrder, leavingPlr.UserId)
            end
            if PersistLastSeen then PersistLastSeen(leavingPlr.UserId, c.lastSeenAt) end
            if PersistPlayerSnapshot and c.snapshot then PersistPlayerSnapshot(leavingPlr.UserId, c.snapshot) end
        end
        task.defer(RefreshPlayerList)

        if TargetPlayers[CurrentTargetIndex] == leavingPlr.UserId then
            task.defer(UpdateTargetUI)
        end
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(60)
            if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
            BackgroundScanAllPlayers()
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if not enterPressed then return end
        local query = string.lower(searchBox.Text or ""):gsub("^%s+", ""):gsub("%s+$", "")
        if query == "" then
            UpdateTargetUI()
            return
        end

        local foundIndex = nil
        for i, uid in ipairs(TargetPlayers) do
            local c = PlayerCache[uid]
            local dn = c and c.snapshot and c.snapshot.displayName
            local un = c and c.snapshot and c.snapshot.name
            if (dn and string.find(string.lower(dn), query, 1, true))
                or (un and string.find(string.lower(un), query, 1, true)) then
                foundIndex = i
                break
            end
        end

        if foundIndex then
            CurrentTargetIndex = foundIndex
            UpdateTargetUI()
        else

            searchBox.Text = ""
            searchBox.PlaceholderText = "Not found: \"" .. query .. "\""
            task.delay(1.4, function()
                pcall(function()
                    searchBox.PlaceholderText = "Search Player..."
                    UpdateTargetUI()
                end)
            end)
        end
    end)

    if getgenv then
        getgenv().JEYHUB_TargetSearchBox = searchBox
        getgenv().JEYHUB_TargetLeftBtn = leftBtn
        getgenv().JEYHUB_TargetRightBtn = rightBtn
        getgenv().JEYHUB_TargetInfoCard = infoCard
    end

            Parent = exampleWindow,
        })
        New("UICorner", { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0), Parent = exampleSheen })
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1, 1, 1), Color3.new(1, 1, 1)),
            Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.55),
                NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
            }),

            Parent = exampleSheen,
        })

        local exampleSpotlight = New("ImageLabel", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 260, 0, 260),
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Image = "rbxassetid://8992237877",
            ImageColor3 = accent,
            ImageTransparency = 0.88,
            ZIndex = 0,
            Parent = exampleWindow,
        })
        local ExampleMouse = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
        if ExampleMouse then
            local RunSvcSpot = SafeService("RunService")
            if RunSvcSpot then
                local lastSpotUpdate = 0
                SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunSvcSpot, "RenderStepped"), function()
                    local now = os.clock()
                    if now - lastSpotUpdate < 0.05 then return end
                    lastSpotUpdate = now
                    if exampleWindow.Visible and exampleSpotlight.Parent then
                        local relX = ExampleMouse.X - exampleWindow.AbsolutePosition.X
                        local relY = ExampleMouse.Y - exampleWindow.AbsolutePosition.Y
                        Tween(exampleSpotlight, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, nil, { Position = UDim2.new(0, relX, 0, relY) })
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,

            Parent = exampleHeader,

            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 32),

        local RunSvcMain = SafeService("RunService")
        if RunSvcMain then
            local lastSync = 0
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(RunSvcMain, "RenderStepped"), function()
                local now = os.clock()
                if now - lastSync < 0.03 then return end
                lastSync = now
                local r = Window.Root
                if not r or not r.Parent then return end
                local shouldShow = r.Visible and (not Window.Minimized) and (Window.CurrentTab == mainTab)
                if exampleWindow.Visible ~= shouldShow then exampleWindow.Visible = shouldShow end
                if exampleGlowOuter then exampleGlowOuter.Visible = shouldShow end
                if exampleGlowInner then exampleGlowInner.Visible = shouldShow end
                if shouldShow then
                    local panelHeight = r.AbsoluteSize.Y
                    local centerX = r.AbsolutePosition.X + r.AbsoluteSize.X + EXAMPLE_WINDOW_GAP + EXAMPLE_WINDOW_WIDTH / 2
                    local centerY = r.AbsolutePosition.Y + panelHeight / 2
                    exampleWindow.Position = UDim2.new(0, r.AbsolutePosition.X + r.AbsoluteSize.X + EXAMPLE_WINDOW_GAP, 0, centerY)
                    exampleWindow.Size = UDim2.new(0, EXAMPLE_WINDOW_WIDTH, 0, panelHeight)
                    if exampleGlowOuter then
                        exampleGlowOuter.Position = UDim2.new(0, centerX, 0, centerY)
                        exampleGlowOuter.Size = UDim2.new(0, EXAMPLE_WINDOW_WIDTH + 24, 0, panelHeight + 24)
                    end
                    if exampleGlowInner then
                        exampleGlowInner.Position = UDim2.new(0, centerX, 0, centerY)
                        exampleGlowInner.Size = UDim2.new(0, EXAMPLE_WINDOW_WIDTH + 14, 0, panelHeight + 14)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    else

        exampleWindow = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0), AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = wrapper })
        exampleScroll = exampleWindow
    end

    local scrollArea = exampleScroll

    local function MainPillBase(parent, height)
        local card = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.12,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, height or 38),
            Parent = parent,

            ClipsDescendants = true,
        })
        Round(card, 14)
        Stroke(card, accent, 1.1, 0.4)
        AddShine(card, 0.16)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 95,
            Parent = card,
        })

        return card
    end

    local function MainPillTitleBlock(card, title, subtitle, rightInset)
        -- CATATAN: subtitle di bawah judul pill (button/toggle/stepper/
        -- slider) SUDAH DIHAPUS sesuai permintaan -- parameter `subtitle`
        -- sengaja tetap diterima biar semua pemanggilan di bawah tidak
        -- perlu diubah, tapi memang tidak pernah dirender lagi. Judulnya
        -- sekarang di-tengah-kan vertikal di pill biar tetap rapi tanpa
        -- baris kosong sisa subtitle.
        local titleLbl = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -(12 + (rightInset or 12)), 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = tostring(title or ""),
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 11,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            Parent = card,
        })
        return titleLbl
    end

    local function CreateMainButton(config)
        config = config or {}
        local card = MainPillBase(scrollArea, 38)
        local cardStroke = card:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
        local titleLbl = MainPillTitleBlock(card, config.Title or "Button", config.Subtitle, 12)

        local hitbox = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
            Text = "",
            Parent = card,
        })

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseEnter"), function()
            Tween(card, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.02 })
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.15 }) end
            Tween(titleLbl, 0.12, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = accent })
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseLeave"), function()
            Tween(card, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.15 })
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.4 }) end
            Tween(titleLbl, 0.12, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = Palette.Text })
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click")
            CreateRipple(card)
            if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback) end
        end)

        return card
    end

    local function CreateMainToggle(config)
        config = config or {}
        local state = (config.Default == true)
        local card = MainPillBase(scrollArea, 38)
        local cardStroke = card:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
        MainPillTitleBlock(card, config.Title or "Toggle", config.Subtitle, 46)

        local switchTrack = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 17),
            BackgroundColor3 = state and accent or Palette.Element,
            BackgroundTransparency = state and 0.15 or 0.1,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(switchTrack, 9)
        Stroke(switchTrack, accent, 1, state and 0.15 or 0.6)

        local knob = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0.5),
            Position = state and UDim2.new(1, -15, 0.5, 0) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 13, 0, 13),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
            Parent = switchTrack,
        })
        Round(knob, 7)
        Stroke(knob, Color3.new(0, 0, 0), 1, 0.85)

        local hitbox = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
            Text = "",
            Parent = card,
        })

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseEnter"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.15 }) end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseLeave"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.4 }) end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(hitbox, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            state = not state
            PlayUISound(state and "ToggleOn" or "ToggleOff")
            Tween(switchTrack, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                BackgroundColor3 = state and accent or Palette.Element,
                BackgroundTransparency = state and 0.15 or 0.1,
            })
            Stroke(switchTrack, accent, 1, state and 0.15 or 0.6)
            Tween(knob, 0.15, nil, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
                Position = state and UDim2.new(1, -15, 0.5, 0) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, 0),
            })
            if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, state) end
        end)

        if config.Callback and config.CallOnInit then SafeCall(config.Callback, state) end
        return card
    end

    local function CreateMainStepper(config)
        config = config or {}
        local min, max, step = config.Min or 0, config.Max or 100, config.Step or 1
        local value = config.Default or min
        local card = MainPillBase(scrollArea, 38)
        local cardStroke = card:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
        MainPillTitleBlock(card, config.Title or "Stepper", config.Subtitle, 84)

        local minusBtn = New("TextButton", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "-",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 13,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(minusBtn, 10)
        Stroke(minusBtn, accent, 1, 0.5)

        local valueLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -34, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 28, 0, 18),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = tostring(value),
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 11,
            Parent = card,
        })

        local plusBtn = New("TextButton", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "+",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 13,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(plusBtn, 10)
        Stroke(plusBtn, accent, 1, 0.5)

        local function setValue(v)
            v = math.clamp(v, min, max)
            value = v
            valueLabel.Text = (step < 1) and string.format("%.1f", v) or tostring(math.floor(v + 0.5))
            if config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, value) end
        end

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(minusBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click"); CreateRipple(minusBtn); setValue(value - step)
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(plusBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            PlayUISound("Click"); CreateRipple(plusBtn); setValue(value + step)
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseEnter"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.15 }) end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseLeave"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.4 }) end
        end)

        if config.CallOnInit and config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, value) end
        return card
    end

    local function CreateMainSlider(config)
        config = config or {}
        local min, max, step = config.Min or 0, config.Max or 100, config.Step or 1
        local value = config.Default or min
        local card = MainPillBase(scrollArea, 48)
        local cardStroke = card:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
        MainPillTitleBlock(card, config.Title or "Slider", config.Subtitle, 50)

        local valueLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 5),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 14),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = tostring(value),
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right,
            Parent = card,
        })

        local track = New("Frame", {
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 1, -12),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 5),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(track, 3)
        local fill = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            Parent = track,
        })
        Round(fill, 3)
        local knob = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
            ZIndex = 2,
            Parent = track,
        })
        Round(knob, 6)
        Stroke(knob, Color3.new(0, 0, 0), 1, 0.85)

        local function ratioOf(v) return (v - min) / math.max(1e-6, (max - min)) end

        local function setValue(v, doCallback)
            v = math.clamp(v, min, max)
            value = v
            local ratio = ratioOf(v)
            fill.Size = UDim2.new(ratio, 0, 1, 0)
            knob.Position = UDim2.new(ratio, 0, 0.5, 0)
            valueLabel.Text = (step < 1) and string.format("%.1f", v) or tostring(math.floor(v + 0.5))
            if doCallback ~= false and config.Callback then SafeCall(config.Callback, value) end
        end

        local dragging = false
        local function updateFromInput(input)
            local rel = (input.Position.X - track.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, track.AbsoluteSize.X)
            rel = math.clamp(rel, 0, 1)
            local raw = min + rel * (max - min)
            local stepped = math.floor((raw - min) / step + 0.5) * step + min
            setValue(stepped)
        end

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(track, "InputBegan"), function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging = true
                updateFromInput(input)
            end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputEnded"), function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging = false
            end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(input)
            if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                updateFromInput(input)
            end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseEnter"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.15 }) end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseLeave"), function()
            if cardStroke then Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.4 }) end
        end)

        setValue(value, config.CallOnInit == true)
        return card
    end

    if getgenv then
        getgenv().JEYHUB_CreateMainButton = CreateMainButton
        getgenv().JEYHUB_CreateMainToggle = CreateMainToggle
        getgenv().JEYHUB_CreateMainStepper = CreateMainStepper
        getgenv().JEYHUB_CreateMainSlider = CreateMainSlider
    end

        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        Text = "Demo status will appear here.",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 9,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextWrapped = true,
        Parent = scrollArea,
    })
    Round(exampleStatus, 8)
    Stroke(exampleStatus, accent, 1, 0.7)
    Pad(exampleStatus, 10, 10, 0, 0)

        Title = "Example Toggle",
        Subtitle = "Nyala/mati sederhana — cek Callback(state)",
        Default = false,

            exampleStatus.Text = "Toggle: " .. (state and "ON ✅" or "OFF ⬜")
        end,
    })

    CreateMainToggle({
        Title = "Sound Effect",
        Subtitle = "Enable click & hover sound effects on the UI",
        Default = true,
        Callback = function(state)
            exampleStatus.Text = "Sound Effect: " .. (state and "ON ✅" or "OFF ⬜")
        end,
    })

    CreateMainButton({
        Title = "Example Button",
        Subtitle = "Click to run Callback() once",
        Callback = function()
            exampleStatus.Text = "Button clicked on " .. os.date("%H:%M:%S")
        end,
    })

    CreateMainButton({
        Title = "Refresh Target",
        Subtitle = "Reload the player list & latest target info",
        Callback = function()
            RefreshPlayerList()
            if #TargetPlayers > 0 and CurrentTargetIndex < 1 then CurrentTargetIndex = 1 end
            UpdateTargetUI()
            exampleStatus.Text = "Target refreshed at " .. os.date("%H:%M:%S")
        end,
    })

    CreateMainStepper({
        Title = "Example Stepper",
        Subtitle = "Click -/+ to see Callback(value) run live",
        Min = 0, Max = 10, Step = 1, Default = 5,
        Callback = function(value)
            exampleStatus.Text = "Stepper: " .. tostring(value)
        end,
    })

    CreateMainStepper({
        Title = "Rotation Speed",
        Subtitle = "Adjust the target viewport camera's rotation speed",
        Min = 0, Max = 3, Step = 0.1, Default = 0.6,
        Callback = function(value)
            rotateSpeed = value
            exampleStatus.Text = "Rotation Speed: " .. tostring(value)
        end,
    })

    CreateMainSlider({
        Title = "Example Slider",
        Subtitle = "Drag to see Callback(value) run live",
        Min = 0, Max = 100, Step = 1, Default = 50,
        Callback = function(value)
            exampleStatus.Text = "Slider: " .. tostring(value)
        end,
    })

    CreateMainSlider({
        Title = "Jarak Kamera Viewport",
        Subtitle = "Adjust how close the 3D camera is to the target",
        Min = 3, Max = 12, Step = 0.5, Default = 6.2,
        Callback = function(value)
            exampleStatus.Text = "Jarak Kamera: " .. tostring(value)
        end,
    })

    -- Inisialisasi awal: bangun daftar target SEKARANG JUGA (bukan
    -- nunggu event PlayerAdded pertama, yang tidak akan pernah nembak
    -- untuk player yang sudah ada duluan di server saat script di-load).
    -- RefreshPlayerList otomatis menggabungkan player yang online SEKARANG
    -- dengan OfflineOrder (daftar riwayat dari data.json) -- jadi begitu
    -- keluar-masuk game lagi/rejoin, semua histori (Encounter Tracker,
    -- chat log, teman yang keluar, terakhir dilihat, snapshot profil, dst)
    -- yang sebelumnya sudah tersimpan langsung kelihatan lagi di kartu
    -- Main tab tanpa perlu klik "Refresh Target" manual dulu.
    RefreshPlayerList()
    if #TargetPlayers > 0 and CurrentTargetIndex < 1 then CurrentTargetIndex = 1 end
    UpdateTargetUI()
end

local function BuildAvatarChangerTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Avatar Changer"]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local AvatarEditorService = SafeService("AvatarEditorService")

    local function enumItem(enumType, name)
        local ok, value = pcall(function() return enumType[name] end)
        if ok then return value end
        return nil
    end

    local function formatItemPrice(item)
        local price = item.Price or item.LowestPrice
        if item.IsForSale == false and not price then
            return "Off-Sale"
        end
        if price == nil then return "—" end
        if type(price) ~= "number" then return tostring(price) end
        if price <= 0 then return "Gratis" end
        return "R$ " .. tostring(price)
    end

    local SUB_TABS = {
        { key = "hats", label = "Hats", placeholder = "Search hat, e.g.: fedora",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "Hat") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "hair", label = "Hair", placeholder = "Search hair",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "HairAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "faceAcc", label = "Face Acc", placeholder = "Search face accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "FaceAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "neck", label = "Neck", placeholder = "Search neck accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "NeckAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "shoulder", label = "Shoulder", placeholder = "Search shoulder accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "ShoulderAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "waist", label = "Waist", placeholder = "Search waist accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "WaistAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "front", label = "Front", placeholder = "Search front accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "FrontAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "back", label = "Back", placeholder = "Search back accessory",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "BackAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "jacket", label = "Jacket", placeholder = "Search jacket",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "JacketAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "sweater", label = "Sweater", placeholder = "Search sweater",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "SweaterAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "pantsAcc", label = "Pants Layered", placeholder = "Search layered pants",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "PantsAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "shoes", label = "Shoes", placeholder = "Search shoes",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "LeftShoeAccessory"), enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "RightShoeAccessory") }, mode = "accessory" },
        { key = "classicShirt", label = "Shirt Classic", placeholder = "Search classic shirt",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "Shirt") }, mode = "single" },
        { key = "classicPants", label = "Pants Classic", placeholder = "Search classic pants",
          assetTypes = { enumItem(Enum.AvatarAssetType, "Pants") }, mode = "single" },
        { key = "body", label = "Body", placeholder = "Adjust body part & body asset below",
          assetTypes = {}, mode = "body" },
        { key = "myitems", label = "My Items", placeholder = "Avatar items you're currently wearing",
          assetTypes = {}, mode = "myitems" },
        { key = "applied", label = "Applied", placeholder = "Currently active items",
          assetTypes = {}, mode = "applied" },
    }
    for _, t in ipairs(SUB_TABS) do
        local filtered = {}
        for _, at in ipairs(t.assetTypes) do
            if at then table.insert(filtered, at) end
        end
        t.assetTypes = filtered
    end

    local KORBLOX_RIGHT_LEG_ASSET = 139607718
    local LOCAL_ACCESSORY_ATTRIBUTE = "JEYHUB_AC_AssetId"
    local LOCAL_GROUP_ATTRIBUTE = "JEYHUB_AC_Group"
    local LOCAL_BODY_ATTRIBUTE = "JEYHUB_AC_BodyVisual"

    local section = tab:CreateSection("Avatar Changer", "Change accessories, face & body locally (client-side only)")
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body
    if not body then return end

    local appliedItems, appliedOrder = {}, {}
    local reapplying = false

    -- Applied items sekarang di section "avatarApplied" pada file JSON
    -- gabungan JEYHUB/data.json -- bukan applied_items.json terpisah.
    local function saveAppliedConfig()
        JD_Set("avatarApplied", {
            appliedOrder = appliedOrder,
            appliedItems = appliedItems,
        })
    end

    local function loadAppliedConfig()
        local data = JD_Get("avatarApplied", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end
        if type(data.appliedItems) ~= "table" or type(data.appliedOrder) ~= "table" then return end

        local cleanOrder = {}
        for _, v in ipairs(data.appliedOrder) do
            if type(v) == "string" then table.insert(cleanOrder, v) end
        end

        appliedItems = data.appliedItems
        appliedOrder = cleanOrder
    end
    loadAppliedConfig()
    local hiddenState = {}
    local classicShirtState = nil
    local classicPantsState = nil
    local originalDescription = nil
    local selectedTab = SUB_TABS[1]
    local currentPages = nil
    local loadingMore = false
    local activeHolder = nil

    local function appliedKey(kind, assetId) return tostring(kind) .. ":" .. tostring(assetId) end

    local function rememberApplied(item)
        local key = item.key or appliedKey(item.kind, item.assetId)
        item.key = key
        if not appliedItems[key] then table.insert(appliedOrder, key) end
        appliedItems[key] = item
        saveAppliedConfig()
    end

    local function forgetAppliedKey(key)
        appliedItems[key] = nil
        for i = #appliedOrder, 1, -1 do
            if appliedOrder[i] == key then table.remove(appliedOrder, i) end
        end
        saveAppliedConfig()
    end

    local function forgetApplied(kind, assetId)
        forgetAppliedKey(appliedKey(kind, assetId))
    end

    local function appliedCount()
        local c = 0
        for _, key in ipairs(appliedOrder) do
            if appliedItems[key] then c = c + 1 end
        end
        return c
    end

    local function getCharacter()
        return LocalPlayer and (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait())
    end

    local function getHumanoid()
        local char = getCharacter()
        if not char then return nil end
        local ok, hum = pcall(function()
            return char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") or char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 8)
        end)
        if ok then return hum end
        return nil
    end

    local function loadAsset(assetId)
        local ok, objects = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. tostring(assetId)) end)
        if not ok then return nil, tostring(objects) end
        if not objects or #objects == 0 then return nil, "Asset failed to load." end
        return objects
    end

    local function findFirstDescendant(root, predicate)
        if predicate(root) then return root end
        for _, child in ipairs(root:GetDescendants()) do
            if predicate(child) then return child end
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function rememberVisual(instance)
        if hiddenState[instance] then return end
        if instance:IsA("BasePart") then
            hiddenState[instance] = { Transparency = instance.Transparency, LocalTransparencyModifier = instance.LocalTransparencyModifier }
        elseif instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture") then
            hiddenState[instance] = { Transparency = instance.Transparency }
        end
    end

    local function hideVisual(instance)
        rememberVisual(instance)
        pcall(function()
            if instance:IsA("BasePart") then
                instance.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
            elseif instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture") then
                instance.Transparency = 1
            end
        end)
    end

    local function restoreVisual(instance)
        local state = hiddenState[instance]
        if not state then return end
        pcall(function()
            if instance:IsA("BasePart") then
                instance.Transparency = state.Transparency
                instance.LocalTransparencyModifier = state.LocalTransparencyModifier
            elseif instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture") then
                instance.Transparency = state.Transparency
            end
        end)
        hiddenState[instance] = nil
    end

    local function findHandleAttachment(handle)
        for _, child in ipairs(handle:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Attachment") then return child end
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function findCharacterAttachment(character, attachmentName)
        for _, d in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if d:IsA("Attachment") and d.Name == attachmentName and d.Parent and d.Parent:IsA("BasePart") then
                return d
            end
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function manualAttachAccessory(accessory)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end
        local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
        if not handle or not handle:IsA("BasePart") then return false, "Accessory has no Handle." end
        local handleAttachment = findHandleAttachment(handle)
        if not handleAttachment then return false, "Handle has no attachment." end
        local characterAttachment = findCharacterAttachment(character, handleAttachment.Name)
        if not characterAttachment then return false, "Character has no attachment " .. handleAttachment.Name end

        local ok = pcall(function()
            accessory.Parent = character
            handle.Anchored = false
            handle.CanCollide = false
            handle.Massless = true
            handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
            handle.CFrame = characterAttachment.Parent.CFrame * characterAttachment.CFrame * handleAttachment.CFrame:Inverse()

            local oldWeld = handle:FindFirstChild("AccessoryWeld")
            if oldWeld then oldWeld:Destroy() end
            local weld = Instance.new("Weld")
            weld.Name = "AccessoryWeld"
            weld.Part0 = handle
            weld.Part1 = characterAttachment.Parent
            weld.C0 = handleAttachment.CFrame
            weld.C1 = characterAttachment.CFrame
            weld.Parent = handle
        end)
        if not ok then return false, "Failed to manually weld accessory." end
        return true
    end

    local function addAccessory(tabKey, assetId)
        local humanoid = getHumanoid()
        if not humanoid then return false, "Humanoid not found." end
        local objects, err = loadAsset(assetId)
        if not objects then return false, err end

        local accessory
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do
            accessory = findFirstDescendant(object, function(c) return c:IsA("Accessory") end)
            if accessory then break end
        end
        if not accessory then
            for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
            return false, "Asset bukan accessory."
        end

        accessory.Parent = nil
        accessory:SetAttribute(LOCAL_ACCESSORY_ATTRIBUTE, tostring(assetId))
        accessory:SetAttribute(LOCAL_GROUP_ATTRIBUTE, tabKey)

        local ok, addErr = pcall(function() humanoid:AddAccessory(accessory) end)
        local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
        local hasWeld = handle and handle:FindFirstChild("AccessoryWeld")
        if ok and hasWeld then return true end

        local weldOk, weldErr = manualAttachAccessory(accessory)
        if weldOk then return true end
        return false, ok and tostring(weldErr) or tostring(addErr)
    end

    local function removeAccessory(tabKey, assetId)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end
        local removed = 0
        for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Accessory")
                and child:GetAttribute(LOCAL_ACCESSORY_ATTRIBUTE) == tostring(assetId)
                and child:GetAttribute(LOCAL_GROUP_ATTRIBUTE) == tabKey then
                pcall(function() child:Destroy() end)
                removed = removed + 1
            end
        end
        return true, removed > 0 and ("Deleting " .. removed .. " local copies.") or "No matching local copy."
    end

    local function applyClassicShirt(assetId)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end

        local objects, err = loadAsset(assetId)
        if not objects then return false, err end

        local sourceShirt
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do
            sourceShirt = findFirstDescendant(object, function(c) return c:IsA("Shirt") end)
            if sourceShirt then break end
        end
        if not sourceShirt then
            for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
            return false, "Asset bukan classic shirt."
        end

        local shirt = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Shirt")
        if not shirt then
            shirt = Instance.new("Shirt")
            shirt.Name = "Shirt"
            shirt.Parent = character
        end
        if not classicShirtState then
            classicShirtState = { Instance = shirt, Template = shirt.ShirtTemplate }
        end
        shirt.ShirtTemplate = sourceShirt.ShirtTemplate
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
        return true
    end

    local function restoreClassicShirt()
        if not classicShirtState or not classicShirtState.Instance or not classicShirtState.Instance.Parent then
            return false, "No saved shirt to restore."
        end
        classicShirtState.Instance.ShirtTemplate = classicShirtState.Template
        classicShirtState = nil
        return true
    end

    local function applyClassicPants(assetId)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end

        local objects, err = loadAsset(assetId)
        if not objects then return false, err end

        local sourcePants
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do
            sourcePants = findFirstDescendant(object, function(c) return c:IsA("Pants") end)
            if sourcePants then break end
        end
        if not sourcePants then
            for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
            return false, "Asset bukan classic pants."
        end

        local pants = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Pants")
        if not pants then
            pants = Instance.new("Pants")
            pants.Name = "Pants"
            pants.Parent = character
        end
        if not classicPantsState then
            classicPantsState = { Instance = pants, Template = pants.PantsTemplate }
        end
        pants.PantsTemplate = sourcePants.PantsTemplate
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
        return true
    end

    local function restoreClassicPants()
        if not classicPantsState or not classicPantsState.Instance or not classicPantsState.Instance.Parent then
            return false, "No saved pants to restore."
        end
        classicPantsState.Instance.PantsTemplate = classicPantsState.Template
        classicPantsState = nil
        return true
    end

    local function applySingle(tabKey, assetId)
        if tabKey == "classicShirt" then return applyClassicShirt(assetId) end
        if tabKey == "classicPants" then return applyClassicPants(assetId) end
        return addAccessory(tabKey, assetId)
    end

    local function setHeadless(enabled)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end

        local head = findFirstDescendant(character, function(inst)
            return inst.Name == "Head" and inst:IsA("BasePart")
        end)
        if not head then return false, "Head not found." end
        if enabled then
            hideVisual(head)
            for _, child in ipairs(head:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Decal") or child:IsA("Texture") then hideVisual(child) end
            end
        else
            restoreVisual(head)
            for _, child in ipairs(head:GetChildren()) do restoreVisual(child) end
        end
        return true
    end

    local function setKorbloxLike(enabled)
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end

        local function findBodyPart(name)
            return findFirstDescendant(character, function(inst)
                return inst.Name == name and inst:IsA("BasePart")
            end)
        end

        for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if child:GetAttribute(LOCAL_BODY_ATTRIBUTE) == "KorbloxRightLeg" then
                pcall(function() child:Destroy() end)
            end
        end

        local function restoreOriginals(names)
            for _, name in ipairs(names) do
                local part = findBodyPart(name)
                if part then
                    restoreVisual(part)
                    for _, child in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do restoreVisual(child) end
                end
            end
        end

        if not enabled then
            restoreOriginals({ "RightUpperLeg", "RightLowerLeg", "RightFoot", "Right Leg" })
            return true
        end

        local isR6 = findBodyPart("Right Leg") ~= nil
        local isR15 = findBodyPart("RightUpperLeg") ~= nil and findBodyPart("RightLowerLeg") ~= nil and findBodyPart("RightFoot") ~= nil
        if not isR6 and not isR15 then
            return false, "Character rig not recognized (not standard R6/R15)."
        end

        local objects, err = loadAsset(KORBLOX_RIGHT_LEG_ASSET)
        if not objects then return false, err end

        local sourceParts = {}
        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do
            for _, d in ipairs(object:GetDescendants()) do
                if d:IsA("MeshPart") and (d.Name == "RightUpperLeg" or d.Name == "RightLowerLeg" or d.Name == "RightFoot") then
                    sourceParts[d.Name] = d
                end
            end
            if object:IsA("MeshPart") and (object.Name == "RightUpperLeg" or object.Name == "RightLowerLeg" or object.Name == "RightFoot") then
                sourceParts[object.Name] = object
            end
        end

        if not sourceParts.RightUpperLeg or not sourceParts.RightLowerLeg or not sourceParts.RightFoot then
            for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
            return false, "Korblox leg mesh failed to load."
        end

        local visualModel = Instance.new("Model")
        visualModel.Name = "JEYHUB_AC_KorbloxRightLeg"
        visualModel:SetAttribute(LOCAL_BODY_ATTRIBUTE, "KorbloxRightLeg")
        visualModel.Parent = character

        local function prepClone(source, name)
            local clone = source:Clone()
            clone.Name = "AC_" .. name
            clone:SetAttribute(LOCAL_BODY_ATTRIBUTE, "KorbloxRightLeg")
            clone.Anchored = false
            clone.CanCollide = false
            clone.Massless = true
            clone.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
            for _, d in ipairs(clone:GetDescendants()) do
                if d:IsA("WrapTarget") or d:IsA("Attachment") or d:IsA("JointInstance") then
                    pcall(function() d:Destroy() end)
                end
            end
            clone.Parent = visualModel
            return clone
        end

        local function weldClone(clone, targetPart, offset)
            clone.CFrame = targetPart.CFrame * (offset or CFrame.new())
            local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint")
            weld.Name = "AC_KorbloxWeld"
            weld.Part0 = clone
            weld.Part1 = targetPart
            weld.Parent = clone
        end

        local attachedCount = 0

        if isR6 then
            local rightLeg = findBodyPart("Right Leg")
            if not rightLeg then
                pcall(function() visualModel:Destroy() end)
                for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end
                return false, "R6 Right Leg not found."
            end
            hideVisual(rightLeg)
            for _, child in ipairs(rightLeg:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Decal") or child:IsA("Texture") then hideVisual(child) end
            end
            local scale = math.clamp(rightLeg.Size.Y / 2, 0.75, 1.6)
            local upper = prepClone(sourceParts.RightUpperLeg, "RightUpperLeg")
            local lower = prepClone(sourceParts.RightLowerLeg, "RightLowerLeg")
            local foot = prepClone(sourceParts.RightFoot, "RightFoot")
            upper.Size = sourceParts.RightUpperLeg.Size * scale
            lower.Size = sourceParts.RightLowerLeg.Size * scale
            foot.Size = sourceParts.RightFoot.Size * scale
            weldClone(upper, rightLeg, CFrame.new(0, rightLeg.Size.Y * 0.24, 0))
            weldClone(lower, rightLeg, CFrame.new(0, -rightLeg.Size.Y * 0.18, 0))
            weldClone(foot, rightLeg, CFrame.new(0, -rightLeg.Size.Y * 0.48, -rightLeg.Size.Z * 0.18))
            attachedCount = 3
        else
            local partNames = { "RightUpperLeg", "RightLowerLeg", "RightFoot" }
            for _, name in ipairs(partNames) do
                local targetPart = findBodyPart(name)
                if targetPart then
                    hideVisual(targetPart)
                    for _, child in ipairs(targetPart:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("Decal") or child:IsA("Texture") then hideVisual(child) end
                    end
                    local clone = prepClone(sourceParts[name], name)
                    clone.Size = targetPart.Size
                    weldClone(clone, targetPart)
                    attachedCount = attachedCount + 1
                end
            end
        end

        for _, object in ipairs(objects) do pcall(function() object:Destroy() end) end

        if attachedCount == 0 then
            pcall(function() visualModel:Destroy() end)
            return false, "No leg parts were successfully attached."
        end

        return true
    end

    local function captureOriginalDescription()
        local humanoid = getHumanoid()
        if not humanoid then return end
        local ok, desc = pcall(function() return humanoid:GetAppliedDescription() end)
        if not ok or not desc then return end
        local okClone, clone = pcall(function() return desc:Clone() end)
        originalDescription = (okClone and clone) or desc
    end
    captureOriginalDescription()

    local BODY_PART_FIELDS = {
        Torso = "Torso", ["Left Arm"] = "LeftArm", ["Right Arm"] = "RightArm",
        ["Left Leg"] = "LeftLeg", ["Right Leg"] = "RightLeg",
    }

    local function applyBodyPart(fieldName, assetId)
        local numericId = tonumber(assetId)
        if not numericId then return false, "Asset ID must be a number." end
        local humanoid = getHumanoid()
        if not humanoid then return false, "Humanoid not found." end
        local okDesc, desc = pcall(function() return humanoid:GetAppliedDescription() end)
        if not okDesc or not desc then return false, "Failed to read HumanoidDescription." end
        local okSet = pcall(function() desc[fieldName] = numericId end)
        if not okSet then return false, "Invalid body part field: " .. tostring(fieldName) end
        local okApply, applyErr = pcall(function() humanoid:ApplyDescription(desc) end)
        if not okApply then return false, tostring(applyErr) end
        return true
    end

    local BODY_SCALE_FIELDS = {
        Height     = "HeightScale",
        Width      = "WidthScale",
        Head       = "HeadScale",
        BodyType   = "BodyTypeScale",
        Proportion = "ProportionScale",
    }

    local function getCurrentScale(fieldName, fallback)
        local humanoid = getHumanoid()
        if not humanoid then return fallback end
        local okDesc, desc = pcall(function() return humanoid:GetAppliedDescription() end)
        if not okDesc or not desc then return fallback end
        local okRead, value = pcall(function() return desc[fieldName] end)
        if not okRead or type(value) ~= "number" then return fallback end
        return value
    end

    local function applyBodyScale(fieldName, value, persist)
        local humanoid = getHumanoid()
        if not humanoid then return false, "Humanoid not found." end
        local okDesc, desc = pcall(function() return humanoid:GetAppliedDescription() end)
        if not okDesc or not desc then return false, "Failed to read HumanoidDescription." end
        local okSet = pcall(function() desc[fieldName] = value end)
        if not okSet then return false, "Invalid scale field: " .. tostring(fieldName) end

        if not persist then

            local okApply, applyErr = pcall(function() humanoid:ApplyDescription(desc) end)
            if not okApply then return false, tostring(applyErr) end
            return true
        end

        if not AvatarEditorService then
            local okApply = pcall(function() humanoid:ApplyDescription(desc) end)
            return okApply, (not okApply) and "AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor; changes are local only." or "AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor; changes are local only."
        end
        local okPrompt, promptErr = pcall(function()
            AvatarEditorService:PromptSaveAvatar(desc, humanoid.RigType)
        end)
        if not okPrompt then return false, tostring(promptErr) end
        local okWait, result = pcall(function()
            return AvatarEditorService.PromptSaveAvatarCompleted:Wait()
        end)
        if not okWait then return false, tostring(result) end
        if result ~= Enum.AvatarPromptResult.Success then
            return false, "Cancelled / failed to save (" .. tostring(result) .. ")."
        end
        pcall(function() humanoid:ApplyDescription(desc) end)
        return true
    end

    local KEEP_POSITION_ON_RIG_SWITCH = true

    local function setRigType(targetRigType)
        if not AvatarEditorService then
            return false, "AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor."
        end
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return false, "Character not found." end
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid then return false, "Humanoid not found." end
        if humanoid.RigType == targetRigType then return true end

        local okDesc, desc = pcall(function() return humanoid:GetAppliedDescription() end)
        if not okDesc or not desc then return false, "Failed to read HumanoidDescription." end

        local savedPos
        if KEEP_POSITION_ON_RIG_SWITCH then
            local hrp = findFirstDescendant(character, function(inst)
                return inst.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" and inst:IsA("BasePart")
            end)
            if hrp then savedPos = hrp.CFrame end
        end

        local okPrompt, promptErr = pcall(function()
            AvatarEditorService:PromptSaveAvatar(desc, targetRigType)
        end)
        if not okPrompt then return false, tostring(promptErr) end

        local okWait, result = pcall(function()
            return AvatarEditorService.PromptSaveAvatarCompleted:Wait()
        end)
        if not okWait then return false, tostring(result) end
        if result ~= Enum.AvatarPromptResult.Success then
            return false, "Cancelled / failed to save (" .. tostring(result) .. ")."
        end

        pcall(function()
            humanoid.Health = 0
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead)
        end)

        local okNewChar, newChar = pcall(function() return LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait() end)
        if okNewChar and newChar and savedPos then
            task.spawn(function()
                local newHRP = newChar:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5)
                if newHRP then pcall(function() newHRP.CFrame = savedPos end) end
            end)
        end

        return true
    end

    local refreshBodyTools = nil

    local SPECIAL_SINGLE_TABS = { classicShirt = true, classicPants = true }

    local function applyStoredItem(item)
        if item.kind == "accessory" then
            removeAccessory(item.tabKey, item.assetId)
            return addAccessory(item.tabKey, item.assetId)
        elseif item.kind == "single" then
            if not SPECIAL_SINGLE_TABS[item.tabKey] then removeAccessory(item.tabKey, item.assetId) end
            return applySingle(item.tabKey, item.assetId)
        elseif item.kind == "headless" then
            return setHeadless(true)
        elseif item.kind == "korblox" then
            return setKorbloxLike(true)
        end
        return false, "Unknown applied item type."
    end

    local function removeAppliedItem(item)
        if item.kind == "accessory" then
            removeAccessory(item.tabKey, item.assetId)
        elseif item.kind == "single" then
            if item.tabKey == "classicShirt" then
                restoreClassicShirt()
            elseif item.tabKey == "classicPants" then
                restoreClassicPants()
            else
                removeAccessory(item.tabKey, item.assetId)
            end
        elseif item.kind == "headless" then
            setHeadless(false)
        elseif item.kind == "korblox" then
            setKorbloxLike(false)
        end
        forgetAppliedKey(item.key)
        return true
    end

    local function reapplyAllStoredItems()
        for _, key in ipairs(appliedOrder) do
            local item = appliedItems[key]
            if item then
                pcall(applyStoredItem, items)
            end
        end
    end

    if LocalPlayer then
        SafeConnect(LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded, function(newCharacter)

            pcall(function() newCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5) end)
            task.wait(0.3)
            if not IsCurrentRun() then return end
            if LocalPlayer.Character ~= newCharacter then return end
            reapplyAllStoredItems()
        end)
    end

    local function buildMetaRow(item, parent, y)
        local metaRow = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, y),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 14),
            Parent = parent,
        })

        local priceStr = formatItemPrice(item)
        local hasRobux = priceStr:sub(1, 2) == "R$"
        local priceValueText = hasRobux and priceStr:gsub("^R%$%s*", "") or priceStr

        if hasRobux then
            New("ImageLabel", {
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 1),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 11, 0, 11),
                Image = "rbxasset://textures/icon_ROBUX.png",
                ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit,
                Parent = metaRow,
            })
        end

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, hasRobux and 14 or 0, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0.5, hasRobux and -14 or 0, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = priceValueText,
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            Parent = metaRow,
        })

        local isVerified = item.CreatorHasVerifiedBadge == true
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0.5, isVerified and -14 or 0, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = tostring(item.CreatorName or "?"),
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            Parent = metaRow,
        })

        if isVerified then
            local badge = New("Frame", {
                BackgroundColor3 = accent,
                Position = UDim2.new(1, -11, 0, 1),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 11, 0, 11),
                Parent = metaRow,
            })
            Round(badge, 6)
            New("TextLabel", {
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
                Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
                Text = "✓",
                TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
                TextSize = 8,
                Parent = badge,
            })
        end
    end

    local function itemCard(item, holder)
        local card = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        Round(card, 12)
        local cardStroke = Stroke(card, accent, 1, 0.7)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 100,
            Parent = card,
        })

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseEnter"), function()
            Tween(card, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.12 })
            Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.35 })
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseLeave"), function()
            if lastSelectedCardStroke == cardStroke then return end
            Tween(card, 0.18, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.25 })
            Tween(cardStroke, 0.18, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.7 })
        end)

        local thumb = New("ImageLabel", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 62),
            ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit,
            Parent = card,
        })
        LoadThumbnail(thumb, "rbxthumb://type=Asset&id=" .. tostring(item.Id) .. "&w=150&h=150")
        Round(thumb, 8)

        local previewClick = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Text = "",
            Position = thumb.Position,
            Size = thumb.Size,
            Parent = card,
        })
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(previewClick, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            setStatus("Preview: " .. tostring(item.Name or item.Id), false)
            if lastSelectedCardStroke and lastSelectedCardStroke ~= cardStroke then
                Tween(lastSelectedCardStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.7, Thickness = 1 })
            end
            Tween(cardStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.1, Thickness = 1.5 })
            lastSelectedCardStroke = cardStroke
        end)

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 70),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = item.Name or ("Asset " .. tostring(item.Id)),
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 9,
            TextWrapped = true,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
            Parent = card,
        })

        buildMetaRow(item, card, 88)

        local isAccessory = selectedTab.mode == "accessory"
        local applyBtn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 105),
            Size = isAccessory and UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 18) or UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 18),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = isAccessory and "Add" or "Apply",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 9,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(applyBtn, 7)
        AddButtonHover(applyBtn)

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(applyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            local ok, err
            if selectedTab.mode == "accessory" then
                ok, err = addAccessory(selectedTab.key, item.Id)
            else
                ok, err = applySingle(selectedTab.key, item.Id)
            end
            if ok then
                rememberApplied({
                    key = selectedTab.mode == "single" and ("single:" .. selectedTab.key) or nil,
                    kind = selectedTab.mode,
                    tabKey = selectedTab.key,
                    assetId = item.Id,
                    name = item.Name or ("Asset " .. tostring(item.Id)),
                    image = "rbxthumb://type=Asset&id=" .. tostring(item.Id) .. "&w=150&h=150",
                })
            end
            setStatus(ok and ("Diterapkan: " .. tostring(item.Name or item.Id)) or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
        end)

        if isAccessory then
            local removeBtn = New("TextButton", {
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 70, 90),
                BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
                Position = UDim2.new(1, -32, 0, 105),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 18),
                Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
                Text = "-",
                TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
                TextSize = 10,
                Parent = card,
            })
            Round(removeBtn, 7)
            AddButtonHover(removeBtn)
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(removeBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
                local ok, err = removeAccessory(selectedTab.key, item.Id)
                if ok then forgetApplied("accessory", item.Id) end
                setStatus(ok and ("Dihapus: " .. tostring(item.Name or item.Id)) or ("Failed to delete: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
            end)
        end
    end

    local function renderPage(page)
        clearResults()
        activeHolder = newCardsHolder()
        for _, item in ipairs(page) do
            itemCard(item, activeHolder)
        end
        if #page == 0 then
            setStatus("No results.", true)
        else
            setStatus("Showing " .. tostring(#page) .. " results.", false)
        end
    end

    local function appendPage(page)
        if not activeHolder then activeHolder = newCardsHolder() end
        for _, item in ipairs(page) do
            itemCard(item, activeHolder)
        end
    end

    local _acLastCall   = 0
    local _acRetries    = 0
    local _AC_MIN_GAP   = 0.7
    local _AC_BACKOFFS  = { 1, 2, 4, 8 }
    local totalLoaded   = 0
    local loadMoreBtn   = nil

    local function updateLoadMoreBtn()
        if not loadMoreBtn then return end
        local okFin, fin = pcall(function() return currentPages and currentPages.IsFinished end)
        local done = okFin and fin
        pcall(function()
            loadMoreBtn.Visible = (currentPages ~= nil) and not done
            loadMoreBtn.Text = loadingMore and "⏳ Loading..." or ("↓ Load More (" .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " items)")
        end)
    end

    local function loadMore()
        if loadingMore then return end
        if selectedTab.mode ~= "accessory" and selectedTab.mode ~= "single" then return end
        if not currentPages then return end
        local okFin, fin = pcall(function() return currentPages.IsFinished end)
        if okFin and fin then
            setStatus("✓ All " .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " items already loaded.", false)
            updateLoadMoreBtn()
            return
        end

        local now = os.clock()
        if now - _acLastCall < _AC_MIN_GAP then return end

        loadingMore = true
        updateLoadMoreBtn()
        setStatus("Loading more...", false)

        task.spawn(function()
            _acLastCall = os.clock()
            local okAdv, advErr = pcall(function() TryElevateIdentity(); currentPages:AdvanceToNextPageAsync() end)

            if not okAdv then

                _acRetries = math.min(_acRetries + 1, #_AC_BACKOFFS)
                local delay = _AC_BACKOFFS[_acRetries]
                setStatus(("⚠ Rate limit! Retry #" .. _acRetries .. " in " .. delay .. "s..."), true)
                task.wait(delay)
                loadingMore = false
                _acLastCall = os.clock()
                updateLoadMoreBtn()

                if _acRetries < #_AC_BACKOFFS then
                    loadMore()
                else
                    setStatus("✕ Failed to load after " .. #_AC_BACKOFFS .. "x retry. Try again manually.", true)
                    _acRetries = 0
                end
                return
            end

            _acRetries = 0
            local okPage, page = pcall(function() return currentPages:GetCurrentPage() end)
            loadingMore = false

            if okPage and page then
                appendPage(page)
                totalLoaded = totalLoaded + #page
                local okFin2, fin2 = pcall(function() return currentPages.IsFinished end)
                if okFin2 and fin2 then
                    setStatus("✓ All " .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " items loaded.", false)
                else
                    setStatus("Loaded: " .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " items  •  scroll / click Load More to continue", false)
                end
            end
            updateLoadMoreBtn()
        end)
    end

        AddButtonHover(actionBtn)

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(actionBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            callback(input.Text)
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
            if enterPressed then callback(input.Text) end
        end)

        return row
    end

    local function bodyScaleSlider(label, detail, fieldName, min, max, decimals)
        local row = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 58),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
            Parent = resultsFrame,
        })
        Round(row, 11)
        Stroke(row, accent, 1, 0.6)
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 4),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -70, 0, 14),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = label,
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            Parent = row,
        })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 18),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -70, 0, 12),
            Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
            Text = detail,
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            Parent = row,
        })
        local valueLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 4),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 14),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "",
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right,
            Parent = row,
        })

        local trackF = New("TextButton", {
            AutoButtonColor = false,
            Text = "",
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 1, -18),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 6),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
            Parent = row,
        })
        Round(trackF, 3)
        local fill = New("Frame", { BackgroundColor3 = accent, Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0), Parent = trackF })
        Round(fill, 3)
        local knob = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Text,
            ZIndex = 2,
            Parent = trackF,
        })
        Round(knob, 6)

        local fmt = "%." .. tostring(decimals or 2) .. "f"
        local function apply(v, persist)
            v = math.clamp(v, min, max)
            local mult = 10 ^ (decimals or 2)
            v = math.floor(v * mult + 0.5) / mult
            local frac = (max > min) and (v - min) / (max - min) or 0
            SafeSet(fill, "Size", UDim2.new(frac, 0, 1, 0))
            SafeSet(knob, "Position", UDim2.new(frac, 0, 0.5, 0))
            valueLabel.Text = string.format(fmt, v)
            if persist then
                setStatus("Saving " .. label .. " permanently to account...", false)
                task.spawn(function()
                    local ok, err = applyBodyScale(fieldName, v, true)
                    setStatus(ok and (label .. " saved permanently (persists after refresh/!re).")
                        or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
                end)
            else
                local ok, err = applyBodyScale(fieldName, v, false)
                if not ok then setStatus("Failed: " .. tostring(err), true) end
            end
            return v
        end

        local dragging = false
        local lastValue = getCurrentScale(fieldName, (min + max) / 2)
        local function fromX(px)
            local rel = (px - trackF.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, trackF.AbsoluteSize.X)
            lastValue = apply(min + math.clamp(rel, 0, 1) * (max - min), false)
        end
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(trackF, "InputBegan"), function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging = true
                fromX(input.Position.X)
                local changedConn
                changedConn = SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "Changed"), function()
                    if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                        dragging = false
                        if changedConn then pcall(function() changedConn:Disconnect() end) end

                        apply(lastValue, true)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(input)
            if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                fromX(input.Position.X)
            end
        end)

        apply(getCurrentScale(fieldName, (min + max) / 2), false)
        return row
    end

    local function bodyRigTypeRow()
        local row = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 56),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,

        local function pill(text, xOffset, targetRig)
            local isActive = currentRigName == text
            local btn = New("TextButton", {
                BackgroundColor3 = isActive and accent or Palette.Element,
                BackgroundTransparency = isActive and 0.1 or 0.15,
                AutoButtonColor = false,
