                    setStatus(ok and ("Rig saved permanently to " .. text .. ".") or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
                    if ok and refreshBodyTools then refreshBodyTools() end
                end)
            end)
        end
        pill("R15", 10, Enum.HumanoidRigType.R15)
        pill("R6", 90, Enum.HumanoidRigType.R6)

        return row
    end

    local function showBodyTools()
        clearResults()
        setStatus("Body edits are purely local visuals, they don't change server data.", false)

        bodyButton("Apply Headless", "Hide head locally", function()
            local ok, err = setHeadless(true)
            if ok then
                rememberApplied({ key = "body:headless", kind = "headless", name = "Headless",
                    image = "rbxthumb://type=Asset&id=134082579&w=150&h=150" })
            end
            setStatus(ok and "Headless applied locally." or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
        end)

        bodyButton("Remove Headless", "Kembalikan kepala seperti semula", function()
            local ok, err = setHeadless(false)
            if ok then forgetAppliedKey("body:headless") end
            setStatus(ok and "Head restored." or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
        end)

        bodyButton("Apply Korblox Right Leg", "Local Korblox leg illusion", function()
            local ok, err = setKorbloxLike(true)
            if ok then
                rememberApplied({ key = "body:korblox", kind = "korblox", name = "Korblox Right Leg",
                    image = "rbxthumb://type=Asset&id=" .. tostring(KORBLOX_RIGHT_LEG_ASSET) .. "&w=150&h=150" })
            end
            setStatus(ok and "Korblox leg applied locally." or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
        end)

        bodyButton("Remove Korblox Right Leg", "Kembalikan kaki seperti semula", function()
            local ok, err = setKorbloxLike(false)
            if ok then forgetAppliedKey("body:korblox") end
            setStatus(ok and "Leg restored." or ("Failed: " .. tostring(err)), not ok)
        end)

    end
    refreshBodyTools = showBodyTools

    local function collectMyItems()
        local items = {}
        local character = getCharacter()
        if not character then return items end

        for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Accoutrement") then
                local fromTool = child:GetAttribute(LOCAL_GROUP_ATTRIBUTE)
                table.insert(items, {
                    Label = child.Name,
                    Sub = fromTool and ("Ditambah via tool • " .. tostring(fromTool)) or "Your original avatar items",
                    Remove = function() return pcall(function() child:Destroy() end) end,
                })
            end
        end

        local shirt = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Shirt")
        if shirt and shirt.ShirtTemplate ~= "" then
            table.insert(items, {
                Label = "Shirt Classic",
                Sub = "Classic shirt currently worn",
                Remove = function() return pcall(function() shirt.ShirtTemplate = "" end) end,
            })
        end

        local pants = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Pants")
        if pants and pants.PantsTemplate ~= "" then
            table.insert(items, {
                Label = "Pants Classic",
                Sub = "Classic pants currently worn",
                Remove = function() return pcall(function() pants.PantsTemplate = "" end) end,
            })
        end

        return items
    end

    showApplied = function()
        clearResults()

        for _, key in ipairs(appliedOrder) do
            local item = appliedItems[key]
            if item then appliedCard(item) end
        end

    local function applyPriceCreatorFilters(p)
        local minTxt = minPriceBox and minPriceBox.Text or ""
        local maxTxt = maxPriceBox and maxPriceBox.Text or ""
        local creatorTxt = creatorBox and creatorBox.Text or ""

        local minVal = tonumber(minTxt)
        if minVal then pcall(function() p.MinPrice = math.max(0, math.floor(minVal)) end) end

        local maxVal = tonumber(maxTxt)
        if maxVal then pcall(function() p.MaxPrice = math.max(0, math.floor(maxVal)) end) end

        creatorTxt = creatorTxt:gsub("^%s+", ""):gsub("%s+$", "")
        if creatorTxt ~= "" then pcall(function() p.CreatorName = creatorTxt end) end

        local sortOpt = filterCtl.GetSort and filterCtl.GetSort()
        if sortOpt then
            local val = ResolveEnumValue(Enum.CatalogSortType, sortOpt.names)
            if val then pcall(function() p.SortType = val end) end
        end

        local creatorTypeOpt = filterCtl.GetCreatorType and filterCtl.GetCreatorType()
        if creatorTypeOpt and #creatorTypeOpt.names > 0 then
            local val = ResolveEnumValue(Enum.CatalogCreatorType, creatorTypeOpt.names)
            if val then pcall(function() p.CreatorType = val end) end
        end

        if filterCtl.GetOffSale then
            pcall(function() p.IncludeOffSale = filterCtl.GetOffSale() end)
        end
    end

    local function loadFeatured()
        if selectedTab.mode ~= "accessory" and selectedTab.mode ~= "single" then return end
        if #selectedTab.assetTypes == 0 then return end
        if not AvatarEditorService then
            setStatus("AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor.", true)
            return
        end

        totalLoaded = 0
        _acRetries  = 0
        _acLastCall = 0
        setStatus("Loading featured items " .. (selectedTab.label or "") .. "...", false)
        clearResults()
        activeHolder = nil
        loadingMore  = false
        currentPages = nil

        task.spawn(function()

            task.wait(0.15)
            local okParams, params = pcall(function()
                local p = CatalogSearchParams.new()
                p.AssetTypes = selectedTab.assetTypes

                local ok1 = pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.Featured end)
                if not ok1 then
                    pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.MostFavorited end)
                end
                applyPriceCreatorFilters(p)
                return p
            end)
            if not okParams then
                setStatus("Failed to build parameters: " .. tostring(params), true)
                return
            end

            local okSearch, pages = pcall(function() TryElevateIdentity(); return AvatarEditorService:SearchCatalog(params) end)
            if not okSearch or not pages then
                setStatus("Failed to load featured items. Try searching manually above.", true)
                return
            end

            currentPages = pages
            local okPage, page = pcall(function() return pages:GetCurrentPage() end)
            if okPage and page and #page > 0 then
                renderPage(page)
                totalLoaded = #page
                setStatus("✨ " .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " featured items " .. (selectedTab.label or "") .. "  •  scroll / Load More untuk lanjut", false)
            else
                setStatus("No featured items. Try searching manually.", false)
            end
            _acLastCall = os.clock()
            updateLoadMoreBtn()
        end)
    end

    local function doSearch()
        if selectedTab.mode == "body" then showBodyTools() return end
        if selectedTab.mode == "applied" then showApplied() return end

        local query = searchBox.Text
        if query:gsub("%s+", "") == "" then

            loadFeatured()
            return
        end
        if #selectedTab.assetTypes == 0 then
            setStatus("This tab isn't supported on this client.", true)
            return
        end
        if not AvatarEditorService then
            setStatus("AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor.", true)
            return
        end

        totalLoaded = 0
        _acRetries  = 0
        _acLastCall = 0
        setStatus("Searching «" .. query .. "»...", false)
        clearResults()
        activeHolder = nil
        loadingMore  = false
        currentPages = nil

        task.spawn(function()
            local okParams, params = pcall(function()
                local p = CatalogSearchParams.new()
                p.SearchKeyword = query
                p.AssetTypes = selectedTab.assetTypes

                pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.Relevance end)
                applyPriceCreatorFilters(p)

                return p
            end)
            if not okParams then
                setStatus("Failed to build search parameters: " .. tostring(params), true)
                return
            end

            local okSearch, pages = pcall(function() TryElevateIdentity(); return AvatarEditorService:SearchCatalog(params) end)
            if not okSearch or not pages then
                currentPages = nil
                setStatus("Search failed: " .. tostring(pages), true)
                return
            end

            currentPages = pages
            _acLastCall  = os.clock()
            local okPage, page = pcall(function() return pages:GetCurrentPage() end)
            if okPage and page then
                renderPage(page)
                totalLoaded = #page
                setStatus("Result: " .. tostring(totalLoaded) .. " items  •  scroll / Load More for more", false)
            else
                setStatus("Failed to read search results.", true)
            end
            updateLoadMoreBtn()
        end)
    end

    local function stylePills()
        for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
            local active = selectedTab.key == entry.Def.key
            Tween(entry.Frame, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                BackgroundColor3 = active and accent or Palette.Glass,
                BackgroundTransparency = active and 0.05 or 0.4,
            })
            Tween(entry.Label, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = active and Palette.Text or Palette.SubText })
            if entry.Stroke then
                Tween(entry.Stroke, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                    Transparency = active and 0.05 or 0.65,
                    Thickness = active and 1.5 or 1,
                })
            end
        end
    end

    local function selectSubTab(t)
        selectedTab = t
        stylePills()
        searchBox.PlaceholderText = t.placeholder
        local showSearch = t.mode ~= "body" and t.mode ~= "applied" and t.mode ~= "myitems"
        SafeSet(searchRow, "Visible", showSearch)

        totalLoaded = 0
        _acRetries  = 0
        _acLastCall = 0
        currentPages = nil
        loadingMore  = false
        activeHolder = nil
        if loadMoreBtn then pcall(function() loadMoreBtn.Visible = false end) end

        if t.mode == "body" then
            showBodyTools()
        elseif t.mode == "applied" then
            showApplied()
        elseif t.mode == "myitems" then
            showMyItems()
        elseif t.mode == "accessory" or t.mode == "single" then

            clearResults()
            setStatus("Loading featured " .. t.label .. "...", false)
            task.spawn(function()
                task.wait(0.2)
                loadFeatured()
            end)
        else
            clearResults()
            setStatus("Search " .. t.label .. " then apply locally.", false)
        end
    end

    for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(entry.Frame, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            selectSubTab(entry.Def)
        end)
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), doSearch)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(filterApplyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), doSearch)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minPriceBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(maxPriceBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(creatorBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)

    loadMoreBtn = New("TextButton", {
        BackgroundColor3 = accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "↓ Load More",
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextSize = 10,
        Visible = false,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(loadMoreBtn, 12)
    local lmbStroke = Stroke(loadMoreBtn, accent, 1, 0.4)
    AddButtonHover(loadMoreBtn, lmbStroke)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(loadMoreBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        loadMore()
    end)

    SafeConnect(resultsFrame:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CanvasPosition"), function()
        local maxScroll = resultsFrame.CanvasSize.Y.Offset - resultsFrame.AbsoluteWindowSize.Y
        if maxScroll > 0 and resultsFrame.CanvasPosition.Y >= maxScroll - 180 then
            loadMore()
        end
    end)

    local function reapplyAll()
        if reapplying then return end
        reapplying = true
        hiddenState = {}
        faceState = nil

        task.wait(1)
        getHumanoid()

        local applied = 0
        for _, key in ipairs(appliedOrder) do
            local item = appliedItems[key]
            if item then
                local ok = applyStoredItem(item)
                if ok then applied = applied + 1 end
                task.wait(0.08)
            end
        end

        reapplying = false
        if applied > 0 then
            setStatus("Diterapkan ulang " .. tostring(applied) .. " items after respawn.", false)
        end
    end

    if LocalPlayer then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(LocalPlayer, "CharacterAdded"), function()

            task.spawn(function()
                task.wait(0.5)
                captureOriginalDescription()
                reapplyAll()
            end)
        end)
    end

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(0.5)
        reapplyAll()
    end)

    stylePills()
    selectSubTab(SUB_TABS[1])

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(0.4)
        loadFeatured()
    end)
end

local function BuildAnimationsTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Animation"]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local AvatarEditorService = SafeService("AvatarEditorService")

    local AnimConfig = {
        favorites  = {},
        lastBundle = nil,
        lastBundleName = nil,
        speed      = 1,
        autoLoad   = true,
        emoteSpeed = 1,
        emoteHold  = false,
    }

    -- Config & cache animasi sekarang di section "animationsConfig" dan
    -- "animationsCache" pada file JSON gabungan JEYHUB/data.json --
    -- bukan config.json/anims_cache.json terpisah lagi.
    local function saveAnimConfig()
        JD_Set("animationsConfig", AnimConfig)
    end

    local function loadAnimConfig()
        local data = JD_Get("animationsConfig", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then return end

        AnimConfig.favorites  = (type(data.favorites) == "table") and data.favorites or {}
        AnimConfig.lastBundle = data.lastBundle
        AnimConfig.lastBundleName = data.lastBundleName
        AnimConfig.stateOverrides = (type(data.stateOverrides) == "table") and data.stateOverrides or {}
        AnimConfig.speed      = tonumber(data.speed) or 1
        AnimConfig.emoteSpeed = tonumber(data.emoteSpeed) or 1
        if type(data.autoLoad) == "boolean" then AnimConfig.autoLoad = data.autoLoad end
        if type(data.emoteHold) == "boolean" then AnimConfig.emoteHold = data.emoteHold end
    end
    loadAnimConfig()

    local resolveCache = {}
    local needResaveCache = false
    do
        local d = JD_Get("animationsCache", nil)
        if type(d) == "table" then
            resolveCache = d

            local cleaned = 0
            for bundleKey, entry in pairs(resolveCache) do
                if type(entry) == "table" then
                    local hasIdle = entry["IdleAnimation"] ~= nil
                    local hasMovement = entry["WalkAnimation"] ~= nil or entry["RunAnimation"] ~= nil
                    if not (hasIdle and hasMovement) then
                        resolveCache[bundleKey] = nil
                        cleaned = cleaned + 1
                    end
                end
            end
            if cleaned > 0 then
                warn("[JEYHUB] Cleaned up " .. cleaned .. " old incomplete animation cache, will be re-resolved when used.")
                needResaveCache = true
            end
        end
    end
    local function saveAnimsCache()
        JD_Set("animationsCache", resolveCache)
    end
    if needResaveCache then saveAnimsCache() end

    local ANIM_ASSET_TYPES = {
        IdleAnimation = true, WalkAnimation = true, RunAnimation = true,
        JumpAnimation = true, FallAnimation = true, ClimbAnimation = true, SwimAnimation = true,
    }

    local STATE_ORDER = { "all", "idle", "walk", "run", "jump", "fall", "climb", "swim" }
    local STATE_LABELS = {
        all = "All (default)", idle = "Idle", walk = "Walk", run = "Run",
        jump = "Jump", fall = "Fall", climb = "Climb", swim = "Swim",
    }
    local STATE_ASSET_TYPE = {
        idle = "IdleAnimation", walk = "WalkAnimation", run = "RunAnimation",
        jump = "JumpAnimation", fall = "FallAnimation", climb = "ClimbAnimation", swim = "SwimAnimation",
    }
    local STATE_PREF_NAME = { idle = "Animation1" }
    local RESOLVE_PRIORITY = {
        IdleAnimation = 1, WalkAnimation = 2, RunAnimation = 3,
        JumpAnimation = 4, FallAnimation = 5, ClimbAnimation = 6, SwimAnimation = 7,
    }
    local ESSENTIAL_TYPES = { IdleAnimation = true, WalkAnimation = true, RunAnimation = true }

    local detailsCache = {}
    local function getBundleDetails(bundleId)
        if detailsCache[bundleId] then return detailsCache[bundleId] end
        if not AvatarEditorService then return nil end
        local ok, res = pcall(function()
            return AvatarEditorService:GetItemDetails(bundleId, Enum.AvatarItemType.Bundle)
        end)
        if ok and res then
            detailsCache[bundleId] = res
            return res
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function isResolved(bundleId) return resolveCache[tostring(bundleId)] ~= nil end

    local function resolveBundle(bundleId, onProgress, onEssential)
        local key = tostring(bundleId)
        if resolveCache[key] then return resolveCache[key], detailsCache[bundleId] end
        local res = getBundleDetails(bundleId)
        if not res or not res.BundledItems then return nil end

        local jobs = {}
        for _, item in ipairs(res.BundledItems) do
            local at = tostring(item.AssetType)
            if ANIM_ASSET_TYPES[at] and item.Id then
                jobs[#jobs + 1] = { at = at, id = item.Id }
            end
        end
        table.sort(jobs, function(a, b) return (RESOLVE_PRIORITY[a.at] or 99) < (RESOLVE_PRIORITY[b.at] or 99) end)

        local lastEssential = 0
        for idx, j in ipairs(jobs) do
            if ESSENTIAL_TYPES[j.at] then lastEssential = idx end
        end

        local resolved = {}
        for i, j in ipairs(jobs) do

            local ok, objs
            for attempt = 1, 3 do
                ok, objs = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. j.id) end)
                if ok and objs and #objs > 0 then break end
                if attempt < 3 then task.wait(0.3 * attempt) end
            end
            if ok and objs then
                local inner = {}
                for _, o in ipairs(objs) do
                    for _, c in ipairs(o:GetDescendants()) do
                        if c:IsA("Animation") then inner[c.Name] = c.AnimationId end
                    end
                end
                if next(inner) then resolved[j.at] = inner end
            end
            if onProgress then pcall(onProgress, i, #jobs) end
            if i == lastEssential and onEssential and next(resolved) then
                pcall(onEssential, resolved)
            end
            task.wait()
        end

        local hasIdle = resolved["IdleAnimation"] ~= nil
        local hasMovement = resolved["WalkAnimation"] ~= nil or resolved["RunAnimation"] ~= nil
        local isComplete = hasIdle and hasMovement
        if next(resolved) and isComplete then
            resolveCache[key] = resolved
            saveAnimsCache()
            return resolved, res
        end
        return nil, res
    end

    local ctrl = { token = 0, conns = {}, tracks = {}, current = nil, pose = "Standing", speedMul = tonumber(AnimConfig.speed) or 1, curBase = 1 }

    local function refreshSpeed()
        if ctrl.current and ctrl.curBase then
            pcall(function() ctrl.current:AdjustSpeed(ctrl.curBase * (ctrl.speedMul or 1)) end)
        end
    end

    local function stopController()
        ctrl.token = ctrl.token + 1
        for _, c in ipairs(ctrl.conns) do pcall(function() c:Disconnect() end) end
        ctrl.conns = {}
        for _, t in pairs(ctrl.tracks) do pcall(function() t:Stop(0) end) end
        ctrl.tracks = {}
        ctrl.current = nil
    end

    local function pickId(resolved, assetType, prefName)
        local inner = resolved[assetType]
        if not inner then return nil end
        local id = prefName and inner[prefName]
        if not id then for _, v in pairs(inner) do id = v; break end end
        return id
    end

    local function makeTrack(animator, id, priority, looped)
        if not id then return nil end
        local num = tostring(id):match("%d+")
        if not num then return nil end
        local a = Instance.new("Animation")
        a.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. num
        local ok, tr = pcall(function() return animator:LoadAnimation(a) end)
        if not ok or not tr then return nil end
        tr.Looped = (looped ~= false)
        tr.Priority = priority or Enum.AnimationPriority.Core
        return tr
    end

    local function isCharacterR6(char)
        if not char then return false end
        if char:FindFirstChild("RightUpperLeg") then return false end
        if char:FindFirstChild("Right Leg") then return true end
        local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        return hum ~= nil and hum.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.R6
    end

    local function buildController(char, resolved)
        stopController()
        local myToken = ctrl.token
        local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not hum then return false end
        local animator = hum:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
        if not animator then return false end

        local animate = char:FindFirstChild("Animate")
        if animate then animate.Disabled = true end
        for _, t in ipairs(animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do pcall(function() t:Stop(0) end) end

        local P = Enum.AnimationPriority
        local T = {
            idle     = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "IdleAnimation", "Animation1"), P.Idle),
            walk     = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "WalkAnimation"),  P.Movement),
            run      = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "RunAnimation"),   P.Movement),
            jump     = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "JumpAnimation"),  P.Action, false),
            fall     = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "FallAnimation"),  P.Action),
            climb    = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "ClimbAnimation"), P.Movement),
            swim     = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "SwimAnimation", "Swim"),     P.Movement),
            swimidle = makeTrack(animator, pickId(resolved, "SwimAnimation", "SwimIdle"), P.Idle),
        }
        ctrl.tracks = T

        local REF = 16
        local builtinEmoteTrack = nil

        local function play(track, fade, speed)
            if not track then return end
            if ctrl.current ~= track then
                if ctrl.current then pcall(function() ctrl.current:Stop(fade or 0.15) end) end
                ctrl.current = track
                pcall(function() track:Play(fade or 0.15) end)
            end
            if speed then
                ctrl.curBase = speed
                pcall(function() track:AdjustSpeed(speed * (ctrl.speedMul or 1)) end)
            end
        end

        local function stopBuiltinEmote(fade)
            if builtinEmoteTrack then
                local e = builtinEmoteTrack; builtinEmoteTrack = nil
                pcall(function() e:Stop(fade or 0.2) end)
            end
        end

        local function planarSpeed()
            local root = hum.RootPart
            if not root then return 0 end
            local v = root.AssemblyLinearVelocity
            return Vector3.new(v.X, 0, v.Z).Magnitude
        end

        local function onRunning(speed)
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            if speed > 0.5 then
                if builtinEmoteTrack then stopBuiltinEmote(0.1) end
                ctrl.pose = "Running"
                local mv = (speed > 9 and T.run) or T.walk or T.run
                play(mv, 0.15, speed / REF)
            elseif builtinEmoteTrack then
                return
            elseif ctrl.pose ~= "Jumping" and ctrl.pose ~= "FreeFall" then
                ctrl.pose = "Standing"
                play(T.idle, 0.2, 1)
            end
        end

        local function onJump()
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            stopBuiltinEmote(0.1)
            ctrl.pose = "Jumping"; play(T.jump or T.fall, 0.1, 1)
        end
        local function onFall(active)
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            if active then
                stopBuiltinEmote(0.1)
                ctrl.pose = "FreeFall"; play(T.fall or T.jump, 0.25, 1)
            else
                ctrl.pose = "Landed"
                onRunning(planarSpeed())
            end
        end
        local function onClimb(speed)
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            stopBuiltinEmote(0.1)
            ctrl.pose = "Climbing"
            play(T.climb, 0.15, speed / 5)
        end
        local function onSwim(speed)
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            ctrl.pose = "Swimming"
            if math.abs(speed or 0) > 1 then play(T.swim, 0.2, 1) else play(T.swimidle or T.swim, 0.2, 1) end
        end

        local function emotePlayableId(raw)
            local id
            if typeof(raw) == "Instance" and raw:IsA("Animation") then
                id = raw.AnimationId:match("%d+")
            elseif type(raw) == "string" and animate and not tonumber(raw) then
                local f = animate:FindFirstChild(raw)
                if f then
                    local a = f:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animation")
                    if a then return a.AnimationId:match("%d+") end
                end
                return nil
            elseif tonumber(raw) then
                id = tostring(tonumber(raw))
            end
            if not id then return nil end
            local key = "e" .. id
            if resolveCache[key] then return resolveCache[key] end
            local good = false
            local test = Instance.new("Animation"); test.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. id
            local ok, tr = pcall(function() return animator:LoadAnimation(test) end)
            if ok and tr then
                for _ = 1, 8 do
                    if tr.Length > 0 then good = true break end
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
                pcall(function() tr:Destroy() end)
            end
            if good then resolveCache[key] = id; return id end
            local ok2, objs = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. id) end)
            if ok2 and objs then
                for _, o in ipairs(objs) do
                    for _, c in ipairs(o:GetDescendants()) do
                        if c:IsA("Animation") then
                            local rid = c.AnimationId:match("%d+")
                            if rid then resolveCache[key] = rid; saveAnimsCache(); return rid end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return id
        end

        local function playBuiltinEmote(raw)
            local id = emotePlayableId(raw)
            if not id then return false end
            stopBuiltinEmote(0)
            local a = Instance.new("Animation"); a.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. id
            local ok, tr = pcall(function() return animator:LoadAnimation(a) end)
            if not ok or not tr then return false end
            tr.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
            builtinEmoteTrack = tr
            if ctrl.current then pcall(function() ctrl.current:Stop(0.15) end) end
            ctrl.current = nil; ctrl.pose = "Emote"
            pcall(function() tr:Play(0.1) end)
            pcall(function()
                tr.Stopped:Once(function()
                    if builtinEmoteTrack == tr then
                        builtinEmoteTrack = nil
                        if myToken == ctrl.token then onRunning(planarSpeed()) end
                    end
                end)
            end)
            return true
        end

        if animate then
            local bf = animate:FindFirstChild("PlayEmote")
            if bf and bf:IsA("BindableFunction") then
                pcall(function() bf.OnInvoke = function(emote) return playBuiltinEmote(emote) end end)
            end
        end

        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Running"), onRunning))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Jumping"), onJump))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "FreeFalling"), onFall))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Climbing"), onClimb))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Swimming"), onSwim))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Seated"), function(active) if not active then onRunning(0) end end))
        table.insert(ctrl.conns, SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "StateChanged"), function(_, new)
            if myToken ~= ctrl.token then return end
            if new == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Landed
                or new == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running
                or new == Enum.HumanoidStateType.RunningNoPhysics then
                if ctrl.pose == "Jumping" or ctrl.pose == "FreeFall" then
                    ctrl.pose = "Landed"
                    onRunning(planarSpeed())
                end
            end
        end))

        play(T.idle, 0.2, 1)

        task.spawn(function()
            while myToken == ctrl.token do
                if animate and not animate.Disabled then animate.Disabled = true end
                local cur = ctrl.current
                if cur and cur.Looped and not cur.IsPlaying then pcall(function() cur:Play(0.1) end) end
                task.wait(0.4)
            end
        end)
        return true
    end

    local function detectCurrentAnimations(char)
        local detected = {}
        if not char then return detected end
        local animate = char:FindFirstChild("Animate")
        if not animate then return detected end

        local FOLDER_TO_ASSET = {
            idle = "IdleAnimation", walk = "WalkAnimation", run = "RunAnimation",
            jump = "JumpAnimation", fall = "FallAnimation", climb = "ClimbAnimation",
            swim = "SwimAnimation", swimidle = "SwimAnimation",
        }
        for _, child in ipairs(animate:GetChildren()) do
            local assetType = FOLDER_TO_ASSET[child.Name:lower()]
            if assetType then
                local ok = pcall(function()
                    for _, c in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                        if c:IsA("Animation") and c.AnimationId ~= "" then
                            detected[assetType] = detected[assetType] or {}
                            detected[assetType][c.Name] = c.AnimationId
                        end
                    end
                end)
                if not ok then end
            end
        end
        return detected
    end

    local detectedResolved = {}

    local defaultResolved = nil

    local allBundleName = AnimConfig.lastBundleName
    local allBundleId = AnimConfig.lastBundle
    local refreshStateRow

    local function getMergedResolved()
        local merged = {}
        for k, v in pairs(detectedResolved) do
            local copy = {}
            for k2, v2 in pairs(v) do copy[k2] = v2 end
            merged[k] = copy
        end
        if defaultResolved then
            for k, v in pairs(defaultResolved) do
                local copy = {}
                for k2, v2 in pairs(v) do copy[k2] = v2 end
                merged[k] = copy
            end
        end
        for stateKey, ov in pairs(AnimConfig.stateOverrides or {}) do
            local assetType = STATE_ASSET_TYPE[stateKey]
            if assetType and ov and ov.id then
                if assetType == "SwimAnimation" then
                    merged[assetType] = { Swim = ov.id, SwimIdle = ov.id }
                else
                    local pref = STATE_PREF_NAME[stateKey] or "Animation"
                    merged[assetType] = { [pref] = ov.id }
                end
            end
        end
        return merged
    end

    local function rebuildFromState()
        local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        if not char then return false end
        if isCharacterR6(char) then

            stopController()
            local animate = char:FindFirstChild("Animate")
            if animate then animate.Disabled = false end
            return false
        end
        local merged = getMergedResolved()
        if not next(merged) then return false end
        return buildController(char, merged)
    end

    local function refreshDetectedAndRebuild(char)
        detectedResolved = detectCurrentAnimations(char)
        rebuildFromState()
    end

    local function applyBundle(bundleId, onProgress, targetState)
        local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        if not char or not char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
            return false, "Character not found."
        end
        if isCharacterR6(char) then
            return false, "This animation bundle was made for the R15 rig. Applying it on R6 would make your pose stiff/broken, so it was cancelled automatically. Switch to R15 first in the Body tab if you want to use it."
        end
        targetState = targetState or "all"

        local resolved, res = resolveBundle(bundleId, onProgress, function(partial)
            if targetState == "all" then
                defaultResolved = partial
                rebuildFromState()
            end
        end)
        if not resolved then
            return false, "Failed to load bundle animation (ID: " .. tostring(bundleId) .. ")"
        end

        if targetState == "all" then
            defaultResolved = resolved
            if not rebuildFromState() then
                return false, "Failed to apply (no Animator)."
            end
            allBundleId = tostring(bundleId)
            allBundleName = (res and res.Name) or nil
            AnimConfig.lastBundle = tostring(bundleId)
            AnimConfig.lastBundleName = allBundleName
            saveAnimConfig()
            if refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
            return true, "Applied to all states: " .. (allBundleName or ("ID " .. bundleId))
        end

        local assetType = STATE_ASSET_TYPE[targetState]
        if not assetType then return false, "Unknown state: " .. tostring(targetState) end
        local id = pickId(resolved, assetType, STATE_PREF_NAME[targetState])
        if not id then
            return false, (STATE_LABELS[targetState] or targetState) .. " not available in this bundle."
        end
        AnimConfig.stateOverrides = AnimConfig.stateOverrides or {}
        AnimConfig.stateOverrides[targetState] = {
            id = tostring(id):match("%d+") or tostring(id),
            name = (res and res.Name) or ("ID " .. bundleId),
            bundleId = tostring(bundleId),
        }
        saveAnimConfig()
        if not rebuildFromState() then
            return false, "Failed to apply (no Animator)."
        end
        if refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
        return true, (STATE_LABELS[targetState] or targetState) .. " applied from: " .. ((res and res.Name) or ("ID " .. bundleId))
    end

    local function clearAllBundle()
        defaultResolved = nil
        allBundleName = nil
        allBundleId = nil
        AnimConfig.lastBundle = nil
        AnimConfig.lastBundleName = nil
        saveAnimConfig()
        rebuildFromState()
        if refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
        return true, "'All' bundle removed. Animations reverted to default/per-state overrides."
    end

    local function resetAnimations()
        stopController()
        local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        local animate = char and char:FindFirstChild("Animate")
        if animate then
            pcall(function() animate.Disabled = true; task.wait(0.1); animate.Disabled = false end)
        end
        AnimConfig.lastBundle = nil
        AnimConfig.lastBundleName = nil
        AnimConfig.stateOverrides = {}
        defaultResolved = nil
        allBundleName = nil
        allBundleId = nil
        saveAnimConfig()
        if refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
        return true, "Default animation restored."
    end

    local uiEmoteTrack, uiEmoteConn = nil, nil
    local function stopUserEmote()
        if uiEmoteConn then pcall(function() uiEmoteConn:Disconnect() end); uiEmoteConn = nil end
        if uiEmoteTrack then pcall(function() uiEmoteTrack:Stop(0.2) end); uiEmoteTrack = nil end
    end

    local function resolveEmoteId(rawId)
        local id = tostring(rawId):match("%d+")
        if not id then return nil end
        local ekey = "e" .. id
        if resolveCache[ekey] then return resolveCache[ekey] end
        local ok2, objs = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. id) end)
        if ok2 and objs then
            for _, o in ipairs(objs) do
                local nodes = { o }
                for _, c in ipairs(o:GetDescendants()) do nodes[#nodes + 1] = c end
                for _, c in ipairs(nodes) do
                    if c:IsA("Animation") then
                        local rid = c.AnimationId:match("%d+")
                        if rid then resolveCache[ekey] = rid; saveAnimsCache(); return rid end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        return id
    end

    local function applyEmote(rawId, name, noAutoStop)
        local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        local hum = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local animator = hum and hum:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
        if not animator then return false, "Character not found." end
        if isCharacterR6(char) then
            return false, "This catalog emote was made for the R15 rig and would break the pose on R6, so it was cancelled automatically."
        end
        local id = resolveEmoteId(rawId)
        if not id then return false, "Failed to load emote." end
        stopUserEmote()
        local a = Instance.new("Animation"); a.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. id
        local ok, tr = pcall(function() return animator:LoadAnimation(a) end)
        if not ok or not tr then return false, "Failed to load emote." end
        tr.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
        tr.Looped = true
        uiEmoteTrack = tr
        pcall(function() tr:Play(0.15) end)
        pcall(function() tr:AdjustSpeed(AnimConfig.emoteSpeed or 1) end)
        if not noAutoStop then
            uiEmoteConn = SafeConnect(GetSignal(hum, "Running"), function(speed)
                if not AnimConfig.emoteHold and speed and speed > 0.5 then stopUserEmote() end
            end)
        end
        return true, "Memutar emote: " .. (name or ("ID " .. id))
    end

    local function refreshEmoteSpeed()
        if uiEmoteTrack then pcall(function() uiEmoteTrack:AdjustSpeed(AnimConfig.emoteSpeed or 1) end) end
    end

    if LocalPlayer then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(LocalPlayer, "CharacterAdded"), function(char)
            task.spawn(function()
                pcall(function() char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10) end)
                task.wait(1)

                detectedResolved = detectCurrentAnimations(char)
                if AnimConfig.lastBundle then
                    applyBundle(tonumber(AnimConfig.lastBundle))
                else
                    rebuildFromState()
                end
            end)
        end)
    end

    local section = tab:CreateSection("Animations", "Change idle/walk/run/emote animations via official Roblox bundles")
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body
    if not body then return end

    local SUB_TABS = {
        { key = "bundle", label = "Bundles" },

            BackgroundTransparency = 1,

            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            Parent = pill,
        })

        AddButtonHover(pill, pillStroke, 0)

        pillButtons[t.key] = { Frame = pill, Label = pillLabel, Def = t, Stroke = pillStroke }
    end

    local zoomCtl, filterCtl, minPriceBox, maxPriceBox, creatorBox, filterApplyBtn
    do

            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X,

            Position = UDim2.new(1, -86, 0.5, -12),

            Parent = toolsCluster,

        zoomCtl = CreateGridZoomControl(toolsCluster, accent, 4)
        filterCtl = CreateCatalogFilterGear(toolsCluster, body, accent)
        minPriceBox    = filterCtl.MinPriceBox
        maxPriceBox    = filterCtl.MaxPriceBox
        creatorBox     = filterCtl.CreatorBox
        filterApplyBtn = filterCtl.ApplyBtn
    end

    local function applyPriceCreatorFilters(p)
        local minVal = tonumber(minPriceBox and minPriceBox.Text or "")
        if minVal then pcall(function() p.MinPrice = math.max(0, math.floor(minVal)) end) end

        local maxVal = tonumber(maxPriceBox and maxPriceBox.Text or "")
        if maxVal then pcall(function() p.MaxPrice = math.max(0, math.floor(maxVal)) end) end

        local creatorTxt = (creatorBox and creatorBox.Text or ""):gsub("^%s+", ""):gsub("%s+$", "")
        if creatorTxt ~= "" then pcall(function() p.CreatorName = creatorTxt end) end

        local sortOpt = filterCtl.GetSort and filterCtl.GetSort()
        if sortOpt then
            local val = ResolveEnumValue(Enum.CatalogSortType, sortOpt.names)
            if val then pcall(function() p.SortType = val end) end
        end

        local creatorTypeOpt = filterCtl.GetCreatorType and filterCtl.GetCreatorType()
        if creatorTypeOpt and #creatorTypeOpt.names > 0 then
            local val = ResolveEnumValue(Enum.CatalogCreatorType, creatorTypeOpt.names)
            if val then pcall(function() p.CreatorType = val end) end
        end

        if filterCtl.GetOffSale then
            pcall(function() p.IncludeOffSale = filterCtl.GetOffSale() end)
        end
    end

    local targetStateIndex = 1

    local stateDotsRow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = body,
    })
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal,

    local stateDots, dotStrokes = {}, {}
    for i, key in ipairs(STATE_ORDER) do
        local dot = New("TextButton", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.7,
            Text = "",
            Parent = stateDotsRow,
        })
        Round(dot, 5)
        local dotStroke = Stroke(dot, Palette.Text, 1.2, 1)
        stateDots[i] = dot
        dotStrokes[i] = dotStroke
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(dot, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            targetStateIndex = i
            refreshStateRow()
        end)
    end

    refreshStateRow = function()
        local key = currentTargetState()
        local label = STATE_LABELS[key] or key
        if key == "all" then
            if allBundleName or allBundleId then
                stateValueLabel.Text = label .. " • " .. tostring(allBundleName or "Bundle")
                    .. (allBundleId and (" [ID: " .. tostring(allBundleId) .. "]") or "")
            else
                stateValueLabel.Text = label
            end
            stateClearBtn.Visible = (allBundleName ~= nil or allBundleId ~= nil)
        else
            local ov = AnimConfig.stateOverrides and AnimConfig.stateOverrides[key]
            if ov then
                stateValueLabel.Text = label .. " • " .. tostring(ov.name)
                    .. (ov.id and (" [ID: " .. tostring(ov.id) .. "]") or "")
            else
                local assetType = STATE_ASSET_TYPE[key]
                local fromActiveBundle = assetType and defaultResolved and defaultResolved[assetType] and next(defaultResolved[assetType])
                local hasDetected = assetType and detectedResolved[assetType] and next(detectedResolved[assetType])
                if fromActiveBundle and allBundleName then
                    stateValueLabel.Text = label .. " • from Bundle: " .. tostring(allBundleName)
                elseif hasDetected then
                    stateValueLabel.Text = label .. " • Bawaan Roblox (terdeteksi)"
                else
                    stateValueLabel.Text = label .. " • empty"
                end
            end
            stateClearBtn.Visible = ov ~= nil
        end

        if stateDots then
            for i, dot in ipairs(stateDots) do
                local dotKey = STATE_ORDER[i]
                local filled
                if dotKey == "all" then
                    filled = (allBundleName ~= nil or allBundleId ~= nil)
                else
                    filled = (AnimConfig.stateOverrides and AnimConfig.stateOverrides[dotKey]) ~= nil
                end
                dot.BackgroundColor3 = filled and accent or Palette.SubText
                dot.BackgroundTransparency = filled and 0.1 or 0.7
                if dotStrokes[i] then
                    dotStrokes[i].Transparency = (i == targetStateIndex) and 0 or 1
                end
            end
        end
    end

    do
        local initChar = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        if initChar then
            detectedResolved = detectCurrentAnimations(initChar)
        end
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(stateLeftBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        targetStateIndex = targetStateIndex - 1
        if targetStateIndex < 1 then targetStateIndex = #STATE_ORDER end
        refreshStateRow()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(stateRightBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        targetStateIndex = targetStateIndex + 1
        if targetStateIndex > #STATE_ORDER then targetStateIndex = 1 end
        refreshStateRow()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(stateClearBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        local key = currentTargetState()
        if key == "all" then
            local ok, msg = clearAllBundle()
            setStatus(msg, not ok)
            return
        end
        if not AnimConfig.stateOverrides then return end
        AnimConfig.stateOverrides[key] = nil
        saveAnimConfig()
        if rebuildFromState then rebuildFromState() end
        refreshStateRow()
        setStatus(STATE_LABELS[key] .. " reverted to default.", false)
    end)
    refreshStateRow()

    local function buildSliderRow(labelText, getValue, onChange)
        local row = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40), BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = settingsPanel })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, Text = labelText, TextColor3 = Palette.Text, TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, Parent = row,
        })
        local valueLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, Position = UDim2.new(1, -56, 0, 0), Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, Text = "1.00x", TextColor3 = accent, TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right, Parent = row,
        })
        local trackF = New("TextButton", {
            AutoButtonColor = false, Text = "",
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 22), Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 6),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass, Parent = row,
        })
        Round(trackF, 3)
        local fill = New("Frame", { BackgroundColor3 = accent, Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0), Parent = trackF })
        Round(fill, 3)
        local knob = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5), Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0), BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Text, ZIndex = 2, Parent = trackF,
        })
        Round(knob, 6)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1), Color3.new(0.82,0.82,0.85)),
            Rotation = 90,
            Parent = knob,
        })

        local SPD_MIN, SPD_MAX = 0.25, 3
        local function apply(v, save)
            v = math.clamp(v, SPD_MIN, SPD_MAX)
            v = math.floor(v * 100 + 0.5) / 100
            local frac = (v - SPD_MIN) / (SPD_MAX - SPD_MIN)
            SafeSet(fill, "Size", UDim2.new(frac, 0, 1, 0))
            SafeSet(knob, "Position", UDim2.new(frac, 0, 0.5, 0))
            valueLabel.Text = string.format("%.2fx", v)
            onChange(v, save)
        end

        local dragging = false
        local function fromX(px)
            local rel = (px - trackF.AbsolutePosition.X) / math.max(1, trackF.AbsoluteSize.X)
            apply(SPD_MIN + math.clamp(rel, 0, 1) * (SPD_MAX - SPD_MIN), true)
        end
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(trackF, "InputBegan"), function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging = true
                fromX(input.Position.X)
                local changedConn
                changedConn = SafeConnect(GetSignal(input, "Changed"), function()
                    if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                        dragging = false
                        if changedConn then pcall(function() changedConn:Disconnect() end) end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(UserInputService, "InputChanged"), function(input)
            if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                fromX(input.Position.X)
            end
        end)
        apply(getValue(), false)
    end

    local function buildToggleRow(labelText, getValue, onToggle)
        local row = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24), BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = settingsPanel })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, Size = UDim2.new(1, -54, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, Text = labelText, TextColor3 = Palette.Text, TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, Parent = row,
        })
        local tgl = New("TextButton", {
            AutoButtonColor = false, Text = "",
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0), Position = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 20), BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass, Parent = row,
        })
        Round(tgl, 10)
        local knob = New("Frame", {
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0.5), Size = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 16),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, 0), BackgroundColor3 = Palette.SubText, Parent = tgl,
        })
        Round(knob, 8)
        local function render()
            local on = getValue() and true or false
            Tween(tgl, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = on and accent or Palette.Glass })
            Tween(knob, 0.12, nil, nil, {
                Position = on and UDim2.new(1, -18, 0.5, 0) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, 0),
                BackgroundColor3 = on and Palette.Text or Palette.SubText,
            })
        end
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(tgl, "MouseButton1Click"), function() onToggle(); render() end)
        render()
    end

    local function newCardsHolder()
        local holder = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
