    local function isFav(id) return AnimConfig.favorites[tostring(id)] ~= nil end

    local function formatItemPrice(item)
        local price = item.Price or item.LowestPrice
        if item.IsForSale == false and not price then
            return "Off-Sale"
        end
        if price == nil then return "—" end
        if type(price) ~= "number" then return tostring(price) end
        if price <= 0 then return "Gratis" end
        return "R$ " .. tostring(price)
    end

    local function buildMetaRow(item, parent, y)
        local metaRow = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, y),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 14),
            Parent = parent,
        })

        local priceStr = formatItemPrice(item)
        local hasRobux = priceStr:sub(1, 2) == "R$"
        local priceValueText = hasRobux and priceStr:gsub("^R%$%s*", "") or priceStr

        if hasRobux then
            New("ImageLabel", {
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 1),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 11, 0, 11),
                Image = "rbxasset://textures/icon_ROBUX.png",
                ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit,
                Parent = metaRow,
            })
        end

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, hasRobux and 14 or 0, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0.5, hasRobux and -14 or 0, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = priceValueText,
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            Parent = metaRow,
        })

        local isVerified = item.CreatorHasVerifiedBadge == true
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0.5, isVerified and -14 or 0, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = tostring(item.CreatorName or "?"),
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 8,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center,
            Parent = metaRow,
        })

        if isVerified then
            local badge = New("Frame", {
                BackgroundColor3 = accent,
                Position = UDim2.new(1, -11, 0, 1),
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 11, 0, 11),
                Parent = metaRow,
            })
            Round(badge, 6)
            New("TextLabel", {
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
                Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
                Text = "✓",
                TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
                TextSize = 8,
                Parent = badge,
            })
        end
    end

    local function catalogCard(item, kind, holder)
        local id = tostring(item.Id)
        local card = New("Frame", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            Parent = holder,
        })
        Round(card, 12)
        local cardStroke = Stroke(card, accent, 1, 0.7)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 100,
            Parent = card,
        })
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseEnter"), function()
            Tween(card, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.12 })
            Tween(cardStroke, 0.12, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.35 })
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseLeave"), function()
            Tween(card, 0.18, nil, nil, { BackgroundTransparency = 0.25 })
            Tween(cardStroke, 0.18, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.7 })
        end)

        local thumbUrl = kind == "emote"
            and ("rbxthumb://type=Asset&id=%s&w=150&h=150"):format(id)
            or ("rbxthumb://type=BundleThumbnail&id=%s&w=150&h=150"):format(id)

        local thumb = New("ImageLabel", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 62),
            ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit,
            Parent = card,
        })
        LoadThumbnail(thumb, thumbUrl)
        Round(thumb, 8)

        local starBtn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 6),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = isFav(id) and "★" or "☆",
            TextColor3 = isFav(id) and accent or Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 11,
            ZIndex = 3,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(starBtn, 7)
        local starStroke = Stroke(starBtn, accent, 1, isFav(id) and 0.3 or 0.85)
        AddButtonHover(starBtn)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(starBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            if isFav(id) then
                AnimConfig.favorites[id] = nil
                starBtn.Text = "☆"; starBtn.TextColor3 = Palette.SubText
                Tween(starStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.85 })
            else
                AnimConfig.favorites[id] = { name = item.Name or (kind .. " " .. id), kind = kind }
                starBtn.Text = "★"; starBtn.TextColor3 = accent
                Tween(starStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.3 })
            end
            saveAnimConfig()
        end)

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 70),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = item.Name or ((kind == "emote" and "Emote " or "Bundle ") .. id),
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 9,
            TextWrapped = true,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
            Parent = card,
        })

        buildMetaRow(item, card, 88)

        local applyBtn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 105),
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 18),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = kind == "emote" and "Play" or "Apply",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 9,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(applyBtn, 7)
        AddButtonHover(applyBtn)

        SafeConnect(GetSignal(applyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            local targetState = currentTargetState()
            if kind == "emote" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    if targetState == "all" then
                        setStatus("Memutar emote...", false)
                        local ok, msg = applyEmote(tonumber(id), item.Name)
                        setStatus(msg, not ok)
                        return
                    end

                    setStatus("Applying to " .. (STATE_LABELS[targetState] or targetState) .. ": " .. tostring(item.Name or id), false)
                    local rid = resolveEmoteId(id)
                    if not rid then
                        setStatus("Failed to load animation.", true)
                        return
                    end
                    AnimConfig.stateOverrides = AnimConfig.stateOverrides or {}
                    AnimConfig.stateOverrides[targetState] = {
                        id = tostring(rid):match("%d+") or tostring(rid),
                        name = item.Name or ("Emote " .. tostring(id)),
                    }
                    saveAnimConfig()
                    local ok = rebuildFromState()
                    setStatus(ok and ((STATE_LABELS[targetState] or targetState) .. " applied from: " .. (item.Name or ("Emote " .. tostring(id))))
                        or "Failed to apply (no Animator).", not ok)
                    if ok and refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
                end)
            else
                task.spawn(function()
                    local firstTime = not isResolved(id)
                    setStatus(firstTime and "Loading animation for the first time (faster next time)..." or ("Applying to " .. (STATE_LABELS[targetState] or targetState) .. ": " .. tostring(item.Name or id)), false)
                    local ok, msg = applyBundle(tonumber(id), (firstTime and function(done, total)
                        setStatus(("Loading animation... %d/%d"):format(done, total), false)
                    end or nil), targetState)
                    setStatus(msg, not ok)
                    if ok and refreshStateRow then refreshStateRow() end
                end)
            end
        end)
    end

    local feeds = {
        bundle = { pages = nil, count = 0, activeHolder = nil, loadingMore = false, kind = "bundle" },
        emote  = { pages = nil, count = 0, activeHolder = nil, loadingMore = false, kind = "emote" },
    }
    local currentSubTab = "bundle"

    local function appendItems(feedName, items)
        local f = feeds[feedName]
        if not f.activeHolder then f.activeHolder = newCardsHolder() end
        for _, it in ipairs(items) do
            f.count = f.count + 1
            catalogCard({
                Id = it.Id, Name = it.Name,
                Price = it.Price, LowestPrice = it.LowestPrice,
                CreatorName = it.CreatorName, IsForSale = it.IsForSale,
                CreatorHasVerifiedBadge = it.CreatorHasVerifiedBadge,
            }, f.kind, f.activeHolder)
        end
    end

    local _animLastCall  = 0
    local _animRetries   = {}
    local _ANIM_MIN_GAP  = 0.7
    local _ANIM_BACKOFFS = { 1, 2, 4, 8 }
    local animLoadMoreBtns = {}

    local function updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
        local btn = animLoadMoreBtns[feedName]
        if not btn then return end
        local f = feeds[feedName]
        local okFin, fin = pcall(function() return f.pages and f.pages.IsFinished end)
        local done = okFin and fin
        pcall(function()
            btn.Visible = (f.pages ~= nil) and not done and (currentSubTab == feedName)
            btn.Text = f.loadingMore and "⏳ Loading..." or ("↓ Load More (" .. tostring(f.count) .. " items)")
        end)
    end

    local function loadMoreFeed(feedName)
        local f = feeds[feedName]
        if f.loadingMore or not f.pages then return end
        local okFin, fin = pcall(function() return f.pages.IsFinished end)
        if okFin and fin then
            setStatus("✓ All " .. tostring(f.count) .. " " .. (f.kind == "emote" and "emote" or "bundle") .. " sudah dimuat.", false)
            updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
            return
        end

        local now = os.clock()
        if now - _animLastCall < _ANIM_MIN_GAP then return end

        _animRetries[feedName] = _animRetries[feedName] or 0
        f.loadingMore = true
        updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
        setStatus("Loading more...", false)

        task.spawn(function()
            _animLastCall = os.clock()
            local okAdv, advErr = pcall(function() TryElevateIdentity(); f.pages:AdvanceToNextPageAsync() end)

            if not okAdv then

                _animRetries[feedName] = math.min(_animRetries[feedName] + 1, #_ANIM_BACKOFFS)
                local delay = _ANIM_BACKOFFS[_animRetries[feedName]]
                setStatus(("⚠ Rate limit! Retry in " .. delay .. "s..."), true)
                task.wait(delay)
                f.loadingMore = false
                _animLastCall = os.clock()
                updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
                if _animRetries[feedName] < #_ANIM_BACKOFFS then
                    loadMoreFeed(feedName)
                else
                    setStatus("✕ Failed after several retries. Try again manually.", true)
                    _animRetries[feedName] = 0
                end
                return
            end

            _animRetries[feedName] = 0
            local okPage, page = pcall(function() return f.pages:GetCurrentPage() end)
            f.loadingMore = false

            if okPage and page then
                appendItems(feedName, page)
                local okFin2, fin2 = pcall(function() return f.pages.IsFinished end)
                if okFin2 and fin2 then
                    setStatus("✓ All " .. tostring(f.count) .. " " .. (f.kind == "emote" and "emote" or "bundle") .. " dimuat.", false)
                else
                    setStatus(("%s loaded: %d  •  scroll / Load More to continue"):format(f.kind == "emote" and "Emotes" or "Bundles", f.count), false)
                end
            end
            updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
        end)
    end

    local function searchFeed(feedName, keyword)
        local f = feeds[feedName]

        f.pages, f.count, f.activeHolder, f.loadingMore = nil, 0, nil, false
        _animRetries[feedName] = 0
        _animLastCall = 0
        clearResults()

        for _, btn in pairs(animLoadMoreBtns) do
            pcall(function() btn.Visible = false end)
        end

        setStatus(keyword ~= "" and ("Searching «" .. keyword .. "»...") or ("✨ Memuat " .. (f.kind == "emote" and "emotes" or "bundles") .. " unggulan..."), false)

        if not AvatarEditorService then
            setStatus("AvatarEditorService is not available on this executor.", true)
            return
        end

        task.spawn(function()

            task.wait(0.15)
            local okParams, params = pcall(function()
                local p = CatalogSearchParams.new()
                if keyword and keyword ~= "" then
                    p.SearchKeyword = keyword
                    pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.Relevance end)
                else

                    local ok1 = pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.Featured end)
                    if not ok1 then
                        pcall(function() p.SortType = Enum.CatalogSortType.MostFavorited end)
                    end
                end
                if feedName == "emote" then
                    p.AssetTypes = { Enum.AvatarAssetType.EmoteAnimation }
                else
                    p.BundleTypes = { Enum.BundleType.Animations }
                end
                applyPriceCreatorFilters(p)

                return p
            end)
            if not okParams then
                setStatus("Failed to build search parameters.", true)
                return
            end
            local okSearch, pages = pcall(function() TryElevateIdentity(); return AvatarEditorService:SearchCatalog(params) end)
            if not okSearch or not pages then
                setStatus("Search failed (rate limit?). Wait a moment then try again.", true)
                return
            end
            f.pages = pages
            _animLastCall = os.clock()
            local okPage, page = pcall(function() return pages:GetCurrentPage() end)
            if okPage and page then
                appendItems(feedName, page)
                local label = keyword ~= "" and ("Result: " .. tostring(f.count)) or ("✨ Unggulan: " .. tostring(f.count))
                setStatus(label .. " " .. (f.kind == "emote" and "emote" or "bundle") .. "  •  scroll / Load More untuk lanjut", false)
            end
            updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
        end)
    end

    local function showFavorites()
        clearResults()
        local holder = newCardsHolder()
        local n = 0
        for id, v in pairs(AnimConfig.favorites) do
            local kind = (type(v) == "table" and v.kind) or "bundle"
            local name = (type(v) == "table" and v.name) or v
            if kind == favFilter then
                n = n + 1
                catalogCard({ Id = tonumber(id), Name = name }, kind, holder)
            end
        end
        setStatus(n == 0 and ("No favorites yet " .. favFilter .. ".") or ("Favorit " .. favFilter .. ": " .. n), n == 0)
    end

    local function renderFavFilterStyle()
        Tween(favBundleBtn, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = favFilter == "bundle" and accent or Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = favFilter == "bundle" and 0.1 or 0.3 })
        Tween(favEmoteBtn, 0.12, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = favFilter == "emote" and accent or Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = favFilter == "emote" and 0.1 or 0.3 })
    end

    local function stylePills()
        for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
            local active = currentSubTab == entry.Def.key
            Tween(entry.Frame, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                BackgroundColor3 = active and accent or Palette.Glass,
                BackgroundTransparency = active and 0.05 or 0.4,
            })
            Tween(entry.Label, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = active and Palette.Text or Palette.SubText })
            if entry.Stroke then
                Tween(entry.Stroke, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                    Transparency = active and 0.05 or 0.65,
                    Thickness = active and 1.5 or 1,
                })
            end
        end
    end

    local function selectSubTab(key)
        currentSubTab = key
        stylePills()
        local showSearch = key == "bundle" or key == "emote"
        SafeSet(searchRow, "Visible", showSearch)
        SafeSet(favFilterRow, "Visible", key == "favorites")
        SafeSet(resultsFrame, "Visible", key ~= "settings")
        SafeSet(settingsPanel, "Visible", key == "settings")

        for feedName in pairs(animLoadMoreBtns) do
            if feedName == key then
                updateAnimLoadBtn(feedName)
            else
                pcall(function() animLoadMoreBtns[feedName].Visible = false end)
            end
        end

        if key == "bundle" or key == "emote" then
            searchBox.PlaceholderText = key == "emote" and "Search emote, e.g.: dance" or "Search animation bundle, e.g.: ninja"

            if not feeds[key].pages then
                searchFeed(key, "")
            else

                clearResults()
                if feeds[key].activeHolder then
                    pcall(function() feeds[key].activeHolder.Parent = resultsFrame end)
                end
                setStatus(("✨ " .. tostring(feeds[key].count) .. " " .. (key == "emote" and "emote" or "bundle") .. " dimuat  •  scroll / Load More untuk lanjut"), false)
                updateAnimLoadBtn(key)
            end
        elseif key == "favorites" then
            renderFavFilterStyle()
            showFavorites()
        else
            clearResults()
        end
    end

    for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(entry.Frame, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            selectSubTab(entry.Def.key)
        end)
    end

    local function doSearch()
        if currentSubTab ~= "bundle" and currentSubTab ~= "emote" then return end
        searchFeed(currentSubTab, searchBox.Text or "")
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), doSearch)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(searchBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(filterApplyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), doSearch)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(minPriceBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(maxPriceBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(creatorBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then doSearch() end
    end)

    for _, feedName in ipairs({ "bundle", "emote" }) do
        local lmBtn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.25,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "↓ Load More",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 10,
            Visible = false,
            Parent = body,
        })
        Round(lmBtn, 12)
        local lmStroke = Stroke(lmBtn, accent, 1, 0.4)
        AddButtonHover(lmBtn, lmStroke)
        animLoadMoreBtns[feedName] = lmBtn
        local capturedFeed = feedName
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(lmBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            loadMoreFeed(capturedFeed)
        end)
    end

    local _origSelectSubTab = selectSubTab

    SafeConnect(resultsFrame:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CanvasPosition"), function()
        if currentSubTab ~= "bundle" and currentSubTab ~= "emote" then return end
        local maxScroll = resultsFrame.CanvasSize.Y.Offset - resultsFrame.AbsoluteWindowSize.Y
        if maxScroll > 0 and resultsFrame.CanvasPosition.Y >= maxScroll - 180 then
            loadMoreFeed(currentSubTab)
        end
    end)

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(favBundleBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        favFilter = "bundle"; renderFavFilterStyle(); showFavorites()
    end)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(favEmoteBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        favFilter = "emote"; renderFavFilterStyle(); showFavorites()
    end)

    stylePills()
    selectSubTab("bundle")

    if AnimConfig.autoLoad and AnimConfig.lastBundle then
        task.spawn(function()
            local ch = LocalPlayer and (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait())
            if ch then
                pcall(function() ch:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10) end)
                task.wait(0.5)

                applyBundle(tonumber(AnimConfig.lastBundle))
            end
        end)
    end
end

-- ================= LASER TAB =================
-- Tab khusus berisi 1 dropdown (Laser 1 - Laser 10), tiap pilihan
-- memutar SEPASANG animasi ID sekaligus lewat 2 AnimationTrack terpisah
-- dengan Priority.Action4 (prioritas tertinggi) supaya keduanya dominan
-- menimpa idle/walk/run bawaan dan TIDAK berhenti sendiri saat player
-- bergerak -- cuma berhenti kalau tombol Stop ditekan manual.
local function BuildLaserTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Laser"]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local LASER_PRESETS = {
        { label = "Laser 1",  ids = { "122319751392556", "70883871260184" } },
        { label = "Laser 2",  ids = { "70883871260184" } },
        { label = "Laser 3",  ids = { "70883871260184", "85902841486026" } },
        { label = "Laser 4",  ids = { "70883871260184", "77094699387328" } },
        { label = "Laser 5",  ids = { "70883871260184", "116701299898198" } },
        { label = "Laser 6",  ids = { "70883871260184", "95329943746305" } },
        { label = "Laser 7",  ids = { "70883871260184", "80083550897917" } },
        { label = "Laser 8",  ids = { "70883871260184", "137367412027854" } },
        { label = "Laser 9",  ids = { "70883871260184", "138672914995772" } },
        { label = "Laser 10", ids = { "11988902106015", "70883871260184" } },
        { label = "Laser 11", ids = { "124522818196151", "70883871260184" } },
        { label = "Laser 12", ids = { "70883871260184", "94569085531218", "14366558676" } },
        { label = "Laser 13", ids = { "70883871260184", "94569085531218" } },
        { label = "Laser 14", ids = { "94569085531218" } },
    }
    local section = tab:CreateSection("Laser Sync Engine", "Combine 2 combo slots (up to 4 animations) with independent speeds")
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body
    if not body then return end

    -- ============ Slot state (A & B) ============
    -- Tiap slot combo (A/B) punya preset, track, DAN speed sendiri-sendiri
    -- -- keduanya dimainkan BERSAMAAN saat Play ditekan, jadi bisa
    -- mengombinasikan sampai 4 animasi sekaligus (2 id combo A + 2 id
    -- combo B), masing-masing dengan kecepatan playback independen.
    local function NewLaserSlotState(defaultPreset)
        return {
            preset = defaultPreset,
            tracks = {},
            speed = 1,
            savedPositions = {},
            resumePresetRef = nil,
            isPlaying = false,
        }
    end
    local slotA = NewLaserSlotState(LASER_PRESETS[1])
    local slotB = NewLaserSlotState(LASER_PRESETS[2])

    -- Simpan TimePosition tiap animasi (key = AnimationId) pas tombol
    -- Stop ditekan, supaya kalau Play ditekan lagi buat SLOT COMBO YANG
    -- SAMA, animasinya lanjut dari detik terakhir itu -- bukan mulai
    -- ulang dari 0. `resumePresetRef` nyimpen referensi preset yang lagi
    -- "dipause" -- kalau kombo di slot itu diganti, referensinya otomatis
    -- beda dan resume ini otomatis diabaikan (mulai fresh buat combo baru).
    local function stopSlot(slot, keepPosition)
        if keepPosition then
            slot.resumePresetRef = slot.preset
            slot.savedPositions = {}
            for _, tr in ipairs(slot.tracks) do
                pcall(function()
                    local animId = tr.Animation and tr.Animation.AnimationId
                    if animId then slot.savedPositions[animId] = tr.TimePosition end
                end)
            end
        end
        for _, tr in ipairs(slot.tracks) do
            pcall(function() tr:Stop(0.15) end)
        end
        slot.tracks = {}
        slot.isPlaying = false
    end

    local function stopLaser(keepPosition)
        stopSlot(slotA, keepPosition)
        stopSlot(slotB, keepPosition)
    end

    -- Auto-stop kalau window utama/GUI script ini ke-close TANPA sengaja --
    -- baik lewat tombol X manual, atau script-nya sendiri di-unload/stop
    -- lewat executor (kebanyakan exploit client ikut men-Destroy semua
    -- Instance yang dibuat script saat di-unload). Instance.Destroying
    -- fire persis SEBELUM instance-nya benar-benar hilang -- ini sinyal
    -- paling reliable yang tersedia buat mendeteksi "window/script keluar"
    -- di lingkungan Roblox/executor manapun. false = jangan simpan posisi
    -- resume, karena window/script-nya sendiri sudah hilang, tidak ada
    -- lagi UI buat nge-resume nanti.
    if Window and Window.Gui then
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(Window.Gui, "Destroying"), function()
            stopLaser(false)
        end)
    end

    -- ============ Card 1: pemilih combo (2 dropdown -- Slot A & Slot B) ============
    local pickerCard = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 58),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(pickerCard, 18)
    Stroke(pickerCard, accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = pickerCard,
    })
    Pad(pickerCard, 14, 14, 12, 12)

    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "COMBO SLOTS (A + B)",
        TextColor3 = accent,
        TextSize = 10,
        LetterSpacing = 1.5,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Parent = pickerCard,
    })

    local statusLbl -- forward declare, dibuat di bawah (card status)

    -- Factory: bikin 1 dropdown combo-slot (dipakai 2x -- Slot A & Slot B).
    -- Semua state dropdown (open/close, floating list, posisi) jadi
    -- closure lokal per pemanggilan, jadi Slot A & Slot B independen
    -- total -- buka salah satu otomatis nutup yang lain (lewat
    -- CloseActiveFloatingPopup, sama seperti popup lain di script ini).
    local function CreateLaserDropdown(posX, sizeX, tag, slot, onSelect)
        local box = New("Frame", {
            Position = UDim2.new(posX, 0, 0, 18),
            Size = UDim2.new(sizeX, 0, 0, 26),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Element,
            Parent = pickerCard,
        })
        Round(box, 8)
        local stroke = Stroke(box, Palette.StrokeSoft, 1, 0.5)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 90,
            Parent = box,
        })

        local label = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -22, 1, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = tag .. ": " .. slot.preset.label,
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            Parent = box,
        })
        local arrow = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -16, 0, 0),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "v",
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 9,
            Parent = box,
        })
        local btn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Text = "",
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
            Parent = box,
        })
        AddButtonHover(btn, stroke)

        local listShadow = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 132, 0, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0),
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.55,
            ZIndex = 200,
            Parent = box,
        })
        Round(listShadow, 8)

        -- FIX: dulu Frame biasa + ClipsDescendants -- semua 13 preset di
        -- LASER_PRESETS langsung mengembang penuh (13*24=312px), bisa
        -- meluber keluar window. Sekarang ScrollingFrame beneran, sama
        -- persis polanya kayak CreateDropdown standar: cap tinggi 5 item
        -- (5*24=120), sisanya di-scroll pakai scrollbar tipis di pinggir.
        local list = New("ScrollingFrame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 132, 0, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.03,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            ScrollBarThickness = 3,
            ScrollBarImageColor3 = accent,
            CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, #LASER_PRESETS * 24),
            ZIndex = 201,
            Parent = box,
        })
        Round(list, 8)
        Stroke(list, accent, 1, 0.4)
        New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent = list })

        local listHomeParent = list.Parent
        local repositionConn = nil
        local function updateListPosition()
            local pos = box.AbsolutePosition
            local size = box.AbsoluteSize
            local layer, scaleObj = GetFloatingLayer(box:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui"))
            local s = (scaleObj and scaleObj.Scale) or UserUIScale
            if s <= 0 then s = 1 end
            -- Lebar list ngikutin lebar box ASLI (bukan fixed 132 kayak
            -- dulu) -- supaya pas walau box-nya sekarang scale-based
            -- (kira-kira setengah lebar card, bukan fixed penuh lagi
            -- kayak pas cuma ada 1 dropdown).
            local w = math.max(size.X, 110)
            list.Size = UDim2.new(0, w, 0, list.Size.Y.Offset)
            listShadow.Size = UDim2.new(0, w, 0, listShadow.Size.Y.Offset)
            -- FIX: dulu list di-parent LANGSUNG ke ScreenGui (bukan lewat
            -- GetFloatingLayer), jadi TIDAK IKUT mengecil/membesar sama
            -- sekali walau UI Scale di Settings diubah. Sekarang lewat
            -- floating layer yang sama dipakai CreateDropdown/ColorPicker
            -- -- posisinya dibagi scale layer (s) dulu, supaya abis
            -- dikali balik pas dirender, hasilnya PAS di posisi layar
            -- yang sama persis (bukan meleset kena scale dobel).
            list.Position = UDim2.new(0, pos.X / s, 0, (pos.Y + size.Y + 4) / s)
            listShadow.Position = UDim2.new(0, (pos.X - 1) / s, 0, (pos.Y + size.Y + 6) / s)
        end
        local function floatList()
            local screenGui = box:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("ScreenGui")
            if not screenGui then return end
            local layer = GetFloatingLayer(screenGui)
            if not layer then return end
            list.Parent = layer
            listShadow.Parent = layer
            updateListPosition()
            if repositionConn then pcall(function() repositionConn:Disconnect() end) end
            repositionConn = SafeConnect(box:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsolutePosition"), updateListPosition)
        end
        local function unfloatList()
            if repositionConn then
                pcall(function() repositionConn:Disconnect() end)
                repositionConn = nil
            end
            list.Parent = listHomeParent
            listShadow.Parent = listHomeParent
            list.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 4)
            listShadow.Position = UDim2.new(0, -1, 1, 6)
        end

        local isOpen = false
        local function closeList()
            isOpen = false
            Tween(list, 0.15, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, list.Size.X.Offset, 0, 0) })
            Tween(listShadow, 0.15, nil, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, listShadow.Size.X.Offset, 0, 0) })
            Tween(arrow, 0.15, nil, nil, { Rotation = 0 })
            task.delay(0.16, function()
                pcall(function()
                    if not isOpen then
                        box.ZIndex = 1
                        unfloatList()
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end

        local function selectPreset(preset)
            slot.preset = preset
            label.Text = tag .. ": " .. preset.label
            if onSelect then onSelect(preset) end
        end

        for _, preset in ipairs(LASER_PRESETS) do
            local item = New("TextButton", {
                Text = preset.label, Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, TextSize = 11,
                TextColor3 = Palette.Text, BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
                BackgroundTransparency = 0.05,
                Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24), ZIndex = 201,
                Parent = list,
            })
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseEnter"), function() Tween(item, 0.1, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.ElementHover }) end)
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseLeave"), function() Tween(item, 0.1, nil, nil, { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass }) end)
            SafeConnect(GetSignal(item, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
                selectPreset(preset)
                closeList()
            end)
        end

        local lastToggle = 0
        local function toggleList()
            if os.clock() - lastToggle < 0.1 then return end
            lastToggle = os.clock()

            isOpen = not isOpen
            if isOpen then
                CloseActiveFloatingPopup(closeList)
                RegisterFloatingPopup(closeList)
                box.ZIndex = 20
                floatList()
            end
            local w = list.Size.X.Offset
            -- Cap tinggi 5 item (5*24=120), sama persis kayak dropdown
            -- standar -- sisanya (13 preset Laser) tinggal di-scroll.
            local h = isOpen and math.min(#LASER_PRESETS * 24, 120) or 0
            list.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, #LASER_PRESETS * 24)
            Tween(list, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, w, 0, h) })
            Tween(listShadow, 0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Size = UDim2.new(0, w, 0, h) })
            Tween(arrow, 0.18, nil, nil, { Rotation = isOpen and 180 or 0 })
            if not isOpen then
                task.delay(0.16, function()
                    pcall(function()
                        if not isOpen then
                            box.ZIndex = 1
                            unfloatList()
                        end
                    end)
                end)
            end
        end
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(btn, "MouseButton1Click"), toggleList)

        return { box = box, closeList = closeList }
    end

    -- Kalau salah satu slot lagi jalan terus kombo-nya diganti, hentikan
    -- slot ITU SAJA (slot yang satunya tetap jalan tanpa terganggu) --
    -- resume-position slot ini juga dibersihkan karena kombo barunya
    -- beda, harus mulai fresh dari 0.
    local function onSlotChanged(slot, slotTag)
        if slot.isPlaying then
            stopSlot(slot, false)
            slot.resumePresetRef = nil
            slot.savedPositions = {}
            if statusLbl then
                statusLbl.Text = ("Slot %s stopped (switched combo) — press Play to run %s again."):format(slotTag, slot.preset.label)
                statusLbl.TextColor3 = Palette.SubText
            end
        end
    end

    CreateLaserDropdown(0, 0.48, "A", slotA, function() onSlotChanged(slotA, "A") end)
    CreateLaserDropdown(0.52, 0.48, "B", slotB, function() onSlotChanged(slotB, "B") end)

    -- ============ Speed slider Slot A & Slot B (0.1x - 10000x) ============
    -- Ditaruh lewat section:CreateSlider standar (bukan card custom)
    -- supaya otomatis dapat styling/hover yang sama dengan slider di
    -- tab lain. Callback langsung nge-adjust track SLOT-nya SENDIRI yang
    -- lagi jalan (kalau ada) pakai AdjustSpeed -- Slot A dan Slot B punya
    -- kecepatan yang benar-benar independen satu sama lain.
    section:CreateSlider({
        Title = "Playback Speed — Slot A",
        Subtitle = "Kecepatan animasi Slot A (0x - 100000x)",
        Min = 0, Max = 100000, Step = 0.1, Default = 1,
        Callback = function(value)
            slotA.speed = value
            for _, tr in ipairs(slotA.tracks) do
                pcall(function() tr:AdjustSpeed(slotA.speed) end)
            end
        end,
    })
    section:CreateSlider({
        Title = "Playback Speed — Slot B",
        Subtitle = "Kecepatan animasi Slot B (0x - 100000x)",
        Min = 0, Max = 100000, Step = 0.1, Default = 1,
        Callback = function(value)
            slotB.speed = value
            for _, tr in ipairs(slotB.tracks) do
                pcall(function() tr:AdjustSpeed(slotB.speed) end)
            end
        end,
    })

    -- ============ Card 2: kontrol Play / Stop ============
    local controlCard = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(controlCard, 18)
    Stroke(controlCard, accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    New("UIGradient", {
        Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
        Rotation = 90,
        Parent = controlCard,
    })
    New("UIListLayout", {
        FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal,
        Padding = UDim.new(0, 0),
        Parent = controlCard,
    })
    Pad(controlCard, 4, 4, 4, 4)

    local playBtn = New("TextButton", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "▶  Play",
        TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 235, 160),
        TextSize = 12,
        Parent = controlCard,
    })
    AddButtonHover(playBtn)

    local controlDivider = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 1, 1, -8),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.StrokeSoft,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.4,
        Parent = controlCard,
    })

    local stopBtn = New("TextButton", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "■  Stop",
        TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 120, 130),
        TextSize = 12,
        Parent = controlCard,
    })
    AddButtonHover(stopBtn)

    -- ============ Status row ============
    local statusRow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Parent = body,
    })
    statusLbl = New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        Text = "Idle — pick Slot A & Slot B above, then press Play.",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 9,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd,
        Parent = statusRow,
    })

    -- ============ Notice card ============
    local noticeCard = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 190, 60),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.88,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(noticeCard, 14)
    Stroke(noticeCard, Color3.fromRGB(255, 190, 60), 1, 0.5)
    Pad(noticeCard, 12, 12, 10, 10)
    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        Text = "⚠ Requires a special laser shirt or body mesh to display correctly. Without it, the animation still plays but the visual effect will not show up.",
        TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 214, 130),
        TextSize = 10,
        TextWrapped = true,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Parent = noticeCard,
    })

    -- ============ Logic ============
    -- Mainin combo 1 slot (dipanggil 2x oleh playLaser -- sekali buat
    -- Slot A, sekali buat Slot B) -- keduanya jalan BERSAMAAN, jadi total
    -- bisa sampai 4 animasi (2 id combo A + 2 id combo B) muter sekaligus,
    -- masing-masing pasang dengan speed slot-nya sendiri.
    local function playSlot(slot, animator)
        stopSlot(slot, false)
        local resuming = (slot.resumePresetRef == slot.preset) and (next(slot.savedPositions) ~= nil)
        local playedCount = 0
        for _, rawId in ipairs(slot.preset.ids) do
            local num = tostring(rawId):match("%d+")
            if num then
                local animId = "rbxassetid://" .. num
                local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
                anim.AnimationId = animId
                local ok, tr = pcall(function() return animator:LoadAnimation(anim) end)
                if ok and tr then
                    -- Priority tertinggi + Looped supaya animasi ini tetap
                    -- dominan & terus muter walau player jalan/lompat,
                    -- TIDAK ada listener apa pun yang bisa menghentikannya
                    -- otomatis -- cuma tombol Stop yang bisa hentikan.
                    tr.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
                    tr.Looped = true
                    pcall(function() tr:Play(0.2) end)
                    pcall(function() tr:AdjustSpeed(slot.speed) end)
                    if resuming and slot.savedPositions[animId] then
                        pcall(function() tr.TimePosition = slot.savedPositions[animId] end)
                    end
                    table.insert(slot.tracks, tr)
                    playedCount = playedCount + 1
                end
            end
        end
        if playedCount > 0 then slot.isPlaying = true end
        return playedCount, resuming
    end

    local function playLaser()
        local char = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character
        local hum = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local animator = hum and hum:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
        if not animator then
            statusLbl.Text = "Failed: character/Animator not found."
            statusLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 120, 120)
            return
        end

        local countA, resumingA = playSlot(slotA, animator)
        local countB, resumingB = playSlot(slotB, animator)
        local total = countA + countB

        if total > 0 then
            local parts = {}
            if countA > 0 then
                table.insert(parts, ("A:%s(%d)%s"):format(slotA.preset.label, countA, resumingA and "*" or ""))
            end
            if countB > 0 then
                table.insert(parts, ("B:%s(%d)%s"):format(slotB.preset.label, countB, resumingB and "*" or ""))
            end
            statusLbl.Text = ("Playing %s — %d animation(s) total. (* = resumed)"):format(table.concat(parts, " + "), total)
            statusLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 235, 160)
        else
            statusLbl.Text = "Failed to load any animation for Slot A/B."
            statusLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 120, 120)
        end
    end

    SafeConnect(GetSignal(playBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), playLaser)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(stopBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        stopLaser(true)
        statusLbl.Text = "Stopped — tekan Play buat lanjut dari posisi ini."
        statusLbl.TextColor3 = Palette.SubText
    end)
end

local function BuildChatAiTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Chat Ai"]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local function DoHttpRequest(opts)
        local requester = (typeof(request) == "function" and request)
            or (typeof(http_request) == "function" and http_request)
            or (syn and typeof(syn.request) == "function" and syn.request)
            or (typeof(fluxus) == "table" and typeof(fluxus.request) == "function" and fluxus.request)
        if not requester then
            return nil, "This executor doesn't support outbound HTTP requests (needs 'request' / 'http_request' / 'syn.request')."
        end
        local ok, response = pcall(requester, opts)
        if not ok then return nil, tostring(response) end
        return response, nil
    end

    local ApiKeys = { gemini = "", anthropic = "", openai = "", groq = "" }

    local MODELS = {
        { key = "gemini", label = "Gemini" },
        { key = "claude", label = "Claude" },
        { key = "groqllama", label = "Groq Llama" },
        { key = "groqgpt", label = "Groq GPT-OSS" },
        { key = "chatgpt", label = "ChatGPT 4o" },
    }
    local currentModel = "gemini"

    local function CallGeminiAPI(userMessage)
        if ApiKeys.gemini == "" then return "Error: Isi dulu Gemini API Key di panel ⚙ API Keys." end
        local body = HttpService:JSONEncode({ contents = {{ parts = {{ text = userMessage }} }} })
        local response, err = DoHttpRequest({
            Url = "https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.0-flash-exp:generateContent?key=" .. ApiKeys.gemini,
            Method = "POST",
            Headers = { ["Content-Type"] = "application/json" },
            Body = body,
        })
        if not response then return "Error: Request failed - " .. tostring(err) end
        if not response.Body then return "Error: No response from server." end
        local ok, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body) end)
        if not ok then return "Error: Invalid response format." end
        if data and data.candidates and data.candidates[1] and data.candidates[1].content
            and data.candidates[1].content.parts and data.candidates[1].content.parts[1]
            and data.candidates[1].content.parts[1].text then
            return data.candidates[1].content.parts[1].text
        end
        if data and data.error then return "Gemini Error: " .. (data.error.message or "Unknown error") end
        return "Error: Failed to read Gemini response."
    end

    local function CallClaudeAPI(userMessage)
        if ApiKeys.anthropic == "" then return "Error: Isi dulu Anthropic API Key di panel ⚙ API Keys." end
        local body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
            model = "claude-sonnet-4-5-20250929",
            max_tokens = 1024,
            messages = {{ role = "user", content = userMessage }},
        })
        local response, err = DoHttpRequest({
            Url = "https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",
            Method = "POST",
            Headers = {
                ["Content-Type"] = "application/json",
                ["x-api-key"] = ApiKeys.anthropic,
                ["anthropic-version"] = "2023-06-01",
            },
            Body = body,
        })
        if not response then return "Error: Request failed - " .. tostring(err) end
        if not response.Body then return "Error: No response from server." end
        local ok, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body) end)
        if not ok then return "Error: Invalid response format." end
        if data and data.content and data.content[1] and data.content[1].text then
            return data.content[1].text
        end
        if data and data.error then return "Claude Error: " .. (data.error.message or "Unknown error") end
        return "Error: Failed to read Claude response."
    end

    local function CallGroqAPI(userMessage, model)
        if ApiKeys.groq == "" then return "Error: Isi dulu Groq API Key di panel ⚙ API Keys." end
        local body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
            model = model,
            messages = {{ role = "user", content = userMessage }},
            max_tokens = 1024,
            temperature = 0.7,
        })
        local response, err = DoHttpRequest({
            Url = "https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions",
            Method = "POST",
            Headers = {
                ["Content-Type"] = "application/json",
                ["Authorization"] = "Bearer " .. ApiKeys.groq,
            },
            Body = body,
        })
        if not response then return "Error: Request failed - " .. tostring(err) end
        if not response.Body then return "Error: No response from server." end
        local ok, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body) end)
        if not ok then return "Error: Invalid response format." end
        if data and data.choices and data.choices[1] and data.choices[1].message and data.choices[1].message.content then
            return data.choices[1].message.content
        end
        if data and data.error then return "Groq Error: " .. (data.error.message or "Unknown error") end
        return "Error: Failed to read Groq response."
    end

    local function CallChatGPTAPI(userMessage)
        if ApiKeys.openai == "" then return "Error: Isi dulu OpenAI API Key di panel ⚙ API Keys." end
        local body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
            model = "gpt-4o-mini",
            messages = {{ role = "user", content = userMessage }},
            max_tokens = 1024,
            temperature = 0.7,
        })
        local response, err = DoHttpRequest({
            Url = "https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions",
            Method = "POST",
            Headers = {
                ["Content-Type"] = "application/json",
                ["Authorization"] = "Bearer " .. ApiKeys.openai,
            },
            Body = body,
        })
        if not response then return "Error: Request failed - " .. tostring(err) end
        if not response.Body then return "Error: No response from server." end
        local ok, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body) end)
        if not ok then return "Error: Invalid response format." end
        if data and data.choices and data.choices[1] and data.choices[1].message and data.choices[1].message.content then
            return data.choices[1].message.content
        end
        if data and data.error then return "ChatGPT Error: " .. (data.error.message or "Unknown error") end
        return "Error: Failed to read ChatGPT response."
    end

    local function CallAI(userMessage)
        if currentModel == "gemini" then return CallGeminiAPI(userMessage)
        elseif currentModel == "claude" then return CallClaudeAPI(userMessage)
        elseif currentModel == "groqllama" then return CallGroqAPI(userMessage, "llama-3.1-8b-instant")
        elseif currentModel == "groqgpt" then return CallGroqAPI(userMessage, "openai/gpt-oss-120b")
        elseif currentModel == "chatgpt" then return CallChatGPTAPI(userMessage)
        end
        return "Pick an AI model above first."
    end

    local function currentModelLabel()
        for _, m in ipairs(MODELS) do
            if m.key == currentModel then return m.label end
        end
        return "AI"
    end

    local section = tab:CreateSection("Chat AI", "Chat with AI directly from the GUI (using your own API key)")
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body
    if not body then return end

    local modelRow = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30), BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = body })
    New("UIGridLayout", {
        CellPadding = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6),
        CellSize = UDim2.new(0.18, 0, 1, 0),
        SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
        Parent = modelRow,
    })
    local modelButtons = {}
    for _, m in ipairs(MODELS) do
        local btn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.35,
            AutoButtonColor = false,
            Text = "",
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            Parent = modelRow,
        })
        Round(btn, 12)
        local btnStroke = Stroke(btn, accent, 1, 0.6)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 90,
            Parent = btn,
        })
        AddButtonHover(btn, btnStroke, 0)
        local lbl = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 1, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,

    end

    local settingsToggleBtn = New("TextButton", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28),

    local function apiKeyRow(label, keyName)
        local row = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40), BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = apiKeyPanel })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1, Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 14),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold, Text = label, TextColor3 = Palette.Text, TextSize = 9,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, Parent = row,
        })
        local box = New("TextBox", {
            Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 16), Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22),
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
            Font = Enum.Font.Code, Text = "", PlaceholderText = "Tempel API key di sini...",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text, PlaceholderColor3 = Palette.SubText, TextSize = 10,
            ClearTextOnFocus = false, TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, Parent = row,
        })
        Round(box, 9)
        local boxStroke = Stroke(box, accent, 1, 0.75)
        Pad(box, 8, 8, 0, 0)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(box, "Focused"), function()
            Tween(boxStroke, 0.15, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.1, Thickness = 1.4 })
        end)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(box, "FocusLost"), function()
            ApiKeys[keyName] = box.Text
            Tween(boxStroke, 0.2, nil, nil, { Transparency = 0.75, Thickness = 1 })
        end)
        return box
    end
    apiKeyRow("Gemini API Key", "gemini")
    apiKeyRow("Anthropic (Claude) API Key", "anthropic")
    apiKeyRow("OpenAI (ChatGPT) API Key", "openai")
    apiKeyRow("Groq API Key (dipakai Llama & GPT-OSS)", "groq")

    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
        Text = "This key is only kept for this session (not written to a file), so it needs to be re-entered every time the script runs.",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 8,
        TextWrapped = true,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
        Parent = apiKeyPanel,
    })

    local chatScroll = New("ScrollingFrame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 220),

    Round(chatScroll, 18)

    Pad(chatScroll, 10, 10, 10, 10)
    New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Padding = UDim.new(0, 8), Parent = chatScroll })

    local inputRow = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(inputRow, 17)
    Stroke(inputRow, accent, 1.2, 0.4)
    New("UIGradient", { Color = ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass), Rotation = 90, Parent = inputRow })

    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = ">",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 15,
        Parent = inputRow,
    })

    local chatBox = New("TextBox", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 0),
        Size = UDim2.new(1, -114, 1, 0),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
        Text = "",
        PlaceholderText = "Ask " .. currentModelLabel() .. "...",
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        PlaceholderColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 11,
        ClearTextOnFocus = false,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Parent = inputRow,
    })
    local sendBtn = New("TextButton", {
        BackgroundColor3 = accent,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
        Position = UDim2.new(1, -74, 0.5, -12),
        Size = UDim2.new(0, 64, 0, 24),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "Send",
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextSize = 11,
        Parent = inputRow,
    })
    Round(sendBtn, 12)
    AddButtonHover(sendBtn)

    local function autoScrollToBottom()
        task.defer(function()
            pcall(function()
                chatScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, math.max(0, chatScroll.CanvasSize.Y.Offset))
            end)
        end)
    end

    local function AddMessage(sender, text, isUser)
        local showSenderLabel = (not isUser) and sender ~= ""

        local wrapper = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Parent = chatScroll,
        })

        local bubble = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0.86, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            Position = isUser and UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0) or UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
            AnchorPoint = isUser and Vector2.new(1, 0) or Vector2.new(0, 0),
            BackgroundColor3 = isUser and accent or Palette.Glass,
            BackgroundTransparency = isUser and 0.15 or 0.25,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            Parent = wrapper,
        })
        Round(bubble, 14)
        New("UIGradient", {
            Color = isUser
                and ColorSequence.new(accent, Palette.AccentDark)
                or ColorSequence.new(Palette.GlassLight, Palette.Glass),
            Rotation = 100,
            Parent = bubble,
        })
        if not isUser then Stroke(bubble, accent, 1, 0.6) end
        local bubbleSheen = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 14),
            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.9,
            ZIndex = 0,
            Parent = bubble,
        })
        Round(bubbleSheen, 14)
        Pad(bubble, 10, 10, 8, 8)
        New("UIListLayout", { SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Padding = UDim.new(0, 3), Parent = bubble })

        if showSenderLabel then
            New("TextLabel", {
                BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 12),
                Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
                Text = sender,
                TextColor3 = accent,
                TextSize = 8,
                TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
                LayoutOrder = 1,
                Parent = bubble,
            })
        end

        local textLabel = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
            Text = text,
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextWrapped = true,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
            LayoutOrder = 2,
            Parent = bubble,
        })

        autoScrollToBottom()
        return wrapper, textLabel
    end

    local function AddCodeBlock(code)
        local wrapper = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Parent = chatScroll,
        })
        local card = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(0.86, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
            ClipsDescendants = true,
            Parent = wrapper,
        })
        Round(card, 12)
        Stroke(card, accent, 1, 0.5)
        Pad(card, 8, 52, 6, 6)

        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0),
            AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
            Font = Enum.Font.Code,
            Text = code,
            TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 240, 170),
            TextSize = 9,
            TextWrapped = true,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
            Parent = card,
        })

        local copyBtn = New("TextButton", {
            BackgroundColor3 = accent,
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
            Position = UDim2.new(1, -46, 0, 4),
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 20),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Text = "Copy",
            TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
            TextSize = 8,
            ZIndex = 3,
            Parent = card,
        })
        Round(copyBtn, 6)
        AddButtonHover(copyBtn)
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(copyBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            local ok = pcall(function()
                local sc = setclipboard or toclipboard
                if sc then sc(code) end
            end)
            copyBtn.Text = ok and "OK" or "Gagal"
            task.delay(1, function() pcall(function() copyBtn.Text = "Copy" end) end)
        end)

        autoScrollToBottom()
        return wrapper
    end

    local function ExtractCodeBlocks(message)
        local parts = {}
        local lastIndex = 1
        for codeStart, language, code, codeEnd in message:gmatch("()```([%w]*)\n?(.-)\n?```()") do
            if codeStart > lastIndex then
                local textBefore = message:sub(lastIndex, codeStart - 1)
                if textBefore:gsub("%s+", "") ~= "" then
                    table.insert(parts, { type = "text", content = textBefore })
                end
            end
            table.insert(parts, { type = "code", content = code, language = language })
            lastIndex = codeEnd
        end
        if lastIndex <= #message then
            local textAfter = message:sub(lastIndex)
            if textAfter:gsub("%s+", "") ~= "" then
                table.insert(parts, { type = "text", content = textAfter })
            end
        end
        if #parts == 0 then
            table.insert(parts, { type = "text", content = message })
        end
        return parts
    end

    local function DisplayAIResponse(message)
        local parts = ExtractCodeBlocks(message)
        local senderAdded = false
        for _, part in ipairs(parts) do
            if part.type == "text" then
                AddMessage(senderAdded and "" or currentModelLabel(), part.content, false)
                senderAdded = true
            elseif part.type == "code" then
                AddCodeBlock(part.content)
            end
        end
    end

    local function ShowLoading()
        local wrapper, textLabel = AddMessage(currentModelLabel(), ".", false)
        local running = true
        task.spawn(function()
            local dots = 0
            while running and textLabel and textLabel.Parent do
                dots = (dots % 3) + 1
                pcall(function() textLabel.Text = string.rep(".", dots) end)
                task.wait(0.4)
            end
        end)
        return wrapper, function() running = false end
    end

    local function stylePillsModel()
        for key, entry in pairs(modelButtons) do
            local active = currentModel == key
            Tween(entry.Frame, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                BackgroundColor3 = active and accent or Palette.Glass,
                BackgroundTransparency = active and 0.05 or 0.4,
            })
            Tween(entry.Label, 0.15, nil, nil, { TextColor3 = active and Palette.Text or Palette.SubText })
            if entry.Stroke then
                Tween(entry.Stroke, 0.15, nil, nil, {
                    Transparency = active and 0.05 or 0.65,
                    Thickness = active and 1.5 or 1,
                })
            end
        end
    end
    for _, m in ipairs(MODELS) do
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(modelButtons[m.key].Frame, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
            currentModel = m.key
            stylePillsModel()
            SafeSet(chatBox, "PlaceholderText", "Ask " .. m.label .. "...")
        end)
    end
    stylePillsModel()

    local settingsOpen = false
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(settingsToggleBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
        settingsOpen = not settingsOpen
        SafeSet(apiKeyPanel, "Visible", settingsOpen)
    end)

    local isResponding = false
    local function sendMessage()
        if isResponding then return end
        local msg = chatBox.Text
        if msg:gsub("%s+", "") == "" then return end
        AddMessage("You", msg, true)
        chatBox.Text = ""
        isResponding = true
        local loadingWrapper, stopLoading = ShowLoading()
        task.spawn(function()
            local response = CallAI(msg)
            stopLoading()
            if loadingWrapper then pcall(function() loadingWrapper:Destroy() end) end
            DisplayAIResponse(response)
            isResponding = false
        end)
    end
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(sendBtn, "MouseButton1Click"), sendMessage)
    SafeConnect(GetSignal(chatBox, "FocusLost"), function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then sendMessage() end
    end)

    AddMessage("System", "Chat AI is ready. Pick a model above, enter your own API key in the ⚙ API Keys panel, then start chatting. The key is only kept for this session (not written to a file).", false)
end

local function BuildSettingsTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs["Settings"]
    if not tab then return end

    tab:OnBuild(function()

        local appearance = tab:CreateSection("Appearance", "Customize the look of JEYHUB UNIVERSAL")

        appearance:CreateSlider({
            Title = "UI Scale",
            Subtitle = "Perbesar / perkecil seluruh window (70% - 130%)",
            Min = 70, Max = 130, Step = 5,
            Default = math.floor(UserUIScale * 100 + 0.5),
            Callback = function(v)
                UserUIScale = v / 100
                if Window and Window.Scale then
                    Tween(Window.Scale, 0.15, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Scale = UserUIScale })
                end

                if Window and Window.GlowOuterScale then
                    Tween(Window.GlowOuterScale, 0.15, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Scale = UserUIScale })
                end
                if Window and Window.GlowInnerScale then
                    Tween(Window.GlowInnerScale, 0.15, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, nil, { Scale = UserUIScale })
                end

                -- Supaya dropdown/color picker yang KEBETULAN lagi
                -- terbuka saat slider ini digeser ikut nge-tween scale-nya
                -- bareng window utama, bukan nunggu ditutup-buka lagi dulu.
                SyncAllFloatingLayers()
            end,
        })

        appearance:CreateColorPicker({
            Title = "Global Theme",
            Subtitle = "Change the main accent color across the sidebar & new tabs",
            Default = Palette.Accent,
            Callback = function(c)
                ApplyGlobalTheme(c)
            end,
        })

        appearance:CreateButton({
            Title = "Reset Window Position",
            Subtitle = "Return the window to center screen if dragged far away",
            ButtonText = "Reset",
            Callback = function()
                if Window and Window.Root then
                    Tween(Window.Root, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, nil, { Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0) })
                end
            end,
        })

        local behavior = tab:CreateSection("Behavior", "Preferensi interaksi & performa")

        behavior:CreateToggle({
            Title = "Sound Effects",
            Subtitle = "Click / toggle / tab switch sounds",
            Default = UIEnableSounds,
            Callback = function(state)
                UIEnableSounds = state
            end,
        })

        behavior:CreateToggle({
            Title = "Reduce Motion",
            Subtitle = "Turn off breathing/glow animations for lower-end devices",
            Default = false,
            Callback = function(state)
                if Window and Window.SetReducedMotion then
                    Window.SetReducedMotion(state)
                end
            end,
        })

        local about = tab:CreateSection("About", "Brief info")
        about:CreateButton({
            Title = "JEYHUB UNIVERSAL",
            Subtitle = "See version details & credits in the Credits tab",
            ButtonText = "OK",
            Callback = function() end,
        })
    end)
end
