            return row
        end

        socialRow("TT", Color3.fromRGB(255, 60, 110), "TikTok", "@jswhizz", 1)
        socialRow("DC", Color3.fromRGB(88, 101, 242), "Discord", "Cameron Alberizan", 2)

        local about = tab:CreateSection("About", "Thank you for using JEYHUB UNIVERSAL")
        local aboutBody = about.Body

        local footer = New("Frame", {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 68),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Parent = aboutBody,
        })
        New("UIListLayout", {
            SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder,
            Padding = UDim.new(0, 2),
            HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center,
            Parent = footer,
        })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack,
            Text = "JEYHUB UNIVERSAL",
            TextColor3 = accent,
            TextSize = 15,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            LayoutOrder = 1,
            Parent = footer,
        })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
            Text = "Built with precision, polished with detail.",
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            LayoutOrder = 2,
            Parent = footer,
        })
        New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = "Made with ♥",
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 10,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center,
            LayoutOrder = 3,
            Parent = footer,
        })
    end)
end

local function BuildPlaceholderTab(tabName, note)
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs[tabName]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local section = tab:CreateSection(tabName, "This tab doesn't have its features filled in yet")
    local accent = section.Accent or Palette.Accent
    local body = section.Body

    local card = New("Frame", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 90),
        BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass,
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        ClipsDescendants = true,
        Parent = body,
    })
    Round(card, 12)
    Stroke(card, accent, 1, 0.5)
    Pad(card, 14, 14, 12, 12)

    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 18),
        Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Text = "🚧 No features in this tab yet",
        TextColor3 = Palette.Text,
        TextSize = 12,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        Parent = card,
    })
    New("TextLabel", {
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 22),
        Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -22),
        Font = Enum.Font.Gotham,
        Text = note or "Tell me what features you want in this tab, and they'll be built right away.",
        TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
        TextSize = 10,
        TextWrapped = true,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top,
        Parent = card,
    })
end

local function BuildVisualTab()
    local tab = CreatedTabs and CreatedTabs["Visual"]
    if not tab or not tab.CreateSection then return end

    local RunService = SafeService("RunService")
    local Lighting = SafeService("Lighting")
    local Workspace = SafeService("Workspace")
    local Terrain = Workspace and Workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain")
    local Camera = Workspace and Workspace.CurrentCamera
    local Players = SafeService("Players")
    local LocalPlayer = Players and Players.LocalPlayer
    local TweenService = SafeService("TweenService")
    local CoreGui = SafeService("CoreGui")

    local fenv = getfenv()
    local set_hidden_prop = fenv.sethiddenproperty or fenv.sethiddenprop or fenv.set_hidden_property or fenv.set_hidden_prop or function() end
    local get_hidden_prop = fenv.gethiddenproperty or fenv.gethiddenprop or function() return nil end

    local wshade = true
    local wl = {
        dof = false, cor = false, rays = false, bl = false, blr = false,
        sflare = false, mblur = false, tech = get_hidden_prop(Lighting, 'Technology') or 'ShadowMap', global = false
    }

    local bmsize = 26
    local adjust = { reflect = 0 }

    local function ReadCurrentQualityLevel()
        local ok, level = pcall(function() return settings().Rendering.QualityLevel end)
        if ok and level then
            local n = tonumber(tostring(level):match("%d+"))
            if n then return math.clamp(n, 1, 21) end
        end
        return 21
    end
    local graphicsQuality = ReadCurrentQualityLevel()

    local visW = {}

    local function getOrMake(class, parent, defaultProps)
        local inst = parent:FindFirstChildOfClass(class)
        if not inst then
            inst = Instance.new(class)
            inst.Parent = parent
        end
        for k, v in pairs(defaultProps or {}) do pcall(function() inst[k] = v end) end
        return inst
    end

    local colorcor = getOrMake("ColorCorrectionEffect", Lighting, {Enabled = false})
    local atmosphere = getOrMake("Atmosphere", Lighting, {Density = 0.3, Offset = 0.25})
    local bloom = getOrMake("BloomEffect", Lighting, {Enabled = false, Intensity = 1, Size = 24, Threshold = 2})
    local blur = getOrMake("BlurEffect", Lighting, {Enabled = false, Size = 0})
    local depth = getOrMake("DepthOfFieldEffect", Lighting, {Enabled = false, FarIntensity = 0.4, FocusDistance = 12, InFocusRadius = 20, NearIntensity = 0.5})
    local sky = getOrMake("Sky", Lighting)
    local sray = getOrMake("SunRaysEffect", Lighting, {Enabled = false, Intensity = 0.25, Spread = 1})
    local cloud = Terrain and getOrMake("Clouds", Terrain, {Cover = 0, Density = 0}) or nil

    local mblur = Instance.new("BlurEffect")
    mblur.Name = "JeyhubMotionBlur"
    mblur.Size = 0
    pcall(function() mblur.Parent = Camera end)

    if not _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting then
        _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting = {
            Ambient = Lighting.Ambient, ClockTime = Lighting.ClockTime, GeographicLatitude = Lighting.GeographicLatitude,
            Brightness = Lighting.Brightness, ColorShift_Bottom = Lighting.ColorShift_Bottom, ColorShift_Top = Lighting.ColorShift_Top,
            EnvironmentDiffuseScale = Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale, EnvironmentSpecularScale = Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale,
            GlobalShadows = Lighting.GlobalShadows, OutdoorAmbient = Lighting.OutdoorAmbient, ExposureCompensation = Lighting.ExposureCompensation,
        }
    end
    local DefaultLighting = {
        Ambient = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.Ambient, ClockTime = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.ClockTime, GeographicLatitude = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.GeographicLatitude,
        Brightness = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.Brightness, ColorShift_Bottom = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.ColorShift_Bottom, ColorShift_Top = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.ColorShift_Top,
        EnvironmentDiffuseScale = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale, EnvironmentSpecularScale = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale,
        GlobalShadows = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.GlobalShadows, OutdoorAmbient = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.OutdoorAmbient, ExposureCompensation = _G.JEYHUB_VisualDefaultLighting.ExposureCompensation,
        ccBrightness = colorcor.Brightness, ccContrast = colorcor.Contrast, ccSaturation = colorcor.Saturation, ccTintColor = colorcor.TintColor,
        blIntensity = bloom.Intensity, blSize = bloom.Size, blThreshold = bloom.Threshold, blrSize = blur.Size,
        dofFar = depth.FarIntensity, dofFocus = depth.FocusDistance, dofRadius = depth.InFocusRadius, dofNear = depth.NearIntensity,
        atDensity = atmosphere.Density, atOffset = atmosphere.Offset, atColor = atmosphere.Color, atDecay = atmosphere.Decay, atGlare = atmosphere.Glare, atHaze = atmosphere.Haze,
        srIntensity = sray.Intensity, srSpread = sray.Spread,
        clCover = cloud and cloud.Cover or 0, clDensity = cloud and cloud.Density or 0, clColor = cloud and cloud.Color or Color3.new(1,1,1),
        skyBk = sky.SkyboxBk, skyDn = sky.SkyboxDn, skyFt = sky.SkyboxFt, skyLf = sky.SkyboxLf, skyRt = sky.SkyboxRt, skyUp = sky.SkyboxUp
    }

    pcall(function()
        Lighting.Ambient = DefaultLighting.Ambient
        Lighting.ClockTime = DefaultLighting.ClockTime
        Lighting.Brightness = DefaultLighting.Brightness
        Lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Bottom
        Lighting.ColorShift_Top = DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Top
        Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale
        Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale
        Lighting.GlobalShadows = DefaultLighting.GlobalShadows
        Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = DefaultLighting.OutdoorAmbient
        Lighting.ExposureCompensation = DefaultLighting.ExposureCompensation
    end)

    local defaultLight = {
        ['yfbghj'] = DefaultLighting.Ambient, ['tgvbyd'] = DefaultLighting.ClockTime, ['ghuybhuyhj'] = DefaultLighting.GeographicLatitude,
        ['khnbfth'] = DefaultLighting.Brightness, ['hgyghkg'] = DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Bottom, ['yfbhjku'] = DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Top,
        ['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale, ['sdfcddc'] = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale,
        ['hgnujuu7thgr'] = DefaultLighting.GlobalShadows, ['hyhnngtf'] = DefaultLighting.OutdoorAmbient, ['hdfr7thgr'] = DefaultLighting.ExposureCompensation,
        ['fhnchvhfjsd'] = DefaultLighting.ccBrightness, ['ugtbbjhygt'] = DefaultLighting.ccContrast, ['tfbghuugbnjhg'] = DefaultLighting.ccSaturation, ['fvrtccvghghj'] = DefaultLighting.ccTintColor,
        ['jnfdhbnfcvh'] = DefaultLighting.blIntensity, ['fvtyghj'] = DefaultLighting.blSize, ['ygbhnj'] = DefaultLighting.blThreshold, ['njnfg'] = DefaultLighting.blrSize,
        ['jdfkd'] = DefaultLighting.dofFar, ['fvgsdfg'] = DefaultLighting.dofFocus, ['sdkvkflv'] = DefaultLighting.dofRadius, ['hbjhd'] = DefaultLighting.dofNear,
        ['gyhgtg'] = DefaultLighting.clCover, ['ygbhggv'] = DefaultLighting.clDensity, ['jghbjhgyfd'] = DefaultLighting.clColor,
        ['shdbsnjfc'] = DefaultLighting.atDensity, ['skdjfkdm'] = DefaultLighting.atOffset, ['sjdjncdjf'] = DefaultLighting.atColor, ['efjdjfk'] = DefaultLighting.atDecay, ['sejfd'] = DefaultLighting.atGlare, ['jddfjsd'] = DefaultLighting.atHaze
    }

    local light = defaultLight

    local function syncVisualWidgets()
        for key, widget in pairs(visW) do
            if widget and widget.Set and light and light[key] ~= nil then
                widget.Set(light[key])
            end
        end
    end

    local defsky = {bk = sky.SkyboxBk, dn = sky.SkyboxDn, ft = sky.SkyboxFt, lt = sky.SkyboxLf, rt = sky.SkyboxRt, up = sky.SkyboxUp}
    local cussky = {bk = 'rbxassetid://9544505500', dn = 'rbxassetid://9544547905', ft = 'rbxassetid://9544504852', lt = 'rbxassetid://9544547694', rt = 'rbxassetid://9544547542', up = 'rbxassetid://9544547398'}

    local PSHADE_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/randomstring0/pshade-ultimate/refs/heads/main/"
    local PshadeCache = {}
    local PshadeSkyCache = {}
    local PshadeFailed = {}
    local PSHADE_MAX_BYTES = 64 * 1024

    local function SanitizePresetTable(t)
        if type(t) ~= "table" then return nil end
        local clean = {}
        local count = 0
        for k, v in pairs(t) do
            count = count + 1
            if count > 200 then break end
            if type(k) == "string" then
                local vt = typeof(v)
                if vt == "number" or vt == "boolean" or vt == "string" or vt == "Color3" or vt == "UDim2" then
                    clean[k] = v
                end
            end
        end
        return clean
    end

    local function FetchAndSanitizePreset(path)
        if PshadeFailed[path] then return nil end
        local okFetch, body = pcall(function() return game:HttpGet(PSHADE_URL .. path) end)
        if not okFetch or type(body) ~= "string" or #body == 0 or #body > PSHADE_MAX_BYTES then
            warn("[JEYHUB] Preset fetch failed/abnormal size:", path)
            PshadeFailed[path] = true
            return nil
        end
        local compiled, compileErr = loadstring(body)
        if type(compiled) ~= "function" then
            warn("[JEYHUB] Preset failed to compile:", path, compileErr)
            PshadeFailed[path] = true
            return nil
        end
        local okRun, res = pcall(compiled)
        local sanitized = okRun and SanitizePresetTable(res) or nil
        if not sanitized then
            warn("[JEYHUB] Preset returned invalid data:", path)
            PshadeFailed[path] = true
            return nil
        end
        return sanitized
    end

    local function ApplyPshadePreset(urlPath, skyPath)
        task.spawn(function()

            if PshadeCache[urlPath] then
                light = PshadeCache[urlPath]
            else
                local sanitized = FetchAndSanitizePreset(urlPath)
                if sanitized then
                    PshadeCache[urlPath] = sanitized
                    light = sanitized
                end
            end

            if skyPath then
                if PshadeSkyCache[skyPath] then
                    cussky = PshadeSkyCache[skyPath]
                else
                    local sanitizedSky = FetchAndSanitizePreset(skyPath)
                    if sanitizedSky then
                        PshadeSkyCache[skyPath] = sanitizedSky
                        cussky = sanitizedSky
                    end
                end
            end

            syncVisualWidgets()
        end)
    end

    local lightfolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Jeyhub_GI_Folder") or Instance.new("Folder")
    lightfolder.Name = "Jeyhub_GI_Folder"
    lightfolder.Parent = Workspace

    local globalil = {
        gridsize = 40, radius = 50, shadowlength = 8, reflectdis = 10, active = {}, maxActive = 30,
        shadowdirection = {
            Vector3.new(1, -1, 0).Unit, Vector3.new(-1, -1, 0).Unit, Vector3.new(0, -1, 1).Unit, Vector3.new(0, -1, -1).Unit
        }
    }

    local function roundToGrid(v) return Vector3.new(math.floor(v.X / globalil.gridsize + 0.5) * globalil.gridsize, math.floor(v.Y / globalil.gridsize + 0.5) * globalil.gridsize, math.floor(v.Z / globalil.gridsize + 0.5) * globalil.gridsize) end
    local function hashVec3(v) return tostring(v.X).."_"..tostring(v.Y).."_"..tostring(v.Z) end
    local function isIndoors(pos) return Workspace:Raycast(pos, Vector3.new(0, 500, 0)) ~= nil end
    local function simulateShadow(pos) for _, dir in ipairs(globalil.shadowdirection) do if Workspace:Raycast(pos, dir * globalil.shadowlength) then return true end end return false end
    local function blendColors(c1, c2, alpha) return Color3.new(c1.R * (1 - alpha) + c2.R * alpha, c1.G * (1 - alpha) + c2.G * alpha, c1.B * (1 - alpha) + c2.B * alpha) end

    -- Dulu tabel arah ini dibuat ulang dari nol tiap kali loop createLightPoint
    -- jalan (tiap 6 detik x jumlah titik aktif) -- sekarang di-cache sekali
    -- sebagai konstanta, mengurangi alokasi memori & tekanan garbage collector.
    local GI_REFLECT_DIRS = {
        Vector3.new(1, 0, 0), Vector3.new(-1, 0, 0),
        Vector3.new(0, 1, 0), Vector3.new(0, -1, 0),
        Vector3.new(0, 0, 1), Vector3.new(0, 0, -1),
    }

    local function createLightPoint(pos)
        local part = Instance.new("Part")
        part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.Transparency = 1
        part.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1); part.Position = pos; part.Name = "GINode"
        part.Parent = lightfolder
        local clight = Instance.new("PointLight")
        clight.Range = 24; clight.Brightness = 0; clight.Shadows = false
        clight.Color = light['yfbghj'] or DefaultLighting.Ambient; clight.Parent = part

        task.spawn(function()
            while part and part.Parent and wl.global and wshade do
                if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
                local indoor = isIndoors(pos)
                local inShadow = simulateShadow(pos)
                local baseColor = indoor and Color3.fromRGB(255, 240, 220) or (light['hyhnngtf'] or DefaultLighting.OutdoorAmbient)
                local brightness = indoor and 0.35 or 0.75
                local r, g, b, hits = 0, 0, 0, 0

                for _, dir in ipairs(GI_REFLECT_DIRS) do
                    local ray = Workspace:Raycast(pos, dir * globalil.reflectdis)
                    if ray and ray.Instance and ray.Instance:IsA("BasePart") then
                        local Color = ray.Instance.Color
                        r = r + Color.R; g = g + Color.G; b = b + Color.B
                        hits = hits + 1
                    end
                end

                if hits > 0 then
                    local avgColor = Color3.new(r / hits, g / hits, b / hits)
                    baseColor = blendColors(baseColor, avgColor, 0.7)
                    if inShadow then brightness = brightness * 0.3 end
                elseif inShadow then brightness = 0 end

                clight.Color = baseColor; clight.Brightness = brightness
                task.wait(6)
            end
        end)
        return part
    end

    local sre = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    sre.Name = "JEYHUB_Sunflare"
    sre.Enabled = false; sre.ResetOnSpawn = false
    pcall(function() sre.Parent = CoreGui end)
    if not sre.Parent and LocalPlayer then sre.Parent = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui", 5) end

    local sflare = Instance.new("ImageLabel", sre)
    sflare.SizeConstraint = Enum.SizeConstraint.RelativeYY
    sflare.BackgroundTransparency = 1; sflare.Image = "rbxassetid://277033149"
    sflare.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 0.95); sflare.Size = UDim2.new(15*0.2, 0, 15*0.2, 0)

    local fls, fdist, fsize, ftrans = {}, {1.7, 0.3, -0.3, -0.9}, {0.7, 0.2, 1.2, 0.45}, {0.8, 0.7, 0.9, 0.6}
    for i = 1, #fdist do
        local f = Instance.new("ImageLabel", sre)
        f.SizeConstraint = Enum.SizeConstraint.RelativeYY
        f.BackgroundTransparency = 1; f.ImageTransparency = ftrans[i]; f.Rotation = -25
        f.Image = "rbxassetid://15164863822"; f.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 0.8)
        f.Size = UDim2.new(fsize[i]*0.2, 0, fsize[i]*0.2, 0)
        table.insert(fls, f)
    end

    local lor = Camera and Camera.CFrame.LookVector or Vector3.new()
    local rmod = 1

    local function GetSunflareScale()
        if not Camera then return 1 end
        local vp = Camera.ViewportSize
        if vp.Y <= 0 then return 1 end
        local aspect = vp.X / vp.Y
        local standardAspect = 16 / 9
        if aspect <= standardAspect then return 1 end
        return math.clamp(1 + (aspect - standardAspect) * 0.35, 1, 1.6)
    end

    local lastEnvSync = 0
    SafeConnect(RunService.RenderStepped, function()
        if not wshade then sre.Enabled = false; mblur.Size = 0 return end

        colorcor.Enabled = wl.cor; blur.Enabled = wl.blr; bloom.Enabled = wl.bl
        depth.Enabled = wl.dof; sray.Enabled = wl.rays

        -- OPTIMASI PERFORMA: blok sinkronisasi ~30 properti Lighting/
        -- PostEffect di bawah ini SEBELUMNYA jalan tiap frame (60x/detik)
        -- TANPA throttle -- itu 1800+ penulisan properti per detik yang
        -- HAMPIR SELALU sia-sia karena nilainya nggak berubah dari frame
        -- sebelumnya (cuma perlu ke-apply ulang kalau ada yang benar-benar
        -- reset dari luar, atau slider baru digeser). Di-throttle jadi
        -- 10x/detik (tiap 0.1s) -- untuk mata manusia nggak ada bedanya
        -- sama sekali (nggak ada delay yang kerasa), tapi beban CPU turun
        -- drastis tanpa mengubah fungsinya sedikit pun.
        local nowSync = os.clock()
        if nowSync - lastEnvSync >= 0.1 then
            lastEnvSync = nowSync
            pcall(function()
            colorcor.Brightness = light['fhnchvhfjsd'] or DefaultLighting.ccBrightness
            colorcor.Contrast = light['ugtbbjhygt'] or DefaultLighting.ccContrast
            colorcor.Saturation = light['tfbghuugbnjhg'] or DefaultLighting.ccSaturation
            colorcor.TintColor = light['fvrtccvghghj'] or DefaultLighting.ccTintColor
            bloom.Intensity = light['jnfdhbnfcvh'] or DefaultLighting.blIntensity
            bloom.Size = light['fvtyghj'] or DefaultLighting.blSize
            bloom.Threshold = light['ygbhnj'] or DefaultLighting.blThreshold
            blur.Size = light['njnfg'] or DefaultLighting.blrSize
            Lighting.Ambient = light['yfbghj'] or DefaultLighting.Ambient
            Lighting.ClockTime = light['tgvbyd'] or DefaultLighting.ClockTime
            Lighting.GeographicLatitude = light['ghuybhuyhj'] or DefaultLighting.GeographicLatitude
            Lighting.Brightness = light['khnbfth'] or DefaultLighting.Brightness
            Lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = light['hgyghkg'] or DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Bottom
            Lighting.ColorShift_Top = light['yfbhjku'] or DefaultLighting.ColorShift_Top
            Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = light['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] or DefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale
            Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = light['sdfcddc'] or DefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale
            Lighting.GlobalShadows = light['hgnujuu7thgr'] or DefaultLighting.GlobalShadows
            Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = light['hyhnngtf'] or DefaultLighting.OutdoorAmbient
            Lighting.ExposureCompensation = light['hdfr7thgr'] or DefaultLighting.ExposureCompensation

            if sray then
                sray.Intensity = light['srIntensity'] or DefaultLighting.srIntensity
                sray.Spread = light['srSpread'] or DefaultLighting.srSpread
            end

            if cloud then
                cloud.Cover = light['gyhgtg'] or DefaultLighting.clCover
                cloud.Density = light['ygbhggv'] or DefaultLighting.clDensity
                cloud.Color = light['jghbjhgyfd'] or DefaultLighting.clColor
            end
            atmosphere.Density = light['shdbsnjfc'] or DefaultLighting.atDensity
            atmosphere.Offset = light['skdjfkdm'] or DefaultLighting.atOffset
            atmosphere.Color = light['sjdjncdjf'] or DefaultLighting.atColor
            atmosphere.Decay = light['efjdjfk'] or DefaultLighting.atDecay
            atmosphere.Glare = light['sejfd'] or DefaultLighting.atGlare
            atmosphere.Haze = light['jddfjsd'] or DefaultLighting.atHaze
            depth.FarIntensity = light['jdfkd'] or DefaultLighting.dofFar
            depth.FocusDistance = light['fvgsdfg'] or DefaultLighting.dofFocus
            depth.InFocusRadius = light['sdkvkflv'] or DefaultLighting.dofRadius
            depth.NearIntensity = light['hbjhd'] or DefaultLighting.dofNear
            sky.SkyboxBk = cussky.bk or DefaultLighting.skyBk
            sky.SkyboxDn = cussky.dn or DefaultLighting.skyDn
            sky.SkyboxFt = cussky.ft or DefaultLighting.skyFt
            sky.SkyboxLf = cussky.lt or DefaultLighting.skyLf
            sky.SkyboxRt = cussky.rt or DefaultLighting.skyRt
            sky.SkyboxUp = cussky.up or DefaultLighting.skyUp
        end)
        end

        if wl.mblur and Camera then
            local mag = (Camera.CFrame.LookVector - lor).Magnitude
            mblur.Size = math.abs(mag) * bmsize * 5 / 2
            lor = Camera.CFrame.LookVector
        else
            mblur.Size = 0
        end

        if wl.sflare and Camera then
            local sunDirection = Lighting:GetSunDirection()

            if sunDirection.Y <= 0.02 then
                sre.Enabled = false
            else
            sre.Enabled = true
            local sunpos, front = Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(Camera.CFrame.Position + sunDirection)
            local hrp = LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local clear = true
            if hrp then
                local ray = Workspace:Raycast(Camera.CFrame.Position, (hrp.Position + Vector3.new(0,1.5,0) - Camera.CFrame.Position))
                if ray and ray.Instance and not ray.Instance:IsDescendantOf(LocalPlayer.Character) then clear = false end
            end

            local viewDot = Camera.CFrame.LookVector:Dot(sunDirection)
            local angleFactor = math.clamp((viewDot + 0.35) / 1.35, 0, 1)
            local visibleRange = front or angleFactor > 0

            rmod = rmod * 0.5 + (clear and 1 or 0) * 0.5
            local finalMod = rmod * angleFactor

            local scen = Camera.ViewportSize / 2
            local vec = Vector2.new(sunpos.X, sunpos.Y) - scen

            local screenScale = math.max(scen.Magnitude, 1)
            local sizeScale = GetSunflareScale()
            for i, v in ipairs(fls) do
                v.ImageTransparency = 1 - finalMod + ftrans[i] * finalMod
                v.Size = UDim2.new(fsize[i]*0.2*sizeScale, 0, fsize[i]*0.2*sizeScale, 0)
                local size = v.AbsoluteSize
                local offset = vec * fdist[i]
                local maxOffset = screenScale * 1.4
                if offset.Magnitude > maxOffset then
                    offset = offset.Unit * maxOffset
                end
                local pos = scen + offset
                v.Position = UDim2.new(0, pos.X - size.X/2, 0, pos.Y - size.Y/2)
                v.Visible = visibleRange
            end
            sflare.ImageTransparency = 1 - finalMod
            sflare.Size = UDim2.new(15*0.2*sizeScale, 0, 15*0.2*sizeScale, 0)
            sflare.Position = UDim2.new(0, sunpos.X - sflare.AbsoluteSize.X/2, 0, sunpos.Y - sflare.AbsoluteSize.Y/2)
            sflare.Visible = visibleRange
            end
        else
            sre.Enabled = false
        end
    end)

    local giLastScanCamPos = nil
    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(3) do
            if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
            if wshade and wl.global and Camera then
                local camPos = Camera.CFrame.Position
                -- Kamera belum pindah cukup jauh sejak scan terakhir -> grid
                -- yang relevan pasti masih sama persis, jadi skip seluruh
                -- triple-nested loop di bawah (hemat CPU signifikan saat
                -- player sedang diam/AFK/lagi buka menu).
                local cameraMoved = (not giLastScanCamPos) or (camPos - giLastScanCamPos).Magnitude >= 5
                if cameraMoved then
                    giLastScanCamPos = camPos
                    local min = camPos - Vector3.new(globalil.radius, globalil.radius, globalil.radius)
                    local max = camPos + Vector3.new(globalil.radius, globalil.radius, globalil.radius)
                    local seen = {}
                    local activeCount = 0
                    for _ in pairs(globalil.active) do activeCount = activeCount + 1 end
                    for x = min.X, max.X, globalil.gridsize do
                        for y = min.Y, max.Y, globalil.gridsize do
                            for z = min.Z, max.Z, globalil.gridsize do
                                if activeCount >= globalil.maxActive then break end
                                local pos = roundToGrid(Vector3.new(x, y, z))
                                local hash = hashVec3(pos)
                                seen[hash] = true
                                if not globalil.active[hash] and (pos - camPos).Magnitude <= globalil.radius then
                                    globalil.active[hash] = createLightPoint(pos)
                                    activeCount = activeCount + 1
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    for hash, part in pairs(globalil.active) do
                        if part and part:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) then
                            if (part.Position - camPos).Magnitude > (globalil.gridsize + globalil.radius) then
                                part:Destroy(); globalil.active[hash] = nil
                            end
                        else
                            globalil.active[hash] = nil
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end)

    local function stylePills()
        for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
            local active = currentSubTab == entry.Def.key
            TweenService:Create(entry.Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.15), { BackgroundColor3 = active and accent or Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = active and 0.05 or 0.4 }):Play()
            TweenService:Create(entry.Label, TweenInfo.new(0.15), { TextColor3 = active and Palette.Text or Palette.SubText }):Play()
            if entry.Stroke then TweenService:Create(entry.Stroke, TweenInfo.new(0.15), { Transparency = active and 0.05 or 0.65, Thickness = active and 1.5 or 1 }):Play() end
        end
        for k, p in pairs(pages) do p.Visible = (k == currentSubTab) end
    end

    for _, entry in pairs(pillButtons) do
        SafeConnect(GetSignal(entry.Frame, "MouseButton1Click"), function() currentSubTab = entry.Def.key; stylePills() end)
    end

    local function CreatePresetGrid(parentBody, presets)
        local gridFrame = New("Frame", { Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0), AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, BackgroundTransparency = 1, Parent = parentBody })
        New("UIGridLayout", { CellPadding = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10), CellSize = UDim2.new(0.31, 0, 0, 110), SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center, Parent = gridFrame })

        for _, preset in ipairs(presets) do
            local card = New("TextButton", { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Glass, BackgroundTransparency = 0.25, ClipsDescendants = true, Text = "", Parent = gridFrame })
            Round(card, 12)
            local cardStroke = Stroke(card, accent, 1, 0.7)
            local thumb = New("ImageLabel", { BackgroundColor3 = Palette.Background, BackgroundTransparency = 0.2, Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6), Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 72), Image = preset.Image, ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit, Parent = card })
            Round(thumb, 8)
            New("TextLabel", { BackgroundTransparency = 1, Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 82), Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 24), Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium, Text = preset.Name, TextColor3 = Palette.Text, TextSize = 10, TextWrapped = true, TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd, TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, Parent = card })
            AddButtonHover(card, cardStroke, 0.12)

            SafeConnect(GetSignal(card, "MouseButton1Click"), function()
                PlayUISound("Click")
                if preset.Name == "Default" then
                    light = defaultLight
                    cussky = defsky
                    syncVisualWidgets()
                else
                    ApplyPshadePreset(preset.Url, preset.Sky)
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local function HD_SafeMaterial(name)
        local ok, m = pcall(function() return Enum.Material[name] end)
        if ok and typeof(m) == "EnumItem" then return m end
        return nil
    end

    local HD_MATERIAL_UPGRADE = {
        [Enum.Material.Plastic] = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic,
    }

    local HD_REFLECTANCE_DB = {}
    local function HD_SetReflectance(materialName, value)
        local m = HD_SafeMaterial(materialName)
        if m then HD_REFLECTANCE_DB[m] = value end
    end
    HD_SetReflectance("Metal", 0.35)
    HD_SetReflectance("DiamondPlate", 0.35)
    HD_SetReflectance("Foil", 0.40)
    HD_SetReflectance("CorrodedMetal", 0.12)
    HD_SetReflectance("Glass", 0.50)
    HD_SetReflectance("ForceField", 0.50)
    HD_SetReflectance("Ice", 0.45)
    HD_SetReflectance("Glacier", 0.40)
    HD_SetReflectance("Marble", 0.25)
    HD_SetReflectance("CeramicTiles", 0.20)
    HD_SetReflectance("Salt", 0.20)
    HD_SetReflectance("Granite", 0.12)
    HD_SetReflectance("CrackedLava", 0.10)
    HD_SetReflectance("Basalt", 0.08)
    HD_SetReflectance("Limestone", 0.08)
    HD_SetReflectance("SmoothPlastic", 0.10)
    HD_SetReflectance("Plastic", 0.10)
    HD_SetReflectance("Neon", 0.15)
    HD_SetReflectance("Wood", 0.06)
    HD_SetReflectance("WoodPlanks", 0.06)
    HD_SetReflectance("Slate", 0.10)
    HD_SetReflectance("Pavement", 0.06)
    HD_SetReflectance("Concrete", 0.05)
    HD_SetReflectance("Asphalt", 0.05)
    HD_SetReflectance("Brick", 0.04)
    HD_SetReflectance("Cobblestone", 0.03)
    HD_SetReflectance("Pebble", 0.03)
    HD_SetReflectance("Sandstone", 0.03)
    HD_SetReflectance("Snow", 0.15)
    HD_SetReflectance("Mud", 0.03)
    HD_SetReflectance("Sand", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("Ground", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("Grass", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("LeafyGrass", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("Fabric", 0.03)
    HD_SetReflectance("Carpet", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("Cardboard", 0.02)
    HD_SetReflectance("Rock", 0.05)
    local HD_REFLECTANCE_DEFAULT = 0.04

    local HD_SHADOW_MIN_SIZE = 0.6
    local HD_MESH_FIDELITY_MIN_SIZE = 1.0

    local hdTexturePartCount = 0
    local hdOriginalTechnology = nil
    local hdOriginalEnvScales = nil
    local hdOriginalGlobalShadows = nil
    local hdOriginalTerrain = nil
    local hdOriginalStreaming = nil


    local function HDStreaming_Apply(enable)
        local okStream, isStreaming = pcall(function() return Workspace.StreamingEnabled end)
        if not okStream or not isStreaming then return end
        if enable then
            hdOriginalStreaming = {
                Target = Workspace.StreamingTargetRadius,
                Min    = Workspace.StreamingMinRadius,
            }
            pcall(function() Workspace.StreamingTargetRadius = math.max(Workspace.StreamingTargetRadius, 4096) end)
            pcall(function() Workspace.StreamingMinRadius = math.max(Workspace.StreamingMinRadius, 512) end)
        else
            if hdOriginalStreaming then
                pcall(function() Workspace.StreamingTargetRadius = hdOriginalStreaming.Target end)
                pcall(function() Workspace.StreamingMinRadius = hdOriginalStreaming.Min end)
                hdOriginalStreaming = nil
            end
        end
    end

    local function TerrainHD_Apply(enable)
        if not Terrain then return end
        if enable then
            hdOriginalTerrain = {
                Decoration        = Terrain.Decoration,
                WaterWaveSize     = Terrain.WaterWaveSize,
                WaterWaveSpeed    = Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed,
                WaterReflectance  = Terrain.WaterReflectance,
                WaterTransparency = Terrain.WaterTransparency,
            }
            pcall(function() Terrain.Decoration = true end)
            pcall(function() Terrain.WaterWaveSize = 0.15 end)
            pcall(function() Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = 8 end)
            pcall(function() Terrain.WaterReflectance = 0.45 end)
            pcall(function() Terrain.WaterTransparency = 0.3 end)
        else
            if hdOriginalTerrain then
                pcall(function() Terrain.Decoration = hdOriginalTerrain.Decoration end)
                pcall(function() Terrain.WaterWaveSize = hdOriginalTerrain.WaterWaveSize end)
                pcall(function() Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = hdOriginalTerrain.WaterWaveSpeed end)
                pcall(function() Terrain.WaterReflectance = hdOriginalTerrain.WaterReflectance end)
                pcall(function() Terrain.WaterTransparency = hdOriginalTerrain.WaterTransparency end)
                hdOriginalTerrain = nil
            end
        end
    end
    local hdOriginalGlobalShadowsKey = nil

    local HD_VariantByMaterial = nil

    local function HD_ScanMaterialVariants()
        HD_VariantByMaterial = {}
        local MaterialService = SafeService("MaterialService")
        if not MaterialService then return end
        for _, child in pairs(MaterialService:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("MaterialVariant") then
                local ok, baseMat = pcall(function() return child.BaseMaterial end)
                if ok and baseMat and not HD_VariantByMaterial[baseMat] then
                    HD_VariantByMaterial[baseMat] = child.Name
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function HD_ApplyMaterialVariant(part, original)
        if not HD_VariantByMaterial then return end
        local variantName = HD_VariantByMaterial[part.Material]
        if not variantName then return end
        local okCur, curVariant = pcall(function() return part.MaterialVariant end)
        if okCur and curVariant ~= variantName then
            original.MaterialVariant = curVariant
            pcall(function() part.MaterialVariant = variantName end)
        end
    end

    local function HDTexture_IsCharacterPart(part)
        local model = part:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("Model")
        return model ~= nil and model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") ~= nil
    end

    local function HDTexture_ShouldSkip(part)
        if not part:IsA("BasePart") then return true end
        if part:IsA("Terrain") then return true end
        if part.Transparency >= 0.94 then return true end
        if HDTexture_IsCharacterPart(part) then return true end
        return false
    end

    local function HDTexture_ApplyToPart(part)
        local env = getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv
        if not env then return end
        if HDTexture_ShouldSkip(part) then return end
        if env.Applied[part] then return end

        local original = { Part = part, Material = part.Material, Reflectance = part.Reflectance, CastShadow = part.CastShadow }

        local upgrade = HD_MATERIAL_UPGRADE[part.Material]
        if upgrade then part.Material = upgrade end

        HD_ApplyMaterialVariant(part, original)

        local targetReflectance = HD_REFLECTANCE_DB[original.Material] or HD_REFLECTANCE_DEFAULT
        if targetReflectance > part.Reflectance then
            part.Reflectance = targetReflectance
        end

        local okSize, sz = pcall(function() return part.Size end)
        if okSize and (sz.X >= HD_SHADOW_MIN_SIZE or sz.Y >= HD_SHADOW_MIN_SIZE or sz.Z >= HD_SHADOW_MIN_SIZE) then
            part.CastShadow = true
        end

        if okSize and part:IsA("MeshPart")
        and (sz.X >= HD_MESH_FIDELITY_MIN_SIZE or sz.Y >= HD_MESH_FIDELITY_MIN_SIZE or sz.Z >= HD_MESH_FIDELITY_MIN_SIZE) then
            original.RenderFidelity = part.RenderFidelity
            if part.RenderFidelity ~= Enum.RenderFidelity.Precise then
                part.RenderFidelity = Enum.RenderFidelity.Precise
            end
        end

        env.Applied[part] = original
        hdTexturePartCount = hdTexturePartCount + 1
    end

    visW.hdTexture = secAdjust:CreateToggle({
        Title = "HD Texture & PBR Renderer",
        Subtitle = "Pipeline PBR resmi + reflection & shadow ditingkatkan, aman di semua map",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(s)
            if s then
                HDStreaming_Apply(true)

                local okGet, curTech = pcall(get_hidden_prop, Lighting, "Technology")
                hdOriginalTechnology = (okGet and curTech) or Lighting.Technology
                pcall(function() set_hidden_prop(Lighting, "Technology", Enum.Technology.Future) end)

                hdOriginalEnvScales = {
                    Diffuse = Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale,
                    Specular = Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale,
                    LightDiffuseKey = light['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'],
                    LightSpecularKey = light['sdfcddc'],
                }
                pcall(function() Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 1 end)
                pcall(function() Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 1 end)
                light['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] = 1
                light['sdfcddc'] = 1
                if visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] and visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'].Set then pcall(visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'].Set, 1) end
                if visW['sdfcddc'] and visW['sdfcddc'].Set then pcall(visW['sdfcddc'].Set, 1) end

                hdOriginalGlobalShadows = Lighting.GlobalShadows
                hdOriginalGlobalShadowsKey = light['hgnujuu7thgr']
                pcall(function() Lighting.GlobalShadows = true end)
                light['hgnujuu7thgr'] = true

                TerrainHD_Apply(true)

                HD_ScanMaterialVariants()

                getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv = { Applied = {}, Conn = nil }
                hdTexturePartCount = 0

                task.spawn(function()
                    local camPos = Camera and Camera.CFrame.Position
                    local queue, qn = {}, 0
                    for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if not getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv then return end
                        local dist = math.huge
                        if camPos then
                            local okPos, pos = pcall(function() return obj.Position end)
                            if okPos and pos then dist = (pos - camPos).Magnitude end
                        end
                        qn = qn + 1
                        queue[qn] = { Obj = obj, Dist = dist }
                        if qn % 500 == 0 then task.wait() end
                    end

                    table.sort(queue, function(a, b) return a.Dist < b.Dist end)

                    local n = 0
                    for _, item in ipairs(queue) do
                        if not getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv then return end
                        pcall(HDTexture_ApplyToPart, item.Obj)
                        n = n + 1
                        if n % 60 == 0 then task.wait() end
                    end
                end)

                getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv.Conn = Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
                    task.defer(function() pcall(HDTexture_ApplyToPart, obj) end)
                end)
            else
                HDStreaming_Apply(false)

                if hdOriginalTechnology then
                    local okCur, curTech = pcall(get_hidden_prop, Lighting, "Technology")
                    local curTechVal = (okCur and curTech) or Lighting.Technology
                    if curTechVal == Enum.Technology.Future then
                        pcall(function() set_hidden_prop(Lighting, "Technology", hdOriginalTechnology) end)
                    end
                    hdOriginalTechnology = nil
                end

                if hdOriginalEnvScales then
                    pcall(function() Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = hdOriginalEnvScales.Diffuse end)
                    pcall(function() Lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = hdOriginalEnvScales.Specular end)
                    light['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] = hdOriginalEnvScales.LightDiffuseKey
                    light['sdfcddc'] = hdOriginalEnvScales.LightSpecularKey
                    if visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] and visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'].Set then
                        pcall(visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'].Set, hdOriginalEnvScales.LightDiffuseKey or DefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale)
                    end
                    if visW['sdfcddc'] and visW['sdfcddc'].Set then
                        pcall(visW['sdfcddc'].Set, hdOriginalEnvScales.LightSpecularKey or DefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale)
                    end
                    hdOriginalEnvScales = nil
                end

                if hdOriginalGlobalShadows ~= nil then
                    local okCurGS, curGS = pcall(function() return Lighting.GlobalShadows end)
                    if okCurGS and curGS == true then
                        pcall(function() Lighting.GlobalShadows = hdOriginalGlobalShadows end)
                    end
                    light['hgnujuu7thgr'] = hdOriginalGlobalShadowsKey
                    hdOriginalGlobalShadows = nil
                    hdOriginalGlobalShadowsKey = nil
                end

                TerrainHD_Apply(false)

                local env = getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv
                if env then
                    if env.Conn then pcall(function() env.Conn:Disconnect() end) end
                    for part, original in pairs(env.Applied) do
                        if part and part.Parent then
                            pcall(function()
                                part.Material = original.Material
                                part.Reflectance = original.Reflectance
                                part.CastShadow = original.CastShadow
                                if original.RenderFidelity ~= nil then
                                    part.RenderFidelity = original.RenderFidelity
                                end
                                if original.MaterialVariant ~= nil then
                                    part.MaterialVariant = original.MaterialVariant
                                end
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                    getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv = nil
                    HD_VariantByMaterial = nil
                end
            end
        end,
    })

    local shadowAOOriginal = nil
    local shadowAOConn = nil
    local shadowAODescConn = nil
    local aoRaycastParts = {}
    local aoRaycastIndex = 0
    local AO_PARTS_PER_FRAME = 4

    local function AO_CollectParts()
        aoRaycastParts = {}
        local n = 0
        for _, part in pairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") and not part:IsA("Terrain")
            and part.Transparency < 0.94 then
                n = n + 1
                aoRaycastParts[n] = { Part = part, OrigColor = part.Color, LastAO = 1.0 }
            end
        end
    end

    local AO_RADIUS   = 8
    local AO_SAMPLES  = 10
    local AO_STRENGTH = 0.65

    local AO_HEMI_BASE = {}
    for i = 1, AO_SAMPLES do
        local phi   = math.acos(1 - i / AO_SAMPLES)
        local theta = math.pi * (1 + math.sqrt(5)) * i
        AO_HEMI_BASE[i] = Vector3.new(
            math.sin(phi) * math.cos(theta),
            math.cos(phi),
            math.sin(phi) * math.sin(theta)
        ).Unit
    end

    local AO_FACE_NORMALS = {
        Vector3.new(0, 1, 0), Vector3.new(0, -1, 0),
        Vector3.new(1, 0, 0), Vector3.new(-1, 0, 0),
        Vector3.new(0, 0, 1), Vector3.new(0, 0, -1),
    }

    local function AO_AlignToNormal(dir, normal)
        if normal.Y > 0.999 then return dir end
        if normal.Y < -0.999 then return Vector3.new(dir.X, -dir.Y, dir.Z) end
        local axis = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0):Cross(normal).Unit
        local angle = math.acos(math.clamp(normal.Y, -1, 1))
        local cosA, sinA = math.cos(angle), math.sin(angle)
        return dir * cosA + axis:Cross(dir) * sinA + axis * (axis:Dot(dir)) * (1 - cosA)
    end

    local function AO_GetExcludeList(part)
        local model = part:FindFirstAncestorWhichIsA("Model")
        if model and model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
            return { model }
        end
        return { part }
    end

    local function AO_Compute(part, rtParams)
        rtParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = AO_GetExcludeList(part)
        local origin = part.Position
        local halfSize = part.Size * 0.5

        local bestNormal, bestDist = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0), math.huge
        for _, n in ipairs(AO_FACE_NORMALS) do
            local faceOrigin = origin + n * (halfSize * n).Magnitude
            local ray = Workspace:Raycast(faceOrigin, n * 0.1, rtParams)
            local d = ray and ray.Distance or 1
            if d < bestDist then bestDist = d; bestNormal = n end
        end

        local hits = 0
        for _, baseDir in ipairs(AO_HEMI_BASE) do
            local dir = AO_AlignToNormal(baseDir, bestNormal)
            local result = Workspace:Raycast(origin, dir * AO_RADIUS, rtParams)
            if result then
                hits = hits + (1 - (result.Distance / AO_RADIUS))
            end
        end
        local rawAO = hits / AO_SAMPLES
        return 1 - math.clamp(rawAO * AO_STRENGTH, 0, 0.75)
    end

    visW.shadowAO = secAdjust:CreateToggle({
        Title = "Shadow & AO (Ambient Occlusion)",
        Subtitle = "Shadow lebih tajam + Ambient Occlusion real-time",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(s)
            if s then
                local okTech, origTech = pcall(function() return Lighting.Technology end)
                shadowAOOriginal = {
                    Technology = okTech and origTech or nil,
                    GlobalShadows = Lighting.GlobalShadows,
                    GlobalShadowsKey = light['hgnujuu7thgr'],
                    ShadowSoftness = Lighting.ShadowSoftness,
                }
                pcall(function() Lighting.Technology = Enum.Technology.Future end)
                Lighting.GlobalShadows = true
                light['hgnujuu7thgr'] = true
                Lighting.ShadowSoftness = 0.15

                local ssao = Lighting:FindFirstChild("JEYHUB_SSAO")
                if not ssao then
                    ssao = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect")
                    ssao.Name = "JEYHUB_SSAO"
                    ssao.Parent = Lighting
                end
                ssao.Enabled    = true
                ssao.Brightness = -0.06
                ssao.Contrast   = 0.15
                ssao.Saturation = -0.03
                ssao.TintColor  = Color3.fromRGB(253, 250, 246)

                AO_CollectParts()

                local rtParams = RaycastParams.new()
                rtParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude

                shadowAODescConn = Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
                    task.defer(function()
                        if not shadowAOConn then return end
                        if obj:IsA("BasePart") and not obj:IsA("Terrain") and obj.Transparency < 0.94 then
                            aoRaycastParts[#aoRaycastParts + 1] = { Part = obj, OrigColor = obj.Color, LastAO = 1.0 }
                        end
                    end)
                end)

                shadowAOConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    if #aoRaycastParts == 0 then return end
                    for _ = 1, AO_PARTS_PER_FRAME do
                        aoRaycastIndex = (aoRaycastIndex % #aoRaycastParts) + 1
                        local ap = aoRaycastParts[aoRaycastIndex]
                        if ap and ap.Part and ap.Part.Parent then
                            local ok, newAO = pcall(AO_Compute, ap.Part, rtParams)
                            if ok then
                                ap.LastAO = ap.LastAO + (newAO - ap.LastAO) * 0.15
                                local orig = ap.OrigColor
                                local ao = ap.LastAO
                                pcall(function()
                                    ap.Part.Color = Color3.new(
                                        orig.R * ao, orig.G * ao, orig.B * ao
                                    )
                                end)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                if shadowAOOriginal then
                    if shadowAOOriginal.Technology then
                        pcall(function() Lighting.Technology = shadowAOOriginal.Technology end)
                    end
                    Lighting.GlobalShadows  = shadowAOOriginal.GlobalShadows
                    Lighting.ShadowSoftness = shadowAOOriginal.ShadowSoftness
                    light['hgnujuu7thgr'] = shadowAOOriginal.GlobalShadowsKey
                    shadowAOOriginal = nil
                end
                local ssao = Lighting:FindFirstChild("JEYHUB_SSAO")
                if ssao then ssao:Destroy() end

                if shadowAOConn then
                    shadowAOConn:Disconnect()
                    shadowAOConn = nil
                end
                if shadowAODescConn then
                    shadowAODescConn:Disconnect()
                    shadowAODescConn = nil
                end
                for _, ap in ipairs(aoRaycastParts) do
                    if ap.Part and ap.Part.Parent then
                        pcall(function() ap.Part.Color = ap.OrigColor end)
                    end
                end
                aoRaycastParts = {}
            end
        end,
    })

    local qualityInitialized = false
    visW.qualityLevel = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Graphics Quality", Min = 1, Max = 21, Step = 1, Default = graphicsQuality, Callback = function(v)
        graphicsQuality = v
        if not qualityInitialized then
            qualityInitialized = true
            return
        end
        pcall(function() if v > 20 then settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level21' else settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level'..string.format("%02d", v) end end)
    end })

    -- OPTIMASI PERFORMA: sebelumnya Callback slider ini langsung scan
    -- SELURUH Workspace:GetDescendants() dan nulis Reflectance ke SEMUA
    -- BasePart TIAP KALI slider digeser. Karena Callback slider terpanggil
    -- puluhan kali per detik selama drag (bukan cuma sekali pas dilepas),
    -- ini artinya puluhan kali scan-seluruh-map per detik -- lag parah,
    -- apalagi di map dengan banyak part. Sekarang: (1) daftar part
    -- di-cache sekali & di-update inkremental lewat DescendantAdded
    -- (bukan scan ulang tiap panggilan), (2) penerapannya di-debounce
    -- maksimal 1x per 0.1 detik -- selama drag cepat, cuma benar-benar
    -- ke-apply beberapa kali (pakai NILAI TERBARU), bukan puluhan kali.
    local reflectPartsCache = nil
    local function GetReflectParts()
        if not reflectPartsCache then
            reflectPartsCache = {}
            for _, p in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                if p:IsA("BasePart") then reflectPartsCache[#reflectPartsCache + 1] = p end
            end
            SafeConnect(Workspace.DescendantAdded, function(obj)
                if obj:IsA("BasePart") then reflectPartsCache[#reflectPartsCache + 1] = obj end
            end)
        end
        return reflectPartsCache
    end
    local reflectApplyScheduled = false
    local reflectLatestValue = 0
    local function ApplyReflectanceDebounced()
        local v = reflectLatestValue
        for _, p in ipairs(GetReflectParts()) do
            if p.Parent then
                pcall(function() p.Reflectance = wshade and v or 0 end)
            end
        end
    end
    visW.reflect = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Reflectance", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = 0, Callback = function(v)
        adjust.reflect = v
        reflectLatestValue = v
        if not reflectApplyScheduled then
            reflectApplyScheduled = true
            task.delay(0.1, function()
                reflectApplyScheduled = false
                ApplyReflectanceDebounced()
            end)
        end
    end })
    visW['tgvbyd'] = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Clock Time", Min = 0, Max = 24, Step = 0.1, Default = DefaultLighting.ClockTime, Callback = function(v) light['tgvbyd'] = v end })
    visW['ghuybhuyhj'] = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Geographic Latitude", Min = 0, Max = 180, Step = 1, Default = DefaultLighting.GeographicLatitude, Callback = function(v) light['ghuybhuyhj'] = v end })
    visW['hdfr7thgr'] = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Exposure", Min = -3, Max = 3, Step = 0.1, Default = DefaultLighting.ExposureCompensation, Callback = function(v) light['hdfr7thgr'] = v end })

    visW['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Environment Diffuse Scale", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale, Callback = function(v) light['ygyyfgvhbjytrt'] = v end })
    visW['sdfcddc'] = secAdjust:CreateSlider({ Title = "Environment Specular Scale", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale, Callback = function(v) light['sdfcddc'] = v end })

    local secAtmos = Section.new(pages["atmosphere"], accent, "Atmosphere", "Adjust fog and weather particles")
    visW['shdbsnjfc'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Density", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.atDensity, Callback = function(v) light['shdbsnjfc'] = v end })
    visW['skdjfkdm'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Offset", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.atOffset, Callback = function(v) light['skdjfkdm'] = v end })
    visW['sejfd'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Glare", Min = 0, Max = 10, Step = 0.1, Default = DefaultLighting.atGlare, Callback = function(v) light['sejfd'] = v end })
    visW['jddfjsd'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Haze", Min = 0, Max = 10, Step = 0.1, Default = DefaultLighting.atHaze, Callback = function(v) light['jddfjsd'] = v end })
    if cloud then
        visW['gyhgtg'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Clouds Cover", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.clCover, Callback = function(v) light['gyhgtg'] = v end })
        visW['ygbhggv'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Clouds Density", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.clDensity, Callback = function(v) light['ygbhggv'] = v end })
    end

    visW.rays = secAtmos:CreateToggle({ Title = "Sunrays Enabled", Default = wl.rays, Callback = function(s) wl.rays = s; sray.Enabled = s end })
    visW['srIntensity'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Sunrays Intensity", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.srIntensity, Callback = function(v) light['srIntensity'] = v end })
    visW['srSpread'] = secAtmos:CreateSlider({ Title = "Sunrays Spread", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.srSpread, Callback = function(v) light['srSpread'] = v end })

    local secPost = Section.new(pages["postfx"], accent, "Post FX", "Screen post-processing")
    visW.cor = secPost:CreateToggle({ Title = "Color Correction Enabled", Default = wl.cor, Callback = function(s) wl.cor = s; colorcor.Enabled = s end })
    visW['fhnchvhfjsd'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Brightness", Min = -1, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.ccBrightness, Callback = function(v) light['fhnchvhfjsd'] = v end })
    visW['ugtbbjhygt'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Contrast", Min = -1, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.ccContrast, Callback = function(v) light['ugtbbjhygt'] = v end })
    visW['tfbghuugbnjhg'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Saturation", Min = -1, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.ccSaturation, Callback = function(v) light['tfbghuugbnjhg'] = v end })

    visW.bl = secPost:CreateToggle({ Title = "Bloom Enabled", Default = wl.bl, Callback = function(s) wl.bl = s; bloom.Enabled = s end })
    visW['jnfdhbnfcvh'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Bloom Intensity", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.blIntensity, Callback = function(v) light['jnfdhbnfcvh'] = v end })
    visW['fvtyghj'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Bloom Size", Min = 0, Max = 56, Step = 1, Default = DefaultLighting.blSize, Callback = function(v) light['fvtyghj'] = v end })
    visW['ygbhnj'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Bloom Threshold", Min = 0, Max = 4, Step = 0.1, Default = DefaultLighting.blThreshold, Callback = function(v) light['ygbhnj'] = v end })

    visW.blr = secPost:CreateToggle({ Title = "Blur Enabled", Default = wl.blr, Callback = function(s) wl.blr = s; blur.Enabled = s end })
    visW['njnfg'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "Blur Size", Min = 0, Max = 56, Step = 1, Default = DefaultLighting.blrSize, Callback = function(v) light['njnfg'] = v end })

    visW.dof = secPost:CreateToggle({ Title = "Depth of Field Enabled", Default = wl.dof, Callback = function(s) wl.dof = s; depth.Enabled = s end })
    visW['jdfkd'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "DoF Far Intensity", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.dofFar, Callback = function(v) light['jdfkd'] = v end })
    visW['fvgsdfg'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "DoF Focus Distance", Min = 0, Max = 200, Step = 1, Default = DefaultLighting.dofFocus, Callback = function(v) light['fvgsdfg'] = v end })
    visW['sdkvkflv'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "DoF In-Focus Radius", Min = 0, Max = 50, Step = 1, Default = DefaultLighting.dofRadius, Callback = function(v) light['sdkvkflv'] = v end })
    visW['hbjhd'] = secPost:CreateSlider({ Title = "DoF Near Intensity", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = DefaultLighting.dofNear, Callback = function(v) light['hbjhd'] = v end })

    local secEff = Section.new(pages["effects"], accent, "Effects", "Extra special visual effects")
    visW.mblur = secEff:CreateToggle({ Title = "Blur Motion", Subtitle = "Blur effect on quick glance", Default = wl.mblur, Callback = function(s) wl.mblur = s end })
    visW.sflare = secEff:CreateToggle({ Title = "Sunflare", Subtitle = "Cahaya lens-flare kustom di matahari", Default = wl.sflare, Callback = function(s) wl.sflare = s end })
    secEff:CreateSlider({ Title = "Water Wave Speed", Min = 0, Max = 100, Step = 1, Default = 10, Callback = function(v) if wshade and Terrain then Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = v end end })
    secEff:CreateSlider({ Title = "Water Transparency", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = 1, Callback = function(v) if wshade and Terrain then Terrain.WaterTransparency = v end end })
    secEff:CreateSlider({ Title = "Water Wave Size", Min = 0, Max = 40, Step = 0.5, Default = 0.15, Callback = function(v) if wshade and Terrain then Terrain.WaterWaveSize = v end end })

    secEff:CreateSlider({ Title = "Water Reflectance", Min = 0, Max = 1, Step = 0.05, Default = 1, Callback = function(v) if wshade and Terrain then Terrain.WaterReflectance = v end end })

    local VisualPrefs     = { autoLoad = false }

    local function serializeLight(tbl)
        local out = {}
        for k, v in pairs(tbl) do
            if typeof(v) == "Color3" then
                out[k] = { __c3 = true, r = v.R, g = v.G, b = v.B }
            else
                out[k] = v
            end
        end
        return out
    end

    local function deserializeLight(tbl)
        local out = {}
        for k, v in pairs(tbl) do
            if type(v) == "table" and v.__c3 then
                out[k] = Color3.new(tonumber(v.r) or 0, tonumber(v.g) or 0, tonumber(v.b) or 0)
            else
                out[k] = v
            end
        end
        return out
    end

    -- Visual config sekarang di section "visualConfig" pada file JSON
    -- gabungan JEYHUB/data.json -- bukan JEYHUB_Visual/config.json lagi.
    local function saveVisualConfig()
        local payload = {
            light = serializeLight(light),
            wl = { dof = wl.dof, cor = wl.cor, rays = wl.rays, bl = wl.bl, blr = wl.blr, sflare = wl.sflare, mblur = wl.mblur, global = wl.global, tech = wl.tech },
            wshade = wshade,
            cussky = cussky,
            bmsize = bmsize,
            reflect = adjust.reflect,
            qualityLevel = graphicsQuality,
            shadowAO = (shadowAOOriginal ~= nil) or (shadowAOConn ~= nil),
            hdTexture = getgenv().JEYHUB_HDTextureEnv ~= nil,
            autoLoad = VisualPrefs.autoLoad,
        }
        JD_Set("visualConfig", payload)
        return true, "Visual settings saved successfully."
    end

    local function loadVisualConfig(silent)
        local data = JD_Get("visualConfig", nil)
        if type(data) ~= "table" then
            return false, "No saved visual settings yet."
        end

        local ok, err = pcall(function()
            if type(data.light) == "table" then
                light = deserializeLight(data.light)
                syncVisualWidgets()
            end
            if data.wshade ~= nil then wshade = data.wshade == true end
            if visW.wshade then visW.wshade.Set(wshade, true) end
            if type(data.wl) == "table" then
                for k, v in pairs(data.wl) do wl[k] = v end
                if visW.global then visW.global.Set(wl.global, true) end
                if visW.tech and wl.tech then visW.tech.Set(wl.tech) end
                if visW.rays then visW.rays.Set(wl.rays, true) end
                if visW.cor then visW.cor.Set(wl.cor, true) end
                if visW.bl then visW.bl.Set(wl.bl, true) end
                if visW.blr then visW.blr.Set(wl.blr, true) end
                if visW.dof then visW.dof.Set(wl.dof, true) end
                if visW.mblur then visW.mblur.Set(wl.mblur, true) end
                if visW.sflare then visW.sflare.Set(wl.sflare, true) end
            end
            if type(data.cussky) == "table" then cussky = data.cussky end
            if type(data.bmsize) == "number" then bmsize = data.bmsize end
            if type(data.reflect) == "number" then
                adjust.reflect = data.reflect
                if visW.reflect then visW.reflect.Set(data.reflect) end
            end
            if type(data.qualityLevel) == "number" then
                graphicsQuality = data.qualityLevel
                pcall(function()
                    if graphicsQuality > 20 then
                        settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level21'
                    else
                        settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level' .. string.format("%02d", graphicsQuality)
                    end
                end)
                if visW.qualityLevel then visW.qualityLevel.Set(graphicsQuality) end
            end
            if data.shadowAO ~= nil and visW.shadowAO then
                visW.shadowAO.Set(data.shadowAO == true, true)
            end
            if data.hdTexture ~= nil and visW.hdTexture then
                visW.hdTexture.Set(data.hdTexture == true, true)
            end
            if data.autoLoad ~= nil then VisualPrefs.autoLoad = data.autoLoad == true end
        end)
        if not silent then
            return ok, (ok and "Visual settings loaded successfully." or ("Failed to load: " .. tostring(err)))
        end
        return ok, err
    end

    local secSettings = Section.new(pages["settings"], accent, "Save & Load Settings", "Persist every preset & slider in the Visual tab to file")
    local settingsStatus

    local function setSettingsStatus(msg, isError)
        if settingsStatus and settingsStatus.Label then
            settingsStatus.Label.Text = msg
            settingsStatus.Label.TextColor3 = isError and Color3.fromRGB(255, 110, 110) or Palette.SubText
        end
    end

    secSettings:CreateButton({
        Title = "Save Visual Settings",
        Subtitle = "Save all sliders/toggles in the current Visual tab to a file",
        ButtonText = "Save",
        Callback = function()
            local ok, msg = saveVisualConfig()
            setSettingsStatus(msg, not ok)
        end,
    })

    secSettings:CreateButton({
        Title = "Load Visual Settings",
        Subtitle = "Re-apply the last saved settings",
        ButtonText = "Load",
        Callback = function()
            local ok, msg = loadVisualConfig(false)
            setSettingsStatus(msg, not ok)
        end,
    })

    secSettings:CreateToggle({
        Title = "Auto-load when the script runs",
        Subtitle = "Automatically apply saved settings every time JEYHUB opens",
        Default = VisualPrefs.autoLoad,
        Callback = function(s)
            VisualPrefs.autoLoad = s
            local ok, msg = saveVisualConfig()
            setSettingsStatus(msg, not ok)
        end,
    })

    do
        local statusRoot = NewElementRoot(secSettings.Body, 24)
        settingsStatus = { Label = New("TextLabel", {
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0),
            Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium,
            Text = "",
            TextColor3 = Palette.SubText,
            TextSize = 11,
            TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
            TextWrapped = true,
            Parent = statusRoot,
        }) }
    end

    do
        local autoData = JD_Get("visualConfig", nil)
        if type(autoData) == "table" and autoData.autoLoad == true then
            pcall(function() loadVisualConfig(true) end)
        end
    end

    stylePills()
end

local okVisualBuild, visualBuildErr = pcall(BuildVisualTab)
if not okVisualBuild then
    warn("[JEYHUB] BuildVisualTab failed (caught safely):", visualBuildErr)
end

for _, emptyTabName in ipairs({ "Usefull", "Utility", "Troll", "Fire Server", "Execute", "Others" }) do
    local okPlaceholder, placeholderErr = pcall(BuildPlaceholderTab, emptyTabName)
    if not okPlaceholder then
        warn("[JEYHUB] Placeholder for tab " .. tostring(emptyTabName) .. " failed:", placeholderErr)
    end
end

if Window and Window.Gui then
    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(5)

            if not IsCurrentRun() then break end
            local gui = Window.Gui
            local stillValid = false
            pcall(function()
                stillValid = gui.Parent ~= nil and gui:IsDescendantOf(game)
            end)
            if not stillValid then
                local okReparent = pcall(function()
                    local newParent = GetGuiParent()
                    if newParent then
                        gui.Parent = newParent
                    end
                end)
                if not okReparent then

                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

return Window
